ShreeJñāneshwarī Adhyay 18 Transliterated

|| ShreeJñāneshwarī || Adhyāya 18 vā

Jayajaya deva nirmaḷa | nijajanākhilamaṅgala | janmajarājaḷadajāḷa- | prabhaṅjana || Jñāne.18.1 || Jayajaya deva prabaḷa | vidaḷitāmaṅgaḷakuḷa | nigamāgamadrumaphaḷa | phalaprada || Jñāne.18.2 || Jayajaya deva sakaḷa | vigata-viṣhayavatsala | kalitakāḷakautūhala | kalātīta || Jñāne.18.3 || Jayajaya deva nishchaḷa | chalita-chittapānatuṅdila | jagadunmīlanāvirala | kelipriya || Jñāne.18.4 || Jayajaya deva niṣhkaḷa | sphurada-maṅdānaṅdabahaḷa | nityanirastākhilamaḷa | mūḷabhūta || Jñāne.18.5 || Jayajaya deva swaprabha | jagadaṁbudagarbhanabha | bhuvanodbhavāraṁbhastaṁbha | bhavadhwaṁsa || Jñāne.18.6 || Jayajaya deva vishuddha | avidyodyānadwirada | shamadama-madanamadabheda | dayārṇava || Jñāne.18.7 || Jayajaya devaikarūpa | atikrutakaṅdarpasarpadarpa | bhaktabhāva bhuvanadīpa | tāpāpaha || Jñāne.18.8 || Jayajaya deva adwitīya | pariṇatoparamaikapriya | nijajanajita bhajanīya | māyāgamya || Jñāne.18.9 || Jayajaya deva Shreeguro | akalpanākalpataro | swasaṁviddrumabījapraro- | haṇāvanī || Jñāne.18.10 || He kāya ekaika aise | nānāparibhāṣhāvashe | stotra karū tuĵadoṣhe | nirvisheṣhā || Jñāne.18.11 || Jihī visheṣhaṇī visheṣhije | te drushya navhe rūpa tuĵhe | he ĵāṇe mī mhaṇoni lāje | vānaṇā iṁhī || Jñāne.18.12 || Pari maryādechā sāgara | hā tavachi tayā ḍagara | jaṅva na dekhe sudhākara | udayā ālā || Jñāne.18.13 || Somakāṅta nijanirjharī | chaṅdrā arghyādika na karī | te tochi avadhārī | karavī kī jī || Jñāne.18.14 || Neṇo kaisī vasaṅtasaṅge | avachitī jhāḍāṅchī aṅge | phuṭatī tai tayāṅhī ĵoge | dharaṇe nohe || Jñāne.18.15 || Padminī ravikiraṇa | lāhe maga lāje kavaṇa | kā jaḷe shiṁvatale lavaṇa | āṅga bhule || Jñāne.18.16 || Taisā tūte jetha mī smare | tetha mīpaṇa mī visare | maga jākaḷilā ḍheṅkare | trupta jaisā || Jñāne.18.17 || Maja tuvā jī kele taise | māĵhe mīpaṇa davaḍūni deshe | stutimiṣhe pāṅchapise | bāṅdhale vāche || Jñāne.18.18 || Nā yerhavī tarī āṭhavī | rāhoni stuti jai karāvī | tai guṇāguṇī dharāvī | sarobharī kī || Jñāne.18.19 || Tarī tū jī ekarasāche liṅga | kevī karū guṇāguṇī vibhāga | motī phoḍoni sāṅdhitā chāṅga | kī taiseṅchi bhale || Jñāne.18.20 || Āṇi bāpa tū māye | iṁhī bolī nā stutī hoye | ḍiṁbhopādhika āhe | viṭāḷa tethe || Jñāne.18.21 || Jī ĵāleni pāike āle | te gosāvīpaṇa kevī bole | aise upādhī ushiṭale | kāya varṇū || Jñāne.18.22 || Jari ātmā tū ekasarā | heṁhī mhaṇatā dātārā | tarī āṅtula tū bāherā | ghāpatāsī || Jñāne.18.23 || Mhaṇūni satyachi tuĵalāgī | stutī na dekho jī jagī | maunāvāṅchūni leṇe āṅgī | susīnā mā || Jñāne.18.24 || Stutī kāhī na bolaṇe | pūjā kāhī na karaṇe | sannidhī kāhī na hoṇe | tujhyā ṭhāyī || Jñāne.18.25 || Tari jitale jaise bhulī | pise ālāpa ghālī | taise vānū te māulī | upasāhāve tuvā || Jñāne.18.26 || Ātā Gītārthāchī muktamudī | levavī mājhiye vāgvruddhī | jeṇe māne he sabhāsadī | sajjanāṅchyā || Jñāne.18.27 || Tetha mhaṇitale Shreenivruttī | nako he puḍhatapuḍhatī | parisī lohā ghruṣhṭī kitī | veḷaveḷā kīje gā || Jñāne.18.28 || Tava vinavī Jñānadev | mhaṇe ho kā jī pasāva | pari avadhāna detu deva | graṅthā ātā || Jñāne.18.29 || [Prāsādakalasharūpakatwenāṣhṭādashaṁ varṇayati] Jī Gītāratnaprāsādāchā | kaḷasa arthachiṅtāmaṇīchā | sarva Gītādarshanāchā | pāḍhāū ĵo || Jñāne.18.30 || Lokī tarī āthī aise | je durūni kaḷasa dise | āṇi bheṭīṅchi hātavase | devatechī tiye || Jñāne.18.31 || Taiseṅchi ethahī āhe | je ekechi yeṇe adhyāye | āghavāchi druṣhṭa hoye | Gītāgama hā || Jñāne.18.32 || Mī kaḷasa yāchikāraṇe | aṭharāvā adhyāya mhaṇe | uvāilā bādarāyaṇe | Gītāprāsādā || Jñāne.18.33 || Nohe kaḷasāparate kāhī | prāsādī kāma nāhī | te sāṅgatase Gītāhī | saṁpalepaṇe || Jñāne.18.34 || Vyāsa sahaĵe sūtrī baḷī | teṇe nigamaratnāchaḷī | upaniṣhadārthāchī māḷī- | mājī khāṅḍilī || Jñāne.18.35 || Tetha trivargāchā aṇuāru | āḍaū nighālā ĵo apāru | to Mahābhārataprākāru | bhoṅvatā kelā || Jñāne.18.36 || Māji ātmajñānāche ekavaṭa | daḷavāḍe jhāḍūni chokhaṭa | ghaḍile PārthaVaikuṅṭha- | saṁvādakusarī || Jñāne.18.37 || Nivruttisūtra-soḍaṇiyā | sarva-shāstrārtha puravaṇiyā | āvo sādhilā māṅḍaṇiyā | mokṣharekhechā || Jñāne.18.38 || Aiseni karitā ubhārā | paṅdharā adhyāyāṅta paṅdharā | bhūmī nirvāḷaliyā purā | prāsāda ĵāhalā || Jñāne.18.39 || Upari soḷāvā adhyāya | to grīve ghaṅṭechā āya | saptadasha to ṭhāya | paḍaghāṇiye || Jñāne.18.40 || Tayāhīvarī aṣhṭādasha | to āpaisā māṅḍalā kaḷasa | upari Gītādikī Vyāsa | dhwaja lāgalā || Jñāne.18.41 || Mhaṇauni māgīla je adhyāya | te chaḍhate bhūmīche āya | tayāṅche pure dāvitāhe | āpulyā āṅgī || Jñāne.18.42 || Jālayā kāmā nāhī chorī | te kaḷase hoya uĵarī | tevi aṣhṭādasha vivarī | sādyaṅta Gītā || Jñāne.18.43 || Aisā Vyāse viṅdāṇiye | Gītāprāsādu ĵoḍaṇiye | āṇūni rākhile prāṇiye | nānāparī || Jñāne.18.44 || Eka pradakṣhiṇā japāchiyā | bāheroni karitī yayā | eka te shravaṇamiṣhe chhāyā | sevitī yayāchī || Jñāne.18.45 || Eka te avadhānāchā purā | viḍāpāuḍa bhītarā | gheūni righatī gābhārā | arthajñānāchyā || Jñāne.18.46 || Te nijabodhe urāurī | bheṭatī ātmayā Shreeharī | parī mokṣhaprāsādī sarī | sarvāṁhī āthī || Jñāne.18.47 || Samarthāṅchiye paṅktibhojane | taḷiṁlyā varilyā eka pakvānne | tevi shravaṇe arthe paṭhaṇe | mokṣhachi lābhe || Jñāne.18.48 || Aisā Gītā vaiṣhṇavaprāsāda | aṭharāvā adhyāya kaḷasa vishada | myā mhaṇitalā hā bheda | ĵāṇoniyā || Jñāne.18.49 || [Aṣhṭādashādhyāyotpattiprastāvaḥ] Ātā saptadashāpāṭhī | adhyāya kaiseni uṭhī | to saṁbaṅdha sāṅgo diṭhī | dise taisā || Jñāne.18.50 || Kā Gaṅgāyamunāudaka | voghabage vegaḷika | dāvī hoūni eka | pāṇīpaṇe || Jñāne.18.51 || Na moḍatā donhī ākāra | ghaḍile eka sharīra | he ardhanārīnaṭeshwara | rūpī dise || Jñāne.18.52 || Nā nā vāḍhalī divase | kaḷā biṁbī paise | pari sināne leve jaise | chaṅdrī nāhī || Jñāne.18.53 || Taisī sinānī chārī pade | shlokashlokāvachchhede | adhyāya adhyāyabhede | game kīra || Jñāne.18.54 || Pari prameyāchī uĵarī | ānāna rūpa na dharī | nānā ratnamaṇī dorī | ekachi jaisī || Jñāne.18.55 || Motiye miḷoni bahuve | ekāvaḷīchā pāḍa āhe | parī shobhe rūpa hoye | ekachi tetha || Jñāne.18.56 || Phulā phulasarā lekha chaḍhe | drutī dujī aṅguḷī na paḍe | shloka adhyāya teṇe pāḍe | ĵāṇāve he || Jñāne.18.57 || Sāta shate shloka | adhyāyā aṭharāṅche lekha | parī deva bolile eka | je duje nāhī || Jñāne.18.58 || Āṇi myāṅhī na sāṅḍoni te soye | graṅthavyaktī kelī āhe | prastuta teṇe nirvāhe | nirūpaṇa āikā || Jñāne.18.59 || [Adhyāyasaṅggatiḥ(hi)] Tarī satarāvā adhyāya | pāvatā puratā ṭhāva | je saṁpatā shlokī deva | bolile aise || Jñāne.18.60 || Arjunā brahmanāmāchyā vikhī | buddhī sāṅḍūni āstikī | karme kijatī titukī | asaṅte hotī || Jñāne.18.61 || Hā aikoni devāchā bola | Arjunā ālā ḍola | mhaṇe karmaniṣhṭhā maḷa | ṭhevilā dekho || Jñāne.18.62 || To ajñānāṅdha tava bāpuḍā | īshwarachi na dekhe evaḍhā | tetha nāmachi eka te puḍhā | kā sujhe tayā || Jñāne.18.63 || Āṇi raja tame donhī | geliyāvīṇa shraddhā sānī | te kā lāge abhidhānī | brahmāchiye || Jñāne.18.64 || Maga kotā kheṅva deṇe | vārtevarīla dhāvaṇe | sāṅḍī paḍe kheḷavaṇe | nāgiṇīche te || Jñāne.18.65 || Taisī karme duvāḍe | tayā janmāṅtarāchī kaḍe | durmeḷāve yevaḍhe | karmāmājī || Jñāne.18.66 || Nā vipāye he ujū hoye | tarī jñānāchī yogyatā lāhe | yerhavī yeṇeṅchi jāye | nirayālayā || Jñāne.18.67 || [Saṁ(n)nyāsatyāgaḥ] Karmī hā ṭhāyavarī | āhātī bahuvā avasarī | ātā karmaṭhā kai ye vārī | mokṣhāchī he || Jñāne.18.68 || Tarī phiṭo karmāchā pāṅga | kīĵo avaghāchi tyāga | ādarīĵo avyaṅga | saṅnyāsa hā || Jñāne.18.69 || Karmabādhechiyā kaṁhī | jetha bhayāchī goṭhī nāhī | te ātmajñāna jihī | swādhīna hoya || Jñāne.18.70 || Jñānāche āvāhanamaṅtra | je jñānapikate sukṣhetra | jñāna ākarṣhite sūtra- | taṅtu je kā || Jñāne.18.71 || Te donī saṅnyāsa tyāga | anuṣhṭhūnī suṭe jaga | tarī hechi ātā chāṅga | vyakta puso || Jñāne.18.72 || Aise mhaṇoni Pārthe | tyāga saṅnyāsavyavasthe | rūpa hoāvayā yethee | prashna kelā || Jñāne.18.73 || Tetha pratyuttare bolī | ShreeKriṣhṇe je chāvaḷilī | tayā vyaktī jālī | aṣhṭādashā || Jñāne.18.74 || Eva janyajanakabhāve | adhyāya adhyāyāte prasave | ātā aikā barave | pusile je || Jñāne.18.75 || Tari Paṅḍukumare teṇe | devāche sarate bolaṇe | ĵāṇoni aṅtaḥkaraṇe | kāṇī ghetalī || Jñāne.18.76 || Yerhavī tattwaviṣhayī bhalā | to nishchita ase kīra ĵāhalā | pari devo rāhe ugalā | te sāhāvenā || Jñāne.18.77 || Vatsa dhāliyāhī varī | dhenū na vachāvī durī | ananya prītīchī parī | aisī āhe || Jñāne.18.78 || Teṇe kājeṁvīṇahī bolāve | te dekhile tari pāhāve | bhogitā ĉhāḍa duṇāve | paḍhiyaṅtayāṭhāyī || Jñāne.18.79 || Aisī premāchī he jātī | āṇi Pārth tava techi mūrtī | mhaṇūni karū lāhe khaṅtī | ugepaṇāchī || Jñāne.18.80 || Āṇi saṁvādācheni miṣhe | je avyavahāra vastu ase | techi bhogije kī jaise | darpaṇī rūpa || Jñāne.18.81 || Maga saṁvāda tochi pārukhe | tari bhogitā bhogaṇe thoke | he kā sāhāvela sukhe | lāṅchāvaleyā || Jñāne.18.82 || Yālāgī tyāga saṅnyāsa | pusāvayāche gheūni misa | maga upalavile dusa | gīteche te || Jñāne.18.83 || Aṭharāvā adhyāya nohe | he ekādhyāyī Gītāchi āhe | jai vatsachi dhenū duhe | tai veḷa kāyasī || Jñāne.18.84 || Taisī saṁpatā avasarī | Gītā ādaravilī māghārī | swāmī bhrutyāĉhā na karī | saṁvāda kāī || Jñāne.18.85 ||

Arjuna uvācha - Saṁ(n)nyāsasya mahābāho tattwamichchhāmi veditum | tyāgasya cha Hruṣhīkesha pruthakkeshiniṣhūdana || Bha.Gī.18.1 ||

[Arjuna uvācha-] Parī he aso aise | Arjune pusijata ase | mhaṇe vinaṅtī vishweshe | avadhāriĵo || Jñāne.18.86 || [Saṁ(n)nyāsasya mahābāho] Hā jī saṅnyāsa āṇi tyāga | iyā dohī eke arthī lāga | jaisā saṅghāta saṅgha | saṅghātechi bolije || Jñāne.18.87 || [Tyāgasya cha Hruṣhīkesha] Taiseṅchi tyāge āṇi saṅnyāse | tyāgachi bolijata ase | [tattwamichchhāmi vedituṁ] āmacheni tava mānase | jāṇije hechi || Jñāne.18.88 || [Pruthakkeshiniṣhūdana] Nā kāhī āthī arthabheda | to deva karotu vishada | [chūrṇikā] tetha mhaṇatī Shreemukuṅda | bhinnachi pai || Jñāne.18.89 || [Shrībhagavānuvācha] Tari Arjunā tujhyā manī | tyāga saṅnyāsa donī | ekārtha gamale he mānī | mīhī sācha || Jñāne.18.90 || Iṅhī dohī kīra shabdī | tyāgachi bolije trishuddhī | pari kāraṇa etha bhedī | yetuleṅchī || Jñāne.18.91 || Nipaṭūni karma sāṅḍije | te sāṅḍaṇe saṅnyāsa mhaṇije | phaḷamātra kā tyajije | to tyāga gā || Jñāne.18.92 || Tarī koṇā karmāche phaḷa | sāṅḍije koṇa karma kevaḷa | heṁhī sāṅgo vivaḷa | chitta deī || Jñāne.18.93 || Tari āpaisī dāṅge ḍoṅgara | jhāḍāḷī vitī apāra | taise lāṁbe rājāgara | nuṭhitī te || Jñāne.18.94 || Na peritā saiṅgha truṇe | uṭhatī taise sāḷīche hoṇe | nāhī gā rābā uṇe | jiyāparī || Jñāne.18.95 || Kā aṅga ĵāhāle sahaĵe | pari leṇe udyame kīje | nadī āpaisī āpādije | vihirī jevī || Jñāne.18.96 || Taise nityanaimittika | karma hoya swābhāvika | pari na kāmitā kāmika | na niphaje || Jñāne.18.97 ||

Shrībhagavānuvācha - Kāmyānāṁ(ṅ) karmaṇāṁ(n) nyāsaṁ saṁ(n)nyāsaṁ(ṅ) kavayo viduḥ(hu) | sarvakarmaphalatyāgaṁ prāhustyāgaṁ vichakṣhaṇāḥ(hā) || Bha.Gī.18.2 ||

[Shrībhagavānuvācha-kāmyānāṁ(ṅ) karmaṇāṁ] Kā kāmanechechi daḷavāḍe | je ubhārāvayā ghaḍe | ashwamedhādika phuḍe | yāga jetha || Jñāne.18.98 || Vāpī kūpa ārāma | agrahāre hana mahāgrama | āṇīkahī nānāsaṁbhrama | vratāṅche te || Jñāne.18.99 || Aise iṣhṭapūrta sakaḷa | jayā kāmanā eka mūḷa | je kele bhogavī phaḷa | bāṅdhoniyā || Jñāne.18.100 || Dehāchiyā gāṁvā āliyā | janmamrutyūchiyā sohaḷyā | nā mhaṇo na ye dhanaṅjayā | jiyāparī || Jñāne.18.101 || Kā lalāṭīṅche lihile | na moḍe gā kāhī kele | kāḷegorepaṇa dhutale | phiṭo neṇe || Jñāne.18.102 || Kele kāmya karma taise | phaḷa bhogāvayā dharaṇe baise | na pheḍitā rhuṇa jaise | vosaṅḍīnā || Jñāne.18.103 || Kā kāmanāhī na karitā | avasāṅta ghaḍe Paṅḍusutā | tarī vāyakāṅḍa ĵuṅĵhatā | lāge jaise || Jñāne.18.104 || Guḷa neṇatā toṅḍī | ghātalā dechi goḍī | āgī mānūni rākhoṅḍī | chepilā poḷī || Jñāne.18.105 || Kāmyakarmī he eka | sāmarthya āthī swābhāvika | mhaṇauni nako kautuka | mumukṣhū etha || Jñāne.18.106 || [Nyāsaṁ] Kiṁbahunā Pārthā aise | je kāmya karma gā ase | te tyajije viṣha jaise | vokūniyā || Jñāne.18.107 || [Saṁ(n)nyāsaṁ(ṅ) kavayo viduḥ(hu)] Maga tayā tyāgāte jagī | saṅnyāsa aisayā bhaṅgī | bolije aṅtaraṅgī | sarvadraṣhṭā || Jñāne.18.108 || He kāmya karma sāṅḍaṇe | te kāmanetechi upaḍaṇe | dravyatyāge davaḍaṇe | bhaya jaise || Jñāne.18.109 || [Sarvakarmaphalatyāgaṁ] [karmaṁ(n) dwividhaṁ(n) nityaṁ(n) naimittikaṁ(ñ) cha] āṇi somasūryagrahaṇe | yeūni karavitī pārvaṇe | kā mātāpitaramaraṇe | aṅkita je divasa || Jñāne.18.110 || Athavā atithī hana pāve | he aisaise paḍe je karāve | te te karma ĵāṇāve | naimittika gā || Jñāne.18.111 || Vārṣhiyā kṣhobhe gagana | vasaṅte duṇāve vana | deha shrruṅgārī yauvana- | dashā jaisī || Jñāne.18.112 || Kā somakāṅta some paghaḷe | sūrye phāṅkatī kamaḷe | etha asateṅcha pālhāḷe | āna na ye || Jñāne.18.113 || Taise nitya je kā karma | te nimittāche lāhe niyama | etha uṅchāve teṇe nāma | naimittika hoya || Jñāne.18.114 || Āṇi sāyaṁprātarmadhyāhnī | je kā karaṇīya pratidinī | pari druṣhṭi jaisī lochanī | adhika nohe || Jñāne.18.115 || Kā nāpāditā gatī | charaṇī jaisī āthī | nā tarī te dīptī | dīpabiṁbī || Jñāne.18.116 || Vāsa neditā jaise | chaṅdanī saurabhya ase | adhikārāche taise | rūpachi je || Jñāne.18.117 || Nitya karma aise janī | Pārthā bolije te mānī | eva nitya naimittika donhī | dāvilī tuĵa || Jñāne.18.118 || Hechi nitya naimittika | anuṣhṭheya āvashyaka | mhaṇauni mhaṇo pāhatī eka | vāṅjha yayāte || Jñāne.18.119 || Pari bhojanī jaise hoye | truptī lābhe bhūka jāye | taise nitya naimittikī āhe | sarvāṅgī phaḷa || Jñāne.18.120 || Kīḍa āgiṭhā paḍe | tari maḷa tuṭe vānī chaḍhe | yayā karmā tayā sāṅgaḍe | phaḷa ĵāṇāve || Jñāne.18.121 || Je pratyavāya tava gaḷe | swādhikāra bahuve ujaḷe | te hātophaḷiyā miḷe | sadgatīsī || Jñāne.18.122 || Yevaḍhevarī ḍhisāḷa | nityanaimittikī āhe phaḷa | [tyāgaṁ] pari te tyajije mūḷa | nakṣhatrī jaise || Jñāne.18.123 || Latā pike āghavī | tava chūta bāṅdhe pālavī | maga hāta na lāvita mādhavī | soḍūni ghālī || Jñāne.18.124 || Taisī nolāṅḍitā karmarekhā | chitta dīje nityanaimittikā | pāṭhī phaḷā kīje ashekhā | vāṅtichiyevānī || Jñāne.18.125 || [Prāhustyāgaṁ vichakṣhaṇāḥ(hā)] Yayā karmaphaḷatyāgāte | tyāga mhaṇatī pai ĵāṇate | [ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] eva tyāga saṅnyāsa tūte | parisavile || Jñāne.18.126 || Hā saṅnyāsa jai saṁbhave | tai kāmya bāṅdhū na pave | niṣhiddha tava swabhāve | niṣhiddhe gele || Jñāne.18.127 || Āṇi nityādika je ase | te yeṇe phaḷatyāge nāse | shira loṭaliyā jaise | yera āṅga || Jñāne.18.128 || Maga sasya phaḷapākāṅta | taise nimāliyā karmajāta | ātmajñāna giṁvasita | apaise ye || Jñāne.18.129 || Aisiyā nigutī donī | tyāga saṅnyāsa anuṣhṭhānī | paḍale gā ātmajñānī | bāṅdhatī pāṭa || Jñāne.18.130 || [Chūrṇikā] Nā tarī he nigutī chuke | maga tyāga kīje hātatuke | te kāhī na tyaje adhike | govīṅchi paḍe || Jñāne.18.131 || Je auṣhadha vyādhī anoḷakha | te ghetaliyā parate vikha | kā anna na mānitā bhūka | na mārī kāya || Jñāne.18.132 || Mhaṇauni tyājya je nohe | tetha tyāgāte na suvāve | tyājyālāgī nohāve | lobhapara || Jñāne.18.133 || Chukaliyā tyāgāche veṅjhe | kelā sarvatyāgahī hoya vojhe | niṣhiddhe tyā sarvatra juṅjhe | vītarāga te || Jñāne.18.134 ||

Tyājyaṁ(n) doṣhavadityeke karma prāhurmanīṣhiṇaḥ | yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyamiti chāpare || Bha.Gī.18.3 ||

[Doṣhavadityeke] Ekā phaḷatyāga na ṭhāke | te karmāte mhaṇatī baṅdhake | jaise āpaṇa nagna bhāṅḍake | jagāte mhaṇe || Jñāne.18.135 || Kā jivhālaṁpaṭa rogiyā | anne dūṣhī dhanaṅjayā | āṅgā na ruse koḍhiyā | māsiyā kope || Jñāne.18.136 || Taise phaḷakāma durbaḷa | mhaṇatī karmachi kiḍāḷa | [tyājyaṁ] maga nirṇaya detī kevaḷa | tyajāve aisā || Jñāne.18.137 || [Yajñadānatapaḥkarma] Eka mhaṇatī yāgādika | karāveṅchi āvashyaka | je yāvāṅchūni shodhaka | āna nase || Jñāne.18.138 || Manashuddhīchyā mārgī | jai vijayī vhāve vegī | tai karma sabaḷālāgī | āḷasa na kīje || Jñāne.18.139 || Bhāṅgāra āthi shodhāve | tarī āgī jevi nubagāve | kā darpaṇālāgī sāṅchāve | adhika raja || Jñāne.18.140 || Nānā vastre chokha hoāvī | aise āthī ĵarī jīvī | tarī saṅvadaṇī na mānāvī | malina jaisī || Jñāne.18.141 || Taisī karme kleshakāre | [na tyājyamiti chāpare] mhaṇauni na nyāvī avhere | kā annalābhe aruvāre | rāṅdhitiye uṇe || Jñāne.18.142 || Iṁhī iṅhī gā shabdī | ekakarmī bāṅdhatī buddhī | aisā tyāga visaṁvādī | paḍoni ṭhelā || Jñāne.18.143 || [Chūrṇikā] Tari visaṁvāda to phiṭe | tyāgāchā nishchaya bheṭe | taise bolo gomaṭe | avadhāna deī || Jñāne.18.144 ||

Nishchayaṁ shrruṇu me tatra tyāge bharatasattama | tyāgo hi puruṣhavyāghra trividhaḥ(s) samprakīrtitaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.4 ||

[Tyāgo hīti] Tari tyāga ethe Pāṅḍavā | trividha pai jāṇāvā | tayā trividhāhī baravā | vibhāga karū || Jñāne.18.145 || Tyāgāche tinhī prakāra | kījatī ĵarī gochara | tarī tū ityarthāche sāra | itule ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.146 || [Nishchayamiti] Maĵa sarvajñāchiyehī buddhī | je aloṭa māne trishuddhī | nishchayatattwa te ādhī | avadhārī pā || Jñāne.18.147 || [Chūrṇikā] Tari āpulīye soḍavaṇe | ĵo mumukṣhū jāgo mhaṇe | tayā sarvaswe karaṇe | heeṅchi eka || Jñāne.18.148 ||

Yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyaṁ(ṅ) kāryameva tat | yajño dānaṁ(n) tapashchaiva pāvanāni manīṣhiṇām || Bha.Gī.18.5 ||

[Yajñadānatapaḥkarma na tyājyaṁ] Jiye yajñadānatapādike | iye karme āvashyake | tiye na sāṅḍāvī pāṅthike | pāule jaisī || Jñāne.18.149 || Harapale na dekhije | tava tayāĉhā māgu na sāṅḍije | kā trupta na hotā na loṭije | bhāṇe jevī || Jñāne.18.150 || Nāva thaḍī na pavatā | na sāṅḍije keḷī na phaḷatā | kā ṭhevile na disatā | dīpa jaisā || Jñāne.18.151 || Taisī ātmajñānāvikhī | jaṅva nishchitī nāhī nikī | tava nohāve yāgādikī | udāsīna || Jñāne.18.152 || [Kāryameva tat] Tari swādhikārānurūpe | tiye yajña dāne tape | anuṣhṭhāvīṅchi sākṣhepe | adhikeṁvara || Jñāne.18.153 || Je chālaṇe vegāvata jāye | to vega baisāvayāchi hoye | taisā karmātishaya āhe | naiṣhkarmyālāgī || Jñāne.18.154 || Adhike jaṅva ĵava auṣhadhī | sevāyāchī māṅḍī bāṅdhī | tava tava mukije vyādhī | tayāchiye || Jñāne.18.155 || Taisī karme hātopātī | jai kījatī yathānigutī | tai rajatame jhaḍatī | jhāḍā deunī || Jñāne.18.156 || Kā pāṭovāṭī puṭe | bhāṅgārā khāra deṇe ghaṭe | tai kīḍa ĵhaḍakarī tuṭe | nirvyāja hoya || Jñāne.18.157 || Taise niṣhṭhā kele karma | te sāṅḍī karūni rajatama | sattwashuddhīche dhāma | ḍoḷā dāvī || Jñāne.18.158 || Mhaṇauniyā dhanaṅjayā | sattwashuddhī giṁvasitayā | tīrthāṅchiyā sāvāyā | ālī karme || Jñāne.18.159 || Tīrthe bāhyamaḷa kṣhāḷe | karme abhyaṅtara ujaḷe | eva tīrthe ĵāṇa nirmaḷe | satkarmeṅchi || Jñāne.18.160 || Truṣhārtā marudeshī | jhaḷe amrute voḷalī jaisī | kī aṅdhālāgī ḍoḷyāṁsī | sūrya ālā || Jñāne.18.161 || Buḍatayā nadīcha dhāṁvinnalī | paḍatayā pruthvīcha kaḷavaḷilī | nimatayā mrutyūne didhalī | āyuṣhyavruddhī || Jñāne.18.162 || Karme karmabaddhatā | mumukṣhū soḍavile Paṅḍusutā | jaisā rasarīti maratā | rākhilā viṣhe || Jñāne.18.163 || [Chūrṇikā] Taisī eke hātavaṭiyā | karme kījatī dhanaṅjayā | baṅdhakeṅchi soḍavāvayā | mukhye hotī || Jñāne.18.164 || Ātā techi hātavaṭī | tuĵa sāṅgo gomaṭī | jayā karmāṅte kirīṭī | karmachi ruse || Jñāne.18.165 ||

Etānyapi tu karmāṇi saṅggaṁ(n) tyaktwā phalāni cha | kartavyānīti me Pārth nishchitaṁ matamuttamam || Bha.Gī.18.6 ||

[Etānyapi tu karmāṇi] Tari mahāyāgapramukhe | karme niphajatāṁhī achuke | [saṅggaṁ(n) tyaktwā] kartepaṇāche na ṭake | phuṅjaṇe āṅgī || Jñāne.18.166 || Ĵo mole tīrthā jāye | tayā mī yātrā karīta āhe | aisiye shlāghyatechā nohe | toṣha jevī || Jñāne.18.167 || Kā mudrā samarthāchiyā | ĵo ekavaṭu jhoṁbe rāyā | to mī jiṇatā aisiyā | na yechi garvā || Jñāne.18.168 || Ĵo kāṁse lāgoni tare | tayā poṁhatī ūrmī nure | purohita nāviṣhkare | dātepaṇe || Jñāne.18.169 || Taise kartrutwa ahaṅkāre | neghoni yathāavasare | krutyajātāṅche mohare | sārījatī || Jñāne.18.170 || [Phalāni cha] Kelyā karmā Pāṅḍavā | ĵo āthī phaḷāchā yāvā | tayā moharā ho nedāvā | manoratha || Jñāne.18.171 || Ādhīṅchi phaḷī āsa tuṭiliyā | karme āraṅbhāvī dhanaṅjayā | parāve bāḷa dhāyā | pāḷije jaise || Jñāne.18.172 || Piṁparuvāṅchiyā āshā | na shiṁpije piṅpaḷa jaisā | taisiyā phaḷanirāshā | kījatī karme || Jñāne.18.173 || Sāṅḍūni dudhāchī ṭakaḷī | goṅvārī gāṁvadhenu veṅṭāḷī | kiṅbahunā karmaphaḷī | taise kīje || Jñāne.18.174 || [Kartavyānīti] Aisī he hātavaṭī | gheūni je kriyā uṭhī | āpaṇā āpuliyā gāṅṭhī | lāhechi to || Jñāne.18.175 || Mhaṇoni phaḷī lāga | sāṅḍonī dehasaṅga | karme karāvī hā chāṅga | niropa mājhā || Jñāne.18.176 || [Chūrṇikā] Ĵo jīvabaṅdhe shīṇalā | suṭake jāche āpalā | teṇe puḍhatapuḍhatī yā bolā | āna na kīje || Jñāne.18.177 ||

Niyatasya tu saṁ(n)nyāsaḥ(kh) karmaṇo nopapadyate | mohāttasya parityāgastāmasaḥ(ph) parikīrtitaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.7 ||

[Mohāditi] Nā tarī aṅdhārācheni rokhe | jaisī ḍoḷā roṅvijatī nakhe | taisā karmadweṣhe ashekhe | karmeṅchi sāṅḍī || Jñāne.18.178 || Tayāche karma sāṅḍaṇe | te tāmasa mī mhaṇe | shisārāche rāge lāvaṇe | shisachi jaise || Jñāne.18.179 || [Niyatasyeti] Hā gā mārga duvāḍa hoye | tarī nistaritīla pāye | kī techi khāṅḍaṇe āhe | mārgāparādhe || Jñāne.18.180 || Bhukeliyāpuḍhe anna | ho kā bhalataise ūnha | tarī buddhī na ghetā laṅghana | bhāṇe pāparā hālyā || Jñāne.18.181 || Taisā karmāchā bādha karme | nistarije kariteni varme | he tāmasa neṇe bhrame | mājavilā || Jñāne.18.182 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Kī swabhāve āle vibhāgā | te karmachi vosaṅḍī pai gā | tari ĵhaṇe ātaḷā tyāgā | tāmasā tayā || Jñāne.18.183 ||

Duḥ(hu)khamityeva yatkarma kāyakleshabhayāttyajet | sa krutwā rājasaṁ(n) tyāgaṁ(n) naiva tyāgaphalaṁ labhet || Bha.Gī.18.8 ||

[Duḥ(hu)khamityeva yatkarma] Athavā swādhikāra bujhe | āpale vihitahī sujhe | pari karitayā ubaje | nibarapaṇā || Jñāne.18.184 || Je karmāchī ailīkaḍa | nāveka dise duvāḍa | je vāhatiye veḷa jaḍa | shidorī jaisī || Jñāne.18.185 || Jaisā niṅba jibhe kaḍavaṭa | hiraḍā pahile turaṭa | taisā karmā aila sevaṭa | khaṇuvāḷā hoya || Jñāne.18.186 || Kā dhenū duvāḍa shiṅga | shevaṅtīye aḍava āṅga | bhojanasukha mahāga | pāka karitā || Jñāne.18.187 || Taise puḍhatapuḍhatī karma | āraṁbhīṅcha ativiṣhama | mhaṇauni to te shrama | karitā mānī || Jñāne.18.188 || Yerhavī vihitatwe māṅḍī | pari ghālitā asuravāḍī | tetha poḷalā aisā sāṅḍī | ādarileṁhī || Jñāne.18.189 || [Kāyakleshabhayāttyajet] Mhaṇe vastu dehāsārikhī | ālī bahutī bhāgyavishekhī | mā jāchū kā karmādikī | pāpiyā jaisā || Jñāne.18.190 || Kele karmī je dyāve | te ĵhaṇe maĵa hoāve | āji bhogu nā barave | hātiṅche bhoga || Jñāne.18.191 || Aisā sharīrāchiyā kleshā | bheṇe karme vīreshā | sāṅḍī to [sa krutwā rājasaṁ(n) tyāgaṁ] pariyesā | rājasa tyāga || Jñāne.18.192 || [Naiva tyāgaphalaṁ labhet] Yerhavī tethahī karma sāṅḍe | pari tayā tyāgaphaḷa na ĵoḍe | jaise utale āgī paḍe | te nalagechi homā || Jñāne.18.193 || Kā buḍoni prāṇa gele | te ardhodakī nimāle | he mhaṇo naye ĵāhale | durmaraṇachi || Jñāne.18.194 || Taise dehāchechi lobhe | jeṇe karmā pāṇī subhe | teṇe sācha na labhe | tyāgāche phaḷa || Jñāne.18.195 || [Chūrṇikā] Kiṁbahunā āpule | jai jñāna hoya udayā āle | tai nakṣhatrāṅte pāhale | giḷī jaise || Jñāne.18.196 || Taishā sakāraṇa kriyā | hārapatī dhanaṅjayā | to karmatyāga ye jayā | mokṣhaphaḷāsī || Jñāne.18.197 || Te mokṣhaphaḷa ajñānā | tyāgiyā nāhī Arjunā | mhaṇoni to tyāga na mānā | rājasu to || Jñāne.18.198 || Tari koṇe pā etha tyāge | te mokṣhaphaḷa ghara righe | heṁhī āika prasaṅge | bolijela || Jñāne.18.199 ||

Kāryamityeva yatkarma niyataṁ(ṅ) kriyate’rjuna | saṅggaṁ(n) tyaktwā phalaṁ(ñ) chaiva sa tyāgaḥ(s) sāttwiko mataḥ || Bha.Gī.18.9 ||

[Kāryamiti] Tari swādhikārācheni nāve | je vāṅṭiyā āle swabhāve | te āchare vidhigaurave | shrruṅgāroni || Jñāne.18.200 || [Saṅggaṁ(n) tyaktwā phalaṁ(ñ) chaiva] Pari he mī karita ase | aisā āṭhava tyajī mānase | taiseṅchi pāṇī de āshe | phaḷāchiye || Jñāne.18.201 || Pai avajñā āṇi kāmanā | mātechyā ṭhāyī Arjunā | keliyā donī patanā | kāraṇa hotī || Jñāne.18.202 || Tari donī ye tyajāvī | maga mātāchi te bhajāvī | vāṅchūni mukhālāgī vāḷāvī | gāyachi sagaḷī || Jñāne.18.203 || Āvaḍatiyehī phaḷī | asāre sālī āṅṭhoḷī | tyāsāṭhī avagaḷī | phaḷāte koṇhī || Jñāne.18.204 || Taisā kartrutwāchā mada | āṇi karmaphaḷāchā āswāda | yā dohīṅche nāṁva baṅdha | karmāchā kī || Jñāne.18.205 || Tari yā dohīṅchyā vikhī | jaisā bāpa nātaḷe leṅkī | taisā ho na shake duḥkhī | vihitā kriyā || Jñāne.18.206 || [Sa tyāgaḥ(s) sāttwiko mataḥ] Hā to tyāga taruvara | ĵo gā mokṣhaphaḷe ye thora | sāttwika aisā ḍagara | yāsīṅcha jagī || Jñāne.18.207 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Ātā ĵāḷūni bīja jaise | jhāḍā kīje nirvaṁshe | phaḷa tyāgūni karma taise | tyajile jeṇe || Jñāne.18.208 || Tayā lāgatakheṁvo parisī | dhātūchi gaṅdhikāḷimā jaisī | jātī rajatame taisī | tuṭalī donhī || Jñāne.18.209 || Maga sattwe chokhāḷe | ughaḍatī ātmabodhāche ḍoḷe | tetha mrugāṁbu sāṅjaveḷe | hoya jaise || Jñāne.18.210 || Taisā buddhyādikāṁpuḍhā | asatachi vishwābhāsa yevaḍhā | to na dekhe kavaṇīkaḍā | ākāsha jaise || Jñāne.18.211 ||

Na dweṣhṭyakushalaṁ(ṅ) karma kushale nānuṣhajjate | tyāgī sattwasamāviṣhṭo medhāvī chhinnasaṁshayaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.10 ||

[Na dweṣhṭīti] Āṇi prāchīnācheni baḷe | ālī krutye kushalākushale | tiye vyomāāṅgī ābhāḷe | virālī jaisī || Jñāne.18.212 || Taisī tayāchiye diṭhī | karme chokhāḷalī kirīṭī | mhaṇoni sukhaduḥkhī uṭhī | paḍenā to || Jñāne.18.213 || Teṇe shubhakarma ĵāṇāve | maga te harṣhe karāve | kā ashubhālāgī vhāve | dweṣhiyā nā || Jñāne.18.214 || [Chhinnasaṁshayaḥ] Tari iyā viṣhayīṅchā kāhī | tayā ekahī saṅdeha nāhī | jaisā swapnāchyā ṭhāyī | jāginnaliyā || Jñāne.18.215 || [Medhāvī] Mhaṇaūni karma āṇi kartā | yā dwaitabhāvāchī vārtā | neṇe to Paṅḍusutā | [tyāgī sattwasamāviṣhṭo] sāttwika tyāga || Jñāne.18.216 || [Chūrṇikā] Aiseni karme Pārthā | tyajilī tyajitī sarvathā | adhike bāṅdhatī anyathā | sāṅḍilī tarī || Jñāne.18.217 ||

Na hi dehabhrutā shakyaṁ(n) tyaktuṁ(ṅ) karmāṇyasheṣhataḥ | yastu karmaphalatyāgī sa tyāgītyabhidhīyate || Bha.Gī.18.11 ||

[Na hi dehabhruteti] Āṇi hā gā savyasāchī | mūrti lāhoni dehāchī | khaṅtī karitī karmāchī | te gāṅvaḍhe gā || Jñāne.18.218 || Mruttikechā vīṭa | gheūni kāya karīla ghaṭa | keute taṅtū paṭa | sāṅḍīla to || Jñāne.18.219 || Tevīṅchi vahnitwa āṅgī | āṇi ube ubagaṇe āgī | kī to dīpa prabhelāgī | dweṣha karīla kāī || Jñāne.18.220 || Hiṅga trāsalā ghāṇī | tarī kaiṅche sugaṅdhatwa āṇī | drava sāṅḍūni pāṇī | ke rāhe te || Jñāne.18.221 || Taisā sharīrācheni ābhāse | nāṅdata ĵava ase | tava karmatyāgāche pise | kāise tarī || Jñāne.18.222 || Āpaṇa lāvije ṭiḷā | mhaṇoni puso ye avalīḷā | mā ghālī pheḍī niḍaḷā | kā karū ye gā || Jñāne.18.223 || Taise vihita swaye ādarile | mhaṇoni tyajū ye tyajile | pari karmachi deha ātale | te kā sāṅḍīla gā || Jñāne.18.224 || Je shwāsochchhvāsavarī | hota nijeliyāhī varī | kāhī na karaṇeṅchi parī | hotī jayāchī || Jñāne.18.225 || Yā sharīrācheni misake | karmahī lāgale asike | jitā melayā na ṭhāke | iyā rītī || Jñāne.18.226 || [Yastu karmaphalatyāgī] Yayā karmāte sāṅḍitī parī | ekīchi te avadhārī | je karitā na jāije hārī | phaḷāshechiye || Jñāne.18.227 || Karmaphaḷa īshwarī arpe | tatprasāde bodha uddīpe | tetha rajjujñāne lope | vyāḷashaṅkā || Jñāne.18.228 || Teṇe ātmabodhe taise | avidyesī karma nāshe | [sa tyāgītyabhidhīyate] Pārthā tyajije jai aise | tai tyajile hoya || Jñāne.18.229 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Mhaṇoni iyāparī jagī | karme tyajī to mahātyāgī | yera mūrchchhane nāṁva rogī | vishrāṅti jaisī || Jñāne.18.230 || Taisā karmī shiṇe ekī | to visāvo pāhe āṇikī | dāṅḍeyāche ghāya bukī | dhāḍaṇe jaise || Jñāne.18.231 || [Chūrṇikā] Pari he aso puḍhatī | tochi tyāgī trijagatī | jeṇe phalatyāge niṣhkrutī | nele karma || Jñāne.18.232 ||

Aniṣhṭamiṣhṭaṁ mishraṁ(ñ) cha trividhaṁ(ṅ) karmaṇaḥ(ph) phalam | bhavatyatyāgināṁ pretya na tu saṁ(n)nyāsināṁ(ṅ) kvachit || Bha.Gī.18.12 ||

Yerhavī tarī dhanaṅjayā | trividhā karmaphaḷā gā yayā | samartha te kī bhogāvayā | je na sāṅḍitīchi āshā || Jñāne.18.233 || Āpaṇachi viūni duhitā | kī na mama mhaṇe pitā | to suṭe kī pratigrahītā | jāṁvāī shirake || Jñāne.18.234 || Viṣhāche āgarahī vāhatī | te vikitā suṭale jitī | yera nimāle je ghetī | veṅchoni mole || Jñāne.18.235 || Taise kartā karma karū | akartā phaḷāshā na dharū | etha na shake āvarū | dohīṅte karma || Jñāne.18.236 || Vāṭe pikaliyā vrukṣhāche | phaḷa apekṣhī tayāche | tevi sādhāraṇa karmāṅche | phaḷa ghetayā || Jñāne.18.237 || Pari karūni phaḷa neghe | to jagāchyā kāmī na righe | je trividha jaga avaghe | karmakamaḷa he || Jñāne.18.238 || Deva manuṣhya sthāvara | yayā nāṅva jagaḍaṁbara | āṇi he tava tīnhī prakāra | karmaphaḷāche || Jñāne.18.239 || Techi eka gā aniṣhṭa | eka te kevaḷa iṣhṭa | āṇi eka iṣhṭāniṣhṭa | trividha aise || Jñāne.18.240 || [Aniṣhṭaṁ] Pari viṣhayamatā buddhī | āṅgī sūni avadhī | pravartatī je niṣhiddhī | kuvyāpārī || Jñāne.18.241 || Tetha krumi kīṭa loṣhṭa | he deha lāhatī nikruṣhṭa | tayā nāma te aniṣhṭa | karmaphaḷa || Jñāne.18.242 || [Iṣhṭaṁ] Kā swadharmā māna detā | swādhikāra puḍhā sūtā | sukruta kīje pusatā | āmnāyāte || Jñāne.18.243 || Tai iṅdrādika devāṅchī | dehe lāhijatī savyasāchī | tayā karmaphaḷā iṣhṭāchī | prasiddhī gā || Jñāne.18.244 || [Mishraṁ(ñ) cha] Āṇi goḍa āṁbaṭa miḷe | tetha rasāṅtara pharasāḷe | uṭhī dohī vegaḷe | dohī jiṇate || Jñāne.18.245 || Rechakachi yogavashe | hoya staṁbhāvayādoṣhe | satyāsatya-samarase | satyāsatyachi jiṇije || Jñāne.18.246 || Mhaṇoni samabhāge shubhāshubhe | miḷoni anuṣhṭhānāche ubhe | teṇe manuṣhyatwa lābhe | te mishra phaḷa || Jñāne.18.247 || [Trividhaṁ(ṅ) karmaṇaḥ(ph) phalaṁ] Aise trividha yayā bhāgī | karmaphaḷa māṅḍaleṅse jagī | [bhavatyatyāgināṁ pretya] he na sāṅḍī tayā bhogī | je sūdale āshā || Jñāne.18.248 || Jetha jivhechā hāta phāṅṭe | tava jevitā vāṭe gomaṭe | maga pariṇāmī shevaṭe | avashya maraṇa || Jñāne.18.249 || Saṁvachora maitrī chāṅga | jaṅva na pavije te dāṅga | sāmānyā bhalī āṅga | na shive tava || Jñāne.18.250 || Taisī karme karitā sharīrī | lāhatī mahattwāchī pharārī | pāṭhī nidhanī ekasarī | pāvatī phaḷe || Jñāne.18.251 || Jaisā samartha āṇi rhuṇiyā | māgo ālā bāiṇiyā | na loṭe taisā prāṇiyā | paḍe to bhoga || Jñāne.18.252 || Maga kaṇisauni kaṇa jhaḍe | to virūḍhalā kaṇisā chaḍhe | puḍhatī bhūmī paḍe | puḍhatī uṭhī || Jñāne.18.253 || Taise bhogī je phaḷa hoya | te phaḷāṅtare vīta ĵāya | ĉhālatā pāye pāya | jiṇije jaisā || Jñāne.18.254 || Utārāchiye sāṅgaḍī | ṭhāke te ailīcha thaḍī | tevi na mūkījatī voḍhī | bhogyāchiye || Jñāne.18.255 || Pai sādhya sādhana prakāre | phaḷabhoga to pasare | eva goṁvile saṁsāre | atyāgī te || Jñāne.18.256 || [Na tu saṁ(n)nyāsināṁ(ṅ) kvachit] Yerhavī jātipuṣhpāṅche vikasaṇe | tyāchi nāma jaise sukaṇe | taise karmamiṣhe na karaṇe | kele jiṁhī || Jñāne.18.257 || Bījachi varosi veṅche | tetha vāḍhatī kuḷavāḍī khāṅche | tevi phaḷatyāge karmāche | sārile kāma || Jñāne.18.258 || Te sattwashuddhī sāhākāre | gurukrupāmrutatuṣhāre | sāsinnaleni vosare | dwaitadainya || Jñāne.18.259 || Tevhā jagadābhāsamiṣhe | sphure te trividha phaḷa nāshe | etha bhoktā bhogya āpaise | nimāle he || Jñāne.18.260 || Ghaḍe jñānapradhāna aisā | saṅnyāsa jayā vīreshā | techi phaḷabhoga sosā | mukale gā || Jñāne.18.261 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Āṇi yeṇe kīra saṅnyāse | jai ātmarūpī diṭhī paise | tai karma eka aise | dekhaṇe āhe || Jñāne.18.262 || Paḍoni geliyā bhiṅtī | chitrāṅchī kevaḷa hoya mātī | kā pāhāleyā rātī | āṅdhāre ure || Jñāne.18.263 || Jai rūpachi nāhī ubhe | tai chhāyā kāhyāchī shobhe | darpaṇeṁvīṇa biṁbe | vadana ke pā || Jñāne.18.264 || Phiṭaliyā nidrechā ṭhāva | kaiṅchā swapnāsi prastāva | maga satya kī te vāva | koṇa mhaṇe || Jñāne.18.265 || Taise gā saṅnyāse yeṇe | tava avidyesīchi nāhī jiṇe | mā tiyeche kārya koṇe | ghepedīpe || Jñāne.18.266 || Mhaṇoni saṅnyāsiye pāhī | karmāchī goṭhī kījela kāī | [chūrṇikā] pari avidyā āpulyā dehī | āhe jai kā || Jñāne.18.267 || Kartepaṇācheni thāṁve | ātmā shubhāshubhī dhāṁve | druṣhṭi bhedāchiye rāṇive | rachalīse jai || Jñāne.18.268 || Tai tarī gā suvarmā | bījāvaḷī ātmayā karmā | apāḍe jaisī pashchimā | pūrvesi kā || Jñāne.18.269 || Nā tarī ākāshā kā ābhāḷā | sūryā āṇi mrugajaḷā | bījāvaḷī bhūtaḷā | vāyūsi jaisī || Jñāne.18.270 || Pāṅgharoni naīṅche udaka | ase naīṅmāji khaḍaka | pari jāṇije kā vegaḷika | koḍīchī te || Jñāne.18.271 || Ho kā udakāĵavaḷī | pari sinīchi te bābuḷī | kāya saṅgāstava kāĵaḷī | dīpa mhaṇo ye || Jñāne.18.272 || Ĵarī chaṅdrī jālā kalaṅka | tari chaṅdreṅsī navhe eka | āhe druṣhṭī ḍoḷyā viveka | apāḍa jetulā || Jñāne.18.273 || Nānā vāṭā vāṭe jātayā | voghā voghī vāhatayā | ārasā ārasā pāhatayā | apāḍa jetulā || Jñāne.18.274 || Pārthā gā tetuleni māne | ātmenisī karma sine | pari ghevavije ajñāne | te kīra aise || Jñāne.18.275 || Vikāse ravīte upajavī | drutī alīkaravī bhogavī | te sarovarī kā baravī | abjiṇī jaisī || Jñāne.18.276 || Puḍhatapuḍhatī ātmakriyā | anyakāraṇakāchi taishiyā | karū pāṅchāṅhī tayā | kāraṇā rūpa || Jñāne.18.277 || [Saptamādhyāyoktaṁ(ñ) jñānavijñānayogamāha chaturbhiḥ(hi)]-

Pañchaitāni mahābāho kāraṇāni nibodha me | sāṅgkhye krutānte proktāni siddhaye sarvakarmaṇām || Bha.Gī.18.13 ||

[Pañchaitāni mahābāho kāraṇāni] Āṇi pāṁ(ñ)chahī kāraṇeṁ(n) tiyeṁ | tūṁ(ñ)hī ĵāṇasīla vipāyeṁ | [sāṅgkhye krutānte proktāni] je shāstreṁ ubhaūni bāhe | bolatī jayāṁ(n)teṁ || Jñāne.18.278 || Vedarāyāchiyā rājadhānīṁ | sāṁ(ṅ)khya-vedāṁ(n)tāṁ(ñ)chyā bhuvanīṁ | nirūpaṇāchyā nishāṇadhwanīṁ | garjatī jiyeṁ || Jñāne.18.279 || [Siddhaye sarvakarmaṇāṁ] Je sarvakarmasiddhīlāgīṁ | iyeṁ(ñ)chi mudaleṁ ho jagīṁ | tetha na suvāvā abhaṁ(ṅ)gīṁ | ātmarāja || Jñāne.18.280 || Iyā bolāche ḍāṁ(ṅ)guraṭī | tiyeṁ prasiddhī ālīṁ(ṅ) kirīṭī | mhaṇoni tujhyā hana Karṇapuṭīṁ | vasota kāṁ(ñ) je || Jñāne.18.281 || [Nibodha me] Āṇi mukhāṁ(n)tarīṁ āikije | taiseṁ(ṅ) kāyaseṁ heṁ ojheṁ | mī chidratna tuĵhe | asatāṁ hātīṁ || Jñāne.18.282 || Darpaṇa puḍhāṁ māṁ(ṅ)ḍaleyā | kāṁ lokāṁ(ñ)chiyā ḍoḷyāṁ | māna dyāyā pahāvayā | āpuleṁ(n) nikeṁ || Jñāne.18.283 || Bhakta jaiseni jetha pāhe | tetha teṁ(n) teṁ(ñ)chi hota jāye | to mī tuĵheṁ(ñ) jāhaloṁ āheṁ | kheḷaṇeṁ ājī || Jñāne.18.284 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Aiseṁ heṁ prītīcheni vegeṁ | deva bolatāṁ se neghe | tava ānaṁ(n)dāmājī āṁ(ṅ)geṁ | virata Pārth || Jñāne.18.285 || Chāṁ(n)diṇiyāĉhā paḍibhara | hotāṁ somakāṁ(n)tāchā ḍoṁ(ṅ)gara | vigharoni sarovara | hoṁ pāhe jaisā || Jñāne.18.286 || Taiseṁ sukha āṇi anubhūtī | yā bhāvāṁ(ñ)chī moḍūni bhiṁ(n)tī | ātaleṁ Arjunākrutī | sukhachi jetha || Jñāne.18.287 || Tetha samartha mhaṇauni devā | avakāsha jāhālā āṭhavā | maga buḍatayāĉhā dhāṁvā | jīveṁ(ṅ) kelā || Jñāne.18.288 || Arjunā yesaṇeṁ(n) dheṁ(ṅ)ḍeṁ | prajñāpasareṁsīṁ buḍe | āleṁ bharateṁ evaḍheṁ | teṁ sāṁvarūni || Jñāne.18.289 || Deva mhaṇe hāṁ(ṅ) gā Pārthā | tūṁ āpaṇapeṁ(n) dekha sarvathā | tava sāṁvarūni yereṁ māthā | tukiyelā || Jñāne.18.290 || Mhaṇe ĵāṇasī dātārā | mī tuĵasīṁ vyaktishejārā | ubagalā ādīṁ ekāhārā | yevoṁ pāheṁ || Jñāne.18.291 || Tayāhī hā aisā | lobheṁ(n) detasāṁ(ñ) ĵarī lālasā | tarī kāṁ(ñ) jī ghālītasāṁ | āḍa āḍa jīvā || Jñāne.18.292 || Tetha ShreeKriṣhṇa mhaṇatī nikeṁ | adyāpi nāhīṁ mā ṭhāukeṁ | veḍyā chaṁ(n)drā āṇi chaṁ(n)drike | na miḷaṇeṁ āhe || Jñāne.18.293 || Āṇi hāhī boloni bhāvo | tuĵa dāūṁ āmhī bhivoṁ | je rusatāṁ bāṁ(n)dhe thāvo | teṁ prema gā heṁ || Jñāne.18.294 || Etha ekamekāṁ(ñ)chiye khuṇe | visaṁ(n)vāda taṁ(ñ)va jiṇeṁ | mhaṇauni aso heṁ bolaṇeṁ | iyeviṣhayīṁ(ñ)cheṁ || Jñāne.18.295 || Maga kasakaseṁ(n) teṁ ātāṁ | bolata hotoṁ paṁ(ṅ)ḍusutā | sarva karmāṁ bhinnatā | ātmenisīṁ || Jñāne.18.296 || Tava Arjun mhaṇe deveṁ | mājhiye manīṁ(ñ)cheṁ(ñ)chi swabhāveṁ | prastāvileṁ baraveṁ | prameya teṁ(ñ) jī || Jñāne.18.297 || Jeṁ sakaḷa karmāṁ(ñ)cheṁ bīja | kāraṇapaṁ(n)chaka tuĵa | sāṁ(ṅ)gena aisī paija | ghetalī kāṁ || Jñāne.18.298 || Āṇi ātmayā etha kāṁhīṁ | sarvathā lāga nāhīṁ | heṁ puḍhāralāsi teṁ(n) deīṁ | lāhāṇeṁ māĵheṁ || Jñāne.18.299 || Yayā bolā vishwesheṁ | mhaṇitaleṁ(n) toṣheṁ bahuvaseṁ | iyeviṣhayīṁ(n) dharaṇeṁ baise | aiseṁ(ṅ) keṁ(ñ) ĵoḍe || Jñāne.18.300 || Tarī Arjunā nirūpijela | teṁ(ṅ) kīra bhāṣheāṁ(n)tula | pari mechu ye hoijela | rhuṇiyā tuĵa || Jñāne.18.301 || Tava Arjun mhaṇe devo | kāī visarale māgīla bhāvo | iye goṭhī kī rākhata āhoṁ | mītūṁ(ñ)paṇa jī || Jñāne.18.302 || Etha ShreeKriṣhṇa mhaṇatī ho kāṁ | ātāṁ avadhānāchā pasara nikā | karūniyāṁ āikā | puḍhāraloṁ(n) teṁ || Jñāne.18.303 || [Chūrṇikā shlokatrayasya] Tari satyachi gā dhanurdharā | sarva karmāṁ(ñ)chā ubhārā | hotase bāhira-bāhirā | karaṇeṁ pāṁ(ñ)cheṁ || Jñāne.18.304 || Āṇi paṁ(n)chakāraṇa daḷavāḍeṁ | jihīṁ(ṅ) karmākāra māṁ(ṅ)ḍe | te hetu tava ughaḍe | pāṁ(ñ)cha āthī || Jñāne.18.305 || Yetha ātmatattwa udāsīna | teṁ(n) nā hetu nā upādāna | nā teṁ aṁ(ṅ)ga karī saṁvāhana | karmasiddhīcheṁ || Jñāne.18.306 || Tetha shubhāshubhīṁ aṁshīṁ | niphajatī karmeṁ aisīṁ | rātīdivo āKāshīṁ | jiyāparī || Jñāne.18.307 || Toya teja dhūma | yayāṁ vāyūsī saṁ(ṅ)gama | jāliyā hoya abhrāgama | vyoma teṁ(n) neṇe || Jñāne.18.308 || Nānā kāṣhṭhīṁ(n) nāva miḷe | te nāvāḍeni chaḷe | chālavije aniḷeṁ | udaka teṁ sākṣhī || Jñāne.18.309 || Kāṁ(ṅ) kavaṇeṁ ekeṁ piṁ(ṅ)ḍeṁ | veṁ(ñ)chitāṁ avatare bhāṁ(ṅ)ḍeṁ | maga bhavaṁ(n)ḍije daṁ(ṅ)ḍeṁ | bhrame chakra || Jñāne.18.310 || Āṇi kartrutwa kulālācheṁ | tetha kāya teṁ pruthvīyecheṁ | ādhārāvāṁ(ñ)chūni veṁ(ñ)che | vichārīṁ pāṁ || Jñāne.18.311 || Heṁhī aso lokāṁ(ñ)chiyā | rāhāṭī hotāṁ āghaviyā | koṇa kāma savitayā | āṁ(ṅ)gā āleṁ || Jñāne.18.312 || Taiseṁ pāṁ(ñ)cha hetumiḷaṇīṁ | pāṁ(ñ)cheṁ(ñ)chi iṁ(ṅ)hīṁ(ṅ) kāraṇīṁ | kīje karmalatāṁ(ñ)chī lāvaṇī | ātmā sinā || Jñāne.18.313 || Ātāṁ yechi vegaḷālīṁ | pāṁ(ñ)chahī vivaṁ(ñ)chūṁ(ṅ) gā bhalīṁ | tukoni ghetalīṁ | motiyeṁ(ñ) jaisīṁ || Jñāne.18.314 ||

Adhiṣhṭhānaṁ(n) tathā kartā karaṇaṁ(ñ) cha pruthagvidham | vividhāshcha pruthakcheṣhṭā daivaṁ(ñ) chaivātra pañchamam || Bha.Gī.18.14 ||

[Adhiṣhṭhānaṁ] Taisī yathālakṣhaṇe | āike pāṅcha kāraṇe | tari deha he mī mhaṇe | pahile etha || Jñāne.18.315 || Yayāte adhiṣhṭhāna aise | mhaṇije te yāchi doṣhe | je swabhāgyeṁsī vase | bhoktā yetha || Jñāne.18.316 || Iṅdriyāṅchyā dāhe hātī | jāchoni divorātī | sukhaduḥkhe prakrutī | ĵoḍījatī jiye || Jñāne.18.317 || Tiye bhogāvayā purukhā | āna ṭhāvochi nāhī dekhā | mhaṇauni adhiṣhṭhānabhākhā | bolije deha || Jñāne.18.318 || He chovisāṅhī tattwāṅche | kuṭuṁbagharavastīche | tuṭe baṅdhamokṣhāṅche | guṅthāḍe etha || Jñāne.18.319 || Kiṁbahunā avasthātrayā | he adhiṣhṭhāna dhanaṅjayā | mhaṇoni dehā yayā | hechi nāma || Jñāne.18.320 || [Tathā kartā] Āṇi kartā he duje | karmāche kāraṇa jāṇije | pratibiṁba mhaṇije | chaitanyāche je || Jñāne.18.321 || Ākāshachi varṣhe nīra | te taḷavaṭī bāṅdhe nāḍara | maga biṅboni tadākāra | hoya jevī || Jñāne.18.322 || Kā nidrābhare bahuve | rāyā rāyapaṇa ṭhāuve navhe | maga swapnīṅchiye sāmāve | raṅkapaṇī || Jñāne.18.323 || Taise āpuleni visare | chaitanyachi dehākāre | ābhāsoni āviṣhkare | dehapaṇe je || Jñāne.18.324 || Jayā vichārāchyā deshī | prasiddhi gā jīva aisī | jeṇe bhāṣha kelī deheṁsī | āghavāṁviṣhayī || Jñāne.18.325 || Prakrutī karī karme | to myā kelī mhaṇe bhrame | yetha kartā yeṇe nāme | bolije jīva || Jñāne.18.326 || [Karaṇaṁ(ñ) cha pruthagvidhaṁ] Maga pāteyāṅchyā keshī | ekīcha uṭhatī diṭhī jaisī | mokaḷīcha varī aisī | chirīva game || Jñāne.18.327 || Kā gharāāṅtula eka | dīpāchā avaloka | gavākṣhabhede aneka | āvaḍe jevī || Jñāne.18.328 || Kā ekachi puruṣha jaisā | anusarata navā rasā | navavidha aisā | āvaḍo lāge || Jñāne.18.329 || Tevi buddhīche eka ĵāṇaṇe | shrotrādibhede yeṇe | bāheri iṅdriyapaṇe | phāṅke je kā || Jñāne.18.330 || Te pruthagvidha karaṇa | karmāche iyā kāraṇa | tisare gā ĵāṇa | nrupanaṅdanā || Jñāne.18.331 || [Vividhā cha pruthakcheṣhṭā] Āṇi pūrvapashchimavāhaṇī | nighāliyā voghāchiyā miḷaṇī | hoya nadī nada pāṇī | ekachi jevī || Jñāne.18.332 || Taisī kriyāshakti pavanī | ase je anapāyinī | te paḍilī nānā sthānī | nānā hoya || Jñāne.18.333 || Jai vāche karī yeṇe | tai techi hoya bolaṇe | hātā ālī tarī gheṇe | deṇe hoya || Jñāne.18.334 || Agā charaṇāchyā ṭhāyī | tari gatī techi pāhī | adhodwārī dohī | kṣharaṇe techi || Jñāne.18.335 || Kaṅdauni hrudayavarī | praṇavāchī uĵarī | karitā techi sharīrī | prāṇa mhaṇije || Jñāne.18.336 || Maga urdhwīṅchiyā rigānigā | puḍhatī techi shakti pai gā | udāna aisiyā liṅgā | pātra jāhālī || Jñāne.18.337 || Adhoraṅdhrācheni vāhe | apāna he nāma lāhe | vyāpakapaṇe hoye | vyāna techi || Jñāne.18.338 || Ārogileni rase | sharīra bharī sarise | āṇi na sāṅḍitā ase | sarvasaṅdhī || Jñāne.18.339 || Aisiyā iyā rāhaṭī | maga techi kriyā pāṭhī | samāna aisī kirīṭī | bolije gā || Jñāne.18.340 || Āṇi jāṁbhaī shiṅka ḍheṅkara | aisaisā hotase vyāpāra | nāga kūrma krukara | ityādi hoya || Jñāne.18.341 || Eva vāyūchī he cheṣhṭā | ekīchi pari subhaṭā | vartanāstava pālaṭā | yetase je || Jñāne.18.342 || Te bhedalī vruttipaṅthe | vāyushaktī gā ethe | karmakāraṇa chauthe | aise ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.343 || [Daivaṁ(ñ) chaivātra pañchamaṁ] Āṇi rhutu baravā Shāradu | Shāradī puḍhatī chāṅdu | chaṅdrī jaisā saṁbaṅdhu | pūrṇimechā || Jñāne.18.344 || Kā vasaṅtī baravā ārāma | ārāmī priyāsaṅgama | saṅgamī āgama | upachārāṅchā || Jñāne.18.345 || Nānā kamaḷī Pāṅḍavā | vikāsa jaisā baravā | vikāsīṁhī yāvā | parāgāchā to || Jñāne.18.346 || Vāche barave kavitwa | kavitwī barave rasikatwa | rasikatwī paratattwa | sparsha jaisā || Jñāne.18.347 || Taisī sarvavruttivaibhavī | buddhīchi ekalī baravī | buddhīhī barava navī | iṅdriya prauḍhī || Jñāne.18.348 || Iṅdriyaprauḍhīmaṅḍaḷā | shrruṅgāra ekachi nirmaḷā | jai adhiṣhṭhātriya kā meḷā | daivatāṅchā ĵo || Jñāne.18.349 || Mhaṇūni chakṣhurādikī dāhe | iṅdriyā pāṭhī swānugrahe | sūryādikā kā āhe | surāṅchee vruṅda || Jñāne.18.350 || Te devavruṅda barave | karmakāraṇa pāṅchave | Arjunā etha ĵāṇāve | deva mhaṇe || Jñāne.18.351 || Eva māne tujhiye āyaṇī | taisī karmajātāṅchī he khāṇī | paṅchavidha ākarṇī | nirūpilī || Jñāne.18.352 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā hechi khāṇī vāḍhe | maga karmāchī sruṣhṭī ghaḍe | jihī te hetuhī ughaḍe | dāū pāṅchai || Jñāne.18.353 ||

Sharīravāṅgmanobhiryatkarma prārabhate naraḥ | nyāyyaṁ vā viparītaṁ vā pañchaite tasya hetavaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.15 ||

[Sharīravāṅgmanobhiriti pratyekaṁ padaṁ vyāchaṣhṭe tatra manasā] Tari avasāṅta ālī mādhavī | te hetu hoya navapallavī | pallava puṣhpapuṅja dāvī | puṣhpa phaḷāṅte || Jñāne.18.354 || Kā vārṣhiye āṇije megha | meghe vruṣhṭiprasaṅga | vruṣhṭīstava bhoga | sasyasukhāchā || Jñāne.18.355 || Nā tarī prāchī aruṇāte viye | aruṇe sūryodaya hoye | sūrye sagaḷā pāhe | divasa jaisā || Jñāne.18.356 || Taise mana hetu Pāṅḍavā | hoya karmasaṅkalpabhāvā | to saṅkalpa lāvī divā | vāchechā gā || Jñāne.18.357 || [Vāchā] Maga vāchechā to divaṭā | dāvī krutyajātāchiyā vāṭā | tevhā kartā rige kāmaṭhā | kartrutwāchyā || Jñāne.18.358 || [Sharīreṇa] Tetha sharīrādika daḷavāḍe | sharīrādikā hetūchi ghaḍe | lohakāma lokhaṅḍe | nirvāḷije jaise || Jñāne.18.359 || Kā tāṅthuvāchā tāṇā | tāṅthu ghālitā vairaṇā | to taṅtūchi vichakṣhaṇā | hoya paṭa || Jñāne.18.360 || Taise mana vāchā dehāche | karma manādi hetuchi rache | ratnī ghaḍe ratnāche | daḷavāḍe jevī || Jñāne.18.361 || [Yat] Etha sharīrādike kāraṇe | techi hetu kevi he koṇe | apekṣhije tari teṇe | avadhāriĵo || Jñāne.18.362 || [Tasya hetavaḥ] Āikā sūryāchiyā prakāshā | hetu kāraṇa sūryachi jaisā | kā uṅsāche kāṅḍe uṁsā | vāḍhi hetu || Jñāne.18.363 || Nānā vāgdevatā vānāvī | tai vāchāchi lāge kāmavāvī | kā vedā vedeṅchi bolāvī | pratiṣhṭhā jevī || Jñāne.18.364 || Taise karmā sharīrādike | kāraṇa he kīra ṭhāuke | pari hechi hetu na chuke | heṁhī etha || Jñāne.18.365 || [Karma prārabhate naraḥ] Āṇi dehādikī kāraṇī | dehādi hetumiḷaṇī | hoya jayā ubhāraṇī | karmajātā || Jñāne.18.366 || [Nyāyyaṁ vā] Te shāstrārthe mānileyā | mārgā anusare dhanaṅjayā | tari nyāya to nyāyā | hetu hoya || Jñāne.18.367 || Jaisā parjanyodakāchā loṭa | vipāye dharī sāḷīṅchā pāṭa | to jire pari achāṭa | upayoga āthī || Jñāne.18.368 || Kā roṣhe nighāle avachaṭe | paḍile dwārakechiye vāṭe | te shiṇe pari sunāṭe | na vachatī pade || Jñāne.18.369 || Taise hetukāraṇameḷe | uṭhī karma je āṅdhaḷe | te shāstrāche lāhe ḍoḷe | tai nyāyya mhaṇipe || Jñāne.18.370 || [Viparītaṁ vā] Dūdha vāḍhatā ṭhāvo na pave | tava utoni ĵāya swabhāve | tohī veṅcha pari navhe | veṅchile te || Jñāne.18.371 || Taise shāstrasāhyeṁvīṇa | kele nohe ĵarī akāraṇa | tari lāgo kā nāgavaṇa | dānalekhī || Jñāne.18.372 || Agā bāvanā varṇāṁparatā | koṇa maṅtra āhe Paṅḍusutā | kā bāvanahī nuchchāritā | jīva āthī || Jñāne.18.373 || Pari maṅtrāchī kaḍasaṇī | jaṅva neṇije kodaṅḍapāṇī | tava uchchāraphaḷa vāṇī | na pave jevī || Jñāne.18.374 || Tevī kāraṇahetuyoge | je bisāṭa karma nige | te shāstrāchiye na lage | kāṅse ĵava || Jñāne.18.375 || Karma hotachi ase tevhāṁhī | pari te hoṇe navhe pāhī | to anyāya gā anyāyī | hetu hoya || Jñāne.18.376 ||

Tatraivaṁ sati kartāramātmānaṁ(ṅ) kevalaṁ(n) tu yaḥ | pashyatyakrutabuddhitwānna sa pashyati durmatiḥ(hi) || Bha.Gī.18.16 ||

[Pañchaite iti pūrvashlokasthaṁ padaṁ] Eva paṅchakāraṇā karmā | pāṅchahī hetu he sumahimā | [tatraivamiti] ātā ethe pāhe pā ātmā | sāṁpaḍalā ase || Jñāne.18.377 || Bhānu na honi rūpe jaisī | chakṣhu rūpāte kā praKāshī | ātmā na honi karme taisī | prakaṭita ase gā || Jñāne.18.378 || Pai pratibiṁba ārisā | donhī na honi vīreshā | dohīṅte praKāshī jaisā | nyāhāḷitā to || Jñāne.18.379 || Kā ahorātra savitā | na honi karī Paṅḍusutā | taisā ātmā karma kartā | na honi dāvī || Jñāne.18.380 || [Pashyatyakrutabuddhitwāt] Pari dehāhaṁmānabhulī | jayāchī buddhī dehīṅcha ātalī | tayā ātmaviṣhayī jālī | madhyarātrī gā || Jñāne.18.381 || Jeṇe chaitanyā īshwarā Brahmā | dehachi kele paramasīmā | tayā ātmā kartā he pramā | alāṭa upaĵe || Jñāne.18.382 || Ātmāchi karmakartā | hāhī nishchaya nāhī tattwatā | dehachi mī karmakartā | mānito sācha || Jñāne.18.383 || Je ātmā mī karmātīta | sarvakarmasākṣhibhūta | he āpulī kaṁhī māta | nāyakechi kānī || Jñāne.18.384 || [Na sa pashyati durmatiḥ(hi)] Mhaṇauni umapā ātmayāte | dehachivarī mavije ethe | vichitra kāī rātri divasāṅte | ḍuḍuḷa na karī || Jñāne.18.385 || Pai jeṇe āKāshīṅchā kaṁhī | satya sūrya dekhilā nāhī | to thillarīṅche biṅba kāī | mānū na lāhe || Jñāne.18.386 || Thillarācheni ĵālepaṇe | sūryāsi āṇī hoṇe | tyāchyā nāshī nāshaṇe | kaṅpe kaṁpa || Jñāne.18.387 || Āṇi nidristā chevo na ye | tava swapna sācha ho lāhe | rajju neṇatā sarpā bihe | vismo kavaṇa || Jñāne.18.388 || Jaṅva kavaḷa āthi ḍoḷā | tava chaṅdra dekhāvā kī piṁvaḷā | kāya mrugīṁhī mrugajaḷā | bhāḷāve nāhī || Jñāne.18.389 || Taisā shāstragurūcheni nāve | ĵo vārāhī ṭeko nedī sive | kevaḷa mauḍhyāchenīchi jīve | jiyālā ĵo || Jñāne.18.390 || Teṇe dehātmadruṣhṭīmuḷe | ātmayā ghāpe dehāche jāḷe | jaisā abhrāchā vega kolhe | chaṅdrī mānī || Jñāne.18.391 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Maga tayā mānaṇayāsāṭhī | dehabaṅdīshāḷe kirīṭī | karmāchyā vajragāṅṭhī | kaḷāse to || Jñāne.18.392 || Pāhe pā baṅdhabhāvanā druḍhā | naḷiyevarī to bāpuḍā | kāya mokaḷeyāhī chavaḍā | na ṭhakechi puṁsā || Jñāne.18.393 || Mhaṇoni nirmaḷe ātmaswarūpī | ĵo prakrutīche kele āropī | to kalpakoḍīchyā māpī | mavīchi karme || Jñāne.18.394 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā karmāmājī ase | pari tayāte karma na sparshe | vaḍavānaḷāte jaise | samudrodaka || Jñāne.18.395 || Taiseni vegaḷepaṇe | jayāche karmī asaṇe | to kīra voḷakhāvā kavaṇe | tarī sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.396 || Je muktāte nirdhāritā | lābhe āpalīcha muktatā | jaisī dīpe dise pāhatā | āpalī vastu || Jñāne.18.397 || Nā tarī darpaṇa ĵava uṭije | tava āpaṇapayā āpaṇa bheṭije | kā toya pāvatā toya hoije | lavaṇe jevī || Jñāne.18.398 || He aso paratoni māgute | pratibiṁba pāhe biṁbāte | tava pāhaṇe jāūni āyite | biṁbachi hoya || Jñāne.18.399 || Taise hārapale āpaṇape pāve | tai saṅtāṅte pāhātā giṁvasāve | mhaṇoni vānāve aikāve | techi sadā || Jñāne.18.400 || Pari karmī asoni karme | ĵo nāgave samaviṣhame | charmachakṣhūcheni chāme | druṣhṭī jaisī || Jñāne.18.401 || Taisā soḍavalā ĵo āhe | tayāche rūpa ātā pāhe | upapattīchī bāhe | ubhaūni sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.402 ||

Yasya nāhaṅgkruto bhāvo buddhiryasya na lipyate | hatwāpi sa imāँllokānna hanti na nibadhyate || Bha.Gī.18.17 ||

[Yasya nāhaṅgkruto bhāvaḥ] Tari avidyechiyā nidā | vishwaswapnāchā hā dhāṅdā | bhogita hotā prabuddhā | anādi ĵo || Jñāne.18.403 || To mahāvākyācheni nāve | gurukrupecheni thāṁve | māthā hāta ṭhevaṇe navhe | thāpaṭilā jaisā || Jñāne.18.404 || Taisā vishwaswapneṁsī māyā | nīda sāṅḍūni dhanaṅjayā | sahaĵeṅchi cheilā adwayā- | naṅdapaṇe ĵo || Jñāne.18.405 || [Dwitīyādhyāyoktamātmatattwasāṅgkhyamāha] Tevhā mrugajaḷāche pūra | disate eka niraṅtara | hārapatī kā chaṅdrakara | phāṅkatā jaise || Jñāne.18.406 || Kā bāḷatwa nighoni ĵāya | tai bāgulā nāhī trāya | pai jaḷāliyā iṅdhana na hoya | raṅdhana jevī || Jñāne.18.407 || Nā nā chevo āliyā pāṭhī | tai swapna na dise diṭhī | taisī ahaṅmamatā gā kirīṭī | nurechi tayā || Jñāne.18.408 || [Adhiṣhṭhānamiti shloke yāni pañcha karmakāraṇānyuktāni teṣhu nāhaṁ(ṅ)krutabuddhitwamiti vaktumadhiṣhṭhānamiti shlokaṁ punarvyāchaṣhṭe-] Maga sūrya aṅdhārālāgī | righo kā bhalate suraṅgī | pari to tayāchyā bhāgī | nāhīṅchi jaisā || Jñāne.18.409 || Taisā ātmatwe veṣhṭilā hoye | to jayā tayā drushyāte pāhe | te drushya draṣhṭepaṇeṁsī hota jāye | tayāchechi rūpa || Jñāne.18.410 || Jaisā vahni jayā lāge | te vahnīchi jāliyā āṅge | dāhyadāhakavibhāge | sāṅḍije te || Jñāne.18.411 || Taisā karmākārā dujeyā | to kartepaṇāchā ātmayā | āḷa ālā to geliyā | kāhī bāhī je ure || Jñāne.18.412 || Tiye ātmasthitīchā ĵo rāvo | maga to dehī iye ĵāṇela ṭhāvo | kāya pralayāṁbūchā unnāho | vogha mānī || Jñāne.18.413 || Taisī te pūrṇa ahaṅtā | kāī dehapaṇe Paṅḍusutā | āvare kāī savitā | biṅbe dharilā || Jñāne.18.414 || Pai mathūni loṇī ghepe | te māgutī tākī ghāpe | tari te liptapaṇe liṁpe | teṇeṅsī kāī || Jñāne.18.415 || Nā nā kāṣhṭhauni vīreshā | vegaḷāviliyā hutāshā | rāhe kāṣhṭhāchiyā māṅdusā | koṅḍalepaṇe || Jñāne.18.416 || Kā rātrīchiyā udarāṅta | rigālā ĵo hā bhāswata | to rātrīaisī māta | aike kāī || Jñāne.18.417 || Taise vedyavedakapaṇeṁsī | paḍile kā jayāchyā grasī | tayā deha mī aisī | ahaṅtā kaiṅchī || Jñāne.18.418 || Āṇi ākāshe jethe jethunī | jāije tetha ase bharonī | mhaṇoni ṭhele koṅdonī | āpeṁāpa || Jñāne.18.419 || Taise je teṇe karāve | to techi āhe swabhāve | mā koṇe karmī veṣhṭāve | kartepaṇe || Jñāne.18.420 || Nurechi gaganāvīṇa ṭhāvo | nohechi samudrā pravāho | nuṭhīchi dhruvā jāvo | taise ĵāhāle || Jñāne.18.421 || Aiseni ahaṅkrutibhāvo | jayāĉhā bodhī jāhālā vāvo | tarhī dehā jaṅva nirvāho | tava āthī karme || Jñāne.18.422 || Vārā ĵarī vāĵoni vosare | tarī to ḍola rukhī ure | kā seṅde druti rāhe kāpure | veṅchalenī || Jñāne.18.423 || Kā saraleyā Gītāchā samāraṁbhu | na vache vāhavaleyāĉhā kṣhobhu | bhūmī loḷoni geliyā aṁbu | vola thāre || Jñāne.18.424 || Agā māvaḷaleni arke | saṅdhyechiye bhūmike | jyotidīptī kautuke | dise jaisī || Jñāne.18.425 || Pai lakṣha bhediliyāhīvarī | bāṇa dhāṅvechi tavavarī | ĵava bharalī āthī urī | baḷāchī tayā || Jñāne.18.426 || Nā nā chakrī bhāṅḍe ĵāle | te kulāle parate nele | pari bhramechi te māgile | bhovaṅḍilepaṇe || Jñāne.18.427 || Taisā dehābhimāna geliyā | deha jeṇe swabhāve dhanaṅjayā | ĵāle te apaisayā | cheṣhṭavīcha te || Jñāne.18.428 || Saṅkalpeṁvīṇa swapna | na lāvitā dāṅgīche bana | na rachitā gaṅdharvabhuvana | uṭhī jaise || Jñāne.18.429 || Ātmayācheni udyameṁvīṇa | taise dehādipaṅchakāraṇa | hoya āpaṇayā āpaṇa | kriyājāta || Jñāne.18.430 || Pai prāchīnasaṁskārasheṣhe | pāṅchahī kāraṇe sahetuke | kāmavījatī gā aneke | karmākāre || Jñāne.18.431 || [Hatwā’pi sa imāँllokān] Tayā karmāmājī maga | saṁharo āghave jaga | athavā nave chāṅga | anukaro || Jñāne.18.432 || Pari kumuda kaiseni suke | te kamaḷa kaise phāṅke | hī donhī ravī na dekhe | jayāparī || Jñāne.18.433 || Kā viju varṣhoni ābhāḷa | ṭhikariyā āto bhūtaḷa | athavā karū shāḍaḷa | parjanyavruṣhṭī || Jñāne.18.434 || Tari tayā dohīṅte jaise | neṇijechi kā ākāshe | taisā dehīṅcha ĵo ase | videhadruṣhṭī || Jñāne.18.435 || To dehādikī cheṣhṭī | ghaḍatā moḍatā he sruṣhṭī | na dekhe swapna druṣhṭī | cheilā jaisā || Jñāne.18.436 || Yerhavī chāmāche ḍoḷevarī | je dekhatī dehachivarī | te kīra to vyāpārī | aiseṅchi mānitī || Jñāne.18.437 || Kā truṇāchā bāhulā | ĵo āgarāmere ṭhevilā | to satya rākhatā kolhā | na manī kāī || Jñāne.18.438 || | pise nesale kā nāgave | he lokī yeūni ĵāṇāve | ṭhāṇoriyāṅche mavāve | āṇikī ghāya || Jñāne.18.439 || Kā mahāsatīche bhoga | dekhe kīra sakaḷa jaga | pari te āgī nā āṅga | nā loka dekhe || Jñāne.18.440 || Taisā swaswarūpe uṭhilā | ĵo drushyeṅsī draṣhṭā āṭalā | to neṇe kāya rāhaṭalā | iṅdriyagrama || Jñāne.18.441 || Agā thorī kalloḷī kalloḷa sāne | lopatā tirīṅcheni jane | ekā ekī giḷile he mane | mānije jarhī || Jñāne.18.442 || Tarhī udakāprati pāhī | koṇa grasītase kāī | taise pūrṇā duje nāhī | je to mārī || Jñāne.18.443 || Suvarṇāchiyā chaṅḍikā | suvarṇashūḷeṅchi dekhā | suvarṇāchiyā mahikhā | nāsha kelā || Jñāne.18.444 || To devalavasiyā kaḍā | vyavahāra gamalā phuḍā | vāṅchūni mahiṣha shūḷa chāmuṅḍā | suvarṇachi te || Jñāne.18.445 || Pai chitrīṅche jaḷa hutāsha | to druṣhṭīchāchi ābhāsa | paṭī āgna volāṁsha | donhī nāhī || Jñāne.18.446 || Muktāche deha taise | hāle chāle saṁskāravashe | te dekhoni loka pise | to kartā mhaṇatī || Jñāne.18.447 || [Na hanti] Āṇi tayā karaṇeyāṁāṅta | ghaḍo trailokyā ghāta | pari teṇe kelā he māta | bolo na ye || Jñāne.18.448 || Agā aṅdhakāra dekhāvā teje | maga to pheḍije he ke bolije | taise jñāniyā nāhī duje | to mārīla kāī || Jñāne.18.449 || [Buddhiryasya na lipyate] Mhaṇoni tayāchī buddhī | neṇe pāpapuṇyāchī gaṅdhī | Gaṅgā mīnaliyā nadī | viṭāḷa jaisā || Jñāne.18.450 || Agnīsī agni jhagaṭaliyā | kāya poḷe to dhanaṅjayā | kī shastra rupe āpaṇayā | āpaṇachi || Jñāne.18.451 || Taise āpaṇapayāparate | ĵo neṇe kriyājātāte | tetha kāya liṁpavī buddhīte | tayāchiye || Jñāne.18.452 || [Na nibaddhyate] Mhaṇoni kārya kartā kriyā | he swarūpachi ĵāhāle jayā | nāhī sharīrādikī tayā | karmabaṅdha || Jñāne.18.453 || Je kartā jīva viṅdāṇī | kāḍhūni pāṅchahī khāṇī | ghaḍita āhe karaṇī | āutī dāhe || Jñāne.18.454 || Tetha nyāvo āṇi anyāvo | hā dwividha sādhūni āvo | ubhāritā na lavī kheṁvo | karma bhuvane || Jñāne.18.455 || Yā thorāḍā kīra kāmā | virajā nohe ātmā | pari mhaṇasī hana upakramā | hāta lāvī || Jñāne.18.456 || To sākṣhī chidrūpa | karmapravruttīchā saṅkalpa | uṭhī to kā niropa | āpaṇachi de || Jñāne.18.457 || Tarī karmapravruttīhī lāgī | tayā āyāsa nāhī āṅgī | je pravruttīchehī uḷigī | lokachi āthī || Jñāne.18.458 || Mhaṇoni ātmayāche kevaḷa | ĵo rūpachi jāhālā nikhiḷa | tayā nāhī baṅdishāḷa | karmāchī he || Jñāne.18.459 || Pari ajñānāchyā paṭī | anyathā jñānāche chitra uṭhī | tetha chitāraṇī he tripuṭī | prasiddha je kā || Jñāne.18.460 ||

Jñānaṁ(ñ) jñeyaṁ parijñātā trividhā karmachodanā | karaṇaṁ(ṅ) karma karteti trividhaḥ(kh) karmasaṅggrahaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.18 ||

[Parijñātā] Je jñāna jñātā jñeya | he jagāche bījatraya | te karmāchī niḥsaṅdeha | pravruttī ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.461 || Ātā yayāchi gā trayā | vyaktī vegaḷāliyā | āike dhanaṅjayā | karū rūpa || Jñāne.18.462 || Tari jīvasūryabiṁbāche | rashmī shrotrādike pāṅche | dhāṁvoni viṣhayapadmāche | phoḍīta maḍha || Jñāne.18.463 || Kī jīvanrupāche vāru upalāṇe | gheūni iṅdriyāṅchī keṅkāṇe | viṣhayadeshīṅche nāgavaṇe | āṇīta je || Jñāne.18.464 || He aso iṁhī iṅdriyī rāhaṭe | je sukhaduḥkheṅsī jīvā bheṭe | te suṣhuptikāḷī vohaṭe | jetha jñāna || Jñāne.18.465 || Tayā jīvā nāṅva jñātā | āṇi je he sāṅgītale ātā | techi etha Paṅḍusutā | jñāna ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.466 || Je avidyechiye poṭī | upaĵatakheṅvo kirīṭī | āpaṇayāte vāṅṭī | tihī ṭhāyī || Jñāne.18.467 || Āpuliye dhāṁvepuḍhā | ghālūni jñeyāĉhā guṅḍā | ubhārī māgilī kaḍā | jñātrutwāte || Jñāne.18.468 || [Jñānaṁ] Maga jñātayā jñeyā doghā | to nāṅdaṇukechā bagā | māji ĵāleni pai gā | vāhe jeṇe || Jñāne.18.469 || Ṭākūni jñeyāchī shiṁva | pure jayāchī dhāva | sakaḷa padārthā nāṁva | sūtase je || Jñāne.18.470 || Te gā sāmānya jñāna | yā bolā nāhī āna | [jñeyaṁ] jñeyācheṅhī chinha | āīka ātā || Jñāne.18.471 || Tari shabda sparsha | rūpa gaṅdha rasa | hā paṅchavidha ābhāsa | jñeyāĉhā to || Jñāne.18.472 || Jaise ekechi chūtaphaḷe | iṅdriyā vegaḷavegaḷe | rase varṇe parimaḷe | bheṭije sparshe || Jñāne.18.473 || Taise jñeya tarī ekasare | pari jñāna iṅdriyadwāre | ghe mhaṇoni prakāre | pāṅche ĵāle || Jñāne.18.474 || Āṇi samudrī voghāche ĵāṇe | sare lāṇīpāsī dhāvaṇe | kā phaḷī sare vāḍhaṇe | sasyāche jevī || Jñāne.18.475 || Taise iṅdriyāṅchyā vāhavaṭī | dhāṅvatayā jñānā jetha ṭhī | hoya te gā kirīṭī | viṣhaya jñeya || Jñāne.18.476 || Eva jñātayā jñāna jñeyā | tihī rūpa kele dhanaṅjayā | [trividhā karmachodanā] he trividha sarva kriyā- | pravrutti ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.477 || Je shabdādi viṣhaya | he paṅchavidha je jñeya | techi priya kā apriya | eke parīche || Jñāne.18.478 || Jñāna moṭake jñātayā | dāvī nā jaṅva dhanaṅjayā | tava swīkārā kī tyajāvayā | pravartechi to || Jñāne.18.479 || Pari mīnāte dekhoni baka | jaisā nidhānāte raṅka | kā strī dekhoni kāmuka | pravrutti dharī || Jñāne.18.480 || Jaise khālārā dhāṁve pāṇī | bhramara puṣhpāchiye ghāṇī | nā nā suṭalā sāṅjavaṇī | vatsachi pā || Jñāne.18.481 || Agā swargīṅchī urvashī | aikoni jevi māṇusī | varātā lāvījatī āKāshī | yāgāṅchiyā || Jñāne.18.482 || Pai pārivā jaisā kirīṭī | chaḍhalā nabhāchiye poṭī | pāravī dekhoni loṭī | āṅgachi sagaḷe || Jñāne.18.483 || He nā ghanagarjanesarisā | mayūra vovāṅḍe ākāshā | jñātā jñeyā dekhoni taisā | dhāṅvachi ghe || Jñāne.18.484 || Mhaṇoni jñāna jñeya jñātā | he trividha gā Paṅḍusutā | hoyachi karmā samastā | pravrutti yetha || Jñāne.18.485 || [Kartā] Pari techi jñeya vipāye | ĵarī jñātayāte priya hoye | tarī bhogāvayā na sāhe | kṣhaṇahī vilaṁba || Jñāne.18.486 || Nā tarī avachaṭe | techi viruddha hoūni bheṭe | tarī yugāṅta vāṭe | sāṅḍāvayā || Jñāne.18.487 || Vyāḷā kā hārā | varapaḍā ĵāleyā narā | harṣha āṇi darārā | sarasāchi uṭhī || Jñāne.18.488 || Taise jñeya priyāpriye | dekhileni jñātayā hoye | maga tyāga swīkārī vāhe | vyāpārāte || Jñāne.18.489 || Tetha rāgī pratimallāchā | gosāṁvī sarvadaḷāchā | ratha sāṅḍūni pāyāṅchā | hoya jaisā || Jñāne.18.490 || Taise jñātepaṇe je ase | te ye kartā aisiye dashe | jevite baisale jaise | raṅdhana karū || Jñāne.18.491 || Kā bhaṅvareṅchi kelā maḷā | varakala jālā aṅkasaḷā | nā nā deva rigālā deuḷā- | chiyā kāmā || Jñāne.18.492 || Taisā jñeyāchiyā hāṁvā | jñātā iṅdriyāṅchā meḷāvā | rāhāṭavī tetha Pāṅḍavā | kartā hoya || Jñāne.18.493 || Āṇi āpaṇa hoūnī kartā | jñānā āṇi karaṇatā | tethe jñeyachi swabhāvatā | kārya hoya || Jñāne.18.494 || Aisā jñānāchiye nijagatī | pālaṭa paḍe gā sumatī | netrāṅchī shobhā rātī | pālaṭe jaisī || Jñāne.18.495 || Kā adruṣhṭa jāliyā udāsu | pālaṭe Shreemaṅtāṅchā vilāsu | pūrṇimepāṭhī shītāṁshu | pālaṭe jasā || Jñāne.18.496 || Taisā chāḷitā karaṇe | jñātā veṣhṭije kartepaṇe | tethiṅchī tiye lakṣhaṇe | aika ātā || Jñāne.18.497 || Tari buddhi āṇi mana | chitta ahaṅkāra hana | he chaturvidha chinha | aṅtaḥkaraṇāche || Jñāne.18.498 || Bāhya twachā shravaṇa | chakṣhu rasanā ghrāṇa | he paṅchavidha ĵāṇa | iṅdriya gā || Jñāne.18.499 || Tetha āṅtule tava karaṇe | kartā kartavyā ghe umāṇe | maga tai ĵarī ĵāṇe | sukhā yete || Jñāne.18.500 || Tari bāherile tiyeṁhī | chakṣhurādike dāhāhī | uṭhauni lavalāhī | vyāpārā suye || Jñāne.18.501 || Maga to iṅdriyakadaṁba | karavije tava rāba | jaṅva kartavyāĉhā lābha | hātāsi ye || Jñāne.18.502 || Nā te kartavya ĵarī duḥkhe | phaḷela aise dekhe | to lāvī tyāgamukhe | tiye dāhāhī || Jñāne.18.503 || Maga phiṭe duḥkhāchā ṭhāvo | tava rāhāṭavī rātridivo | vikaṇa vāte vāhāvo | jayāparī || Jñāne.18.504 || Taiseni tyāga swīkārī | vāhātā iṅdriyāṅchī dhurī | jñātayāte avadhārī | kartā mhaṇipe || Jñāne.18.505 || [Karaṇaṁ] Āṇi kartayāchyā sarva karmī | āutāṅchiyā pari kṣhamī | mhaṇoni iṅdriyāte āmhī | karaṇe mhaṇo || Jñāne.18.506 || [Karma] Āṇi hechi karaṇeṁvarī | kartā kriyā jyā ubhārī | tiyā vyāpe te avadhārī | karma etha || Jñāne.18.507 || Sonārāchiyā buddhī leṇe | vyāpe chaṅdrakarī chāṅdiṇe | kā vyāpe velhāḷapaṇe | velī jaisī || Jñāne.18.508 || Nā nā prabhā vyāpe prakāshu | goḍiyā ikṣhurasu | he aso avakāshu | āKāshī jaisā || Jñāne.18.509 || Taise kartavyāchiyā kriyā | vyāpale je dhanaṅjayā | te karma gā bolāvayā | āna nāhī || Jñāne.18.510 || [Iti] Eva karma kartā karaṇa | yā tihīṅcheṁhī lakṣhaṇa | sāṅgītale tuĵa vichakṣhaṇa | shiromaṇī || Jñāne.18.511 || [Trividhaḥ(kh) karmasaṅggrahaḥ] Etha jñātā jñāna jñeya | he karmāche pravruttitraya | taiseṅchi kartā karaṇa kārya | hā karmasaṅchaya || Jñāne.18.512 || Vanhī ṭhevilā ase dhūma | āthī bījī jevi druma | kā manī ĵoḍe kāma | sadā jaisā || Jñāne.18.513 || Taisā kartā kriyākaraṇī | karmāche āhe jiṅtavaṇī | sone jaise khāṇī | suvarṇāchiye || Jñāne.18.514 || Mhaṇoni he kārya mī kartā | aise āthi jetha Paṅḍusutā | tetha ātmā dūrī samastā | kriyāpāsī || Jñāne.18.515 || Yālāgī puḍhatapuḍhatī | ātmā vegaḷāchi sumatī | ātā aso he kitī | ĵāṇatāsi tū || Jñāne.18.516 ||

Jñānaṁ(ṅ) karma cha kartā cha tridhaiva guṇabhedataḥ | prochyate guṇasaṅgkhyāne yathāvachchhruṇu tānyapi || Bha.Gī.18.19 ||

[Jñānamiti] Parī sāṅgītale je jñāna | karma kartā hana | te tinhī tinhī ṭhāyī bhinna | guṇī āhātī || Jñāne.18.517 || Mhaṇoni jñānā karmā kartayā | pāteĵo naye dhanaṅjayā | je donī bāṅdhatī soḍāvayā | ekachi prauḍhe || Jñāne.18.518 || [Prochyate guṇasaṅgkhyāne] Te sāttwika ṭhāuve hoye | to guṇabheda sāṅgo pāhe | ĵo sāṅkhyashāstrī āhe | uvāilā || Jñāne.18.519 || Je vichārakṣhīrasamudra | swabodhakumudinīchaṅdra | jñānaḍoḷasā nareṅdra | shāstrāṅchā je || Jñāne.18.520 || Kī prakrutipuruṣha donī | misaḷalī divorajanī | tiye nivaḍitā tribhuvanī | mārtaṅḍa je || Jñāne.18.521 || Jetha apārā moharāshī | tattwāchyā māpī chovisī | umāṇe gheūni pareshī | suravāḍije || Jñāne.18.522 || Arjunā te sāṅkhyashāstra | paḍhe jayāche stotra | [yathāvachchhruṇu tānyapi] te guṇabhedacharitra | aise āhe || Jñāne.18.523 || Je āpuleni āṅgike | trividhapaṇācheni aṅke | drushyajāta titake | aṅkita kele || Jñāne.18.524 || Eva sattwarajatamā | tihīṅchī evaḍhī ase mahimā | je traividhya ādi Brahmā | aṅtī krumi || Jñāne.18.525 || Pari vishwīṅchī āghavī māṅdī | jeṇe bhedaleni guṇabhedī | paḍilī te tava ādī | jñāna sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.526 || Je diṭhī ĵarī chokha kīje | tarī bhalateṅhī chokha suje | taise jñāne shuddhe lāhije | sarvahī shuddha || Jñāne.18.527 || Mhaṇoni te sāttwika jñāna | ātā sāṅgo de avadhāna | kaivalyaguṇanidhāna | ShreeKriṣhṇa mhaṇe || Jñāne.18.528 ||

Sarvabhūteṣhu yenaikaṁ bhāvamavyayamīkṣhate | avibhaktaṁ vibhakteṣhu tajjñānaṁ viddhi sāttwikam || Bha.Gī.18.20 ||

[Sarvabhūteṣhu yenaikaṁ] Tarī Arjunā gā te phuḍe | sāttwika jñāna ĉhokhaḍe | jayāchyā udayī jñeya buḍe | jñātenisī || Jñāne.18.529 || Jaisā sūrya na dekhe āṅdhāre | saritā neṇijatī sāgare | kā kavaḷiliyā na dhare | ātmachchhāyā || Jñāne.18.530 || Tayāparī jayā jñānā | shivādi truṇāvasānā | iyā bhūtavyakti bhinnā | nāḍaḷatī || Jñāne.18.531 || [Bhāvamavyayamīkṣhate] Jaise hāte chitra pāhātā | hoya pāṇiye mīṭha dhutā | kā chevoni swapnā yetā | jaise hoya || Jñāne.18.532 || Taise jñāne jeṇe | karitā jñātavyāte pāhāṇe | ĵāṇatā nā ĵāṇaṇe | ĵāṇāve ure || Jñāne.18.533 || [Avibhaktaṁ vibhakteṣhu] Pai sone āṭūni leṇī | na kāḍhitī āpuliyā āyaṇī | kā taraṅga na ghepatī pāṇī | gāḷūni jaise || Jñāne.18.534 || Taisī jayā jñānāchiyā hātā | nalagechi drushyakathā | [tajjñānaṁ viddhi sāttwikam] te jñāna ĵāṇa sarvathā | sāttwika gā || Jñāne.18.535 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Ārisā pāho jātā koḍe | jaise pāhātechi kā rige puḍhe | taise jñeya loṭoni paḍe | jñātāchi je || Jñāne.18.536 || Puḍhatī techi sāttwika jñāna | je mokṣhalakṣhmīche bhuvana | he aso aika chinha | rājasāche || Jñāne.18.537 ||

Pruthaktwena tu yajjñānaṁ(n) nānābhāvānpruthagvidhān | vetti sarveṣhu bhūteṣhu tajjñānaṁ viddhi rājasam || Bha.Gī.18.21 ||

[Pruthaktwena tu yajjñānaṁ] Tari Pārthā pariyesa | te jñāna gā rājasa | je bhedāchī kāṁsa | dharūni chāle || Jñāne.18.538 || [Nānābhāvānpruthagvidhān] Vichitratā bhūtāṅchiyā | āpaṇa ātoni ṭhikariyā | bahu chakai jñātayā | āṇilī jeṇe || Jñāne.18.539 || Jaise sāchā rūpā āḍa | ghālūni visarāche kavāḍa | maga swapnāche kābāḍa | voirī nidrā || Jñāne.18.540 || Taise swajñānāchiye pauḷī- | bāheri mithyāmohāche khaḷī | tihī avasthāṅchī vahyāḷī | dāvī je jīvā || Jñāne.18.541 || Aḷaṅkārapaṇe jhāṅkale | bāḷakā sone kā vāyā gele | taise nāmī rūpī durāvale | adwaita jayā || Jñāne.18.542 || Avataralī gāḍagyā ghaḍā | pruthvī anoḷakha jālī mūḍhā | vahni jālā kānaḍā | dīpatwāsāṭhī || Jñāne.18.543 || Kā vastrapaṇācheni ārope | mūrkhāprati taṅtu hārape | nānā mugdhā paṭa lope | dāūni chitra || Jñāne.18.544 || Taisī jayā jñānā | [vetti sarveṣhu bhūteṣhu] ĵāṇoni bhūtavyaktī bhinnā | aikyabodhāchī bhāvanā | nimoni gelī || Jñāne.18.545 || Maga iṅdhanī bhedalā anaḷa | phulāvarī parimaḷa | kā jaḷabhede sakaḷa | chaṅdra jaisā || Jñāne.18.546 || Taise padārthabheda bahuvasa | ĵāṇoni lahāna thora veṣha | [tajjñānaṁ viddhi rājasam] ātale te rājasa | jñāna yetha || Jñāne.18.547 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā tāmasācheṁhī liṅga | sāṅgena te voḷakha chāṅga | ḍāvalāvayā mātaṅga- | sadana taise || Jñāne.18.548 ||

Yattu krutsnavadekasminkārye saktamahaitukam | atattwārthavadalpaṁ(ñ) cha tattāmasamudāhrutam || Bha.Gī.18.22 ||

[Yattu] Tari kirīṭī je jñāna | hiṅḍe vidhīcheni vastre hīna | shruti pāṭhamorī nagna | mhaṇoni tayā || Jñāne.18.549 || Yerīhī shāstrabāhyakārī | je niṅdeche viṭāḷavarī | boḷavileṅse ḍoṅgarī | mleṅchchhadharmāchyā || Jñāne.18.550 || Je gā jñāna aise | guṇagrahe tāmase | ghetale bhoṁve pise | hoūniyā || Jñāne.18.551 || Je soyarike bādha neṇe | padārthī niṣhedha na mhaṇe | niropile jaise suṇe | shūnyagramī || Jñāne.18.552 || Tayā toṅḍī je nāḍaḷe | kā khātā jeṇe poḷe | techi yeka vāḷe | yera ghechi te || Jñāne.18.553 || Pai sone choritā uṅdira | na mhaṇe tharavithara | neṇe māṁsakhāira | kāḷe gore || Jñāne.18.554 || Nā nā vanāmājī boharī | kaḍasaṇī jevi na karī | kā jīta mele na vichārī | baisatā māsī || Jñāne.18.555 || Agā vāṅtā kā vāḍhiyelā | sājuka kā saḍaliyā | viveka kāvaḷiyā | nāhī jaisā || Jñāne.18.556 || Taise niṣhiddha sāṅḍūni dyāve | kā vihita ādare ghyāve | he viṣhayāṅcheni nāve | neṇechi je || Jñāne.18.557 || Jetule āḍa paḍe diṭhī | tetule ghechi viṣhayāsāṭhī | maga te strīdravya vāṅṭī | shishnodarā || Jñāne.18.558 || Tīrthātīrtha he bhākha | udakī nāhī sanoḷakha | truṣhā voḷe techi sukha | vāṅchūniyā || Jñāne.18.559 || Tayāchiparī khādyākhādya | na mhaṇe niṅdyāniṅdya | toṅḍā āvaḍe te medhya | aisāchi bodha || Jñāne.18.560 || Āṇi strījāta tituke | twacheṅdriyeṅchi voḷakhe | tiyeviṣhayī soyarike | sādarachi bahu || Jñāne.18.561 || Pai swārthī je upakare | tayāchi nāma soyire | dehasaṅbaṅdha na sare | jiye jñānī || Jñāne.18.562 || Mrutyūche āghaveṅchi anna | āgī āghaveṅchi iṅdhana | taise jagachi āpale dhana | tāmasajñānā || Jñāne.18.563 || [Krutsnavadekasmin] Aiseni vishwa sakaḷa | jeṇe viṣhayachi mānile kevaḷa | tayā eka ĵāṇa phaḷa | dehabharaṇa || Jñāne.18.564 || Ākāsha-patitā nīrā | jaisā siṅdhuchi eka thārā | taise krutyajāta udarā- | lāgīṅchi bujhe || Jñāne.18.565 || [Ahaitukaṁ] Vāṅchūni swarga naraka āthī | tayā hetu pravrutti nivruttī | iye āghavīyechi rātī | jāṇivechī je || Jñāne.18.566 || [Kārye saktaṁ] Je dehakhaṅḍā nāma ātmā | īshwara pāṣhāṇapratimā | yayāparautī pramā | ḍhaḷo neṇe || Jñāne.18.567 || [Atattwārthavat] Mhaṇe paḍileni sharīre | kelenisī ātmā sare | mā bhogāvayā ure | koṇa veṣhe || Jñāne.18.568 || Nā īshwara pāhātā āhe | to bhogavī ĵarī he hoye | tarī devachi khāye | vikūniyā || Jñāne.18.569 || Gāṅvīṅche devaḷeshwara | niyāmakachi hotī sāchāra | tari deshīṅche ḍoṅgara | uge kā asatī || Jñāne.18.570 || [Alpaṁ(ñ) cha] Aisā vipāye deva mānije | tari pāṣhāṇamātrachi jāṇije | āṇi ātmā tava mhaṇije | dehātechi || Jñāne.18.571 || Yere pāpapuṇyādike | te aghaveṅchi karoni laṭike | hita mānī agnimukhe | charaṇe je kā || Jñāne.18.572 || Je charmachakṣhu dāvitī | je iṅdriye goḍī lāvitī | techi sācha he pratītī | phuḍī jayā || Jñāne.18.573 || [Tattāmasaṁ] Kiṁbahunā aisī prathā | vāḍhatī dekhasī Pārthā | dhūmāchī velī vruthā | āKāshī jaisī || Jñāne.18.574 || Koraḍā nā volā | upayogā āthī gelā | to vāḍhoni moḍalā | bheṅḍa jaisā || Jñāne.18.575 || Nā nā usāṅchī kaṇase | kā napuṁsake māṇuse | vana lāgale jaise | sābarīche || Jñāne.18.576 || Nā tarī bāḷakāche mana | kā chorāgharīṅche dhana | athavā gaḷastana | sheḷiyeche || Jñāne.18.577 || Taise je vāyāṇe | vosāḷa dise ĵāṇaṇe | tayāte mī mhaṇe | tāmasa jñāna || Jñāne.18.578 || [Udāhrutaṁ] Teṅhī jñāna iyā bhāṣhā | bolije to bhāva aisā | jātyaṅdhāchā kā jaisā | ḍoḷā vāḍa || Jñāne.18.579 || Kā badhirāche nīṭa kāna | apeyā nāma pāna | taise āḍanāṅva jñāna | tāmasā tayā || Jñāne.18.580 || He aso kitī bolāve | tari aise je dekhāve | te jñāna nohe ĵāṇāve | ḍoḷasa tama || Jñāne.18.581 || [Shlokatrayabhāvārthaḥ] Eva tihī guṇī | bhedale yathālakṣhaṇī | jñāna shroteshiromaṇī | dāvile tuĵa || Jñāne.18.582 || Ātā yāchi triprakārā | jñānācheni dhanurdharā | prakāshe hotī gocharā | kartayāṅchyā kriyā || Jñāne.18.583 || [Uttarashlokatraya-chūrṇikā] Mhaṇauni karma pai gā | anusare tihī bhāgā | mohare jāliyā voghā | toya jaise || Jñāne.18.584 || Techi jñānatrayavashe | trividha karma je ase | tetha sāttwika tava aise | parisa ādhī || Jñāne.18.585 ||

Niyataṁ saṅggarahitamarāgadweṣhataḥ(kh) krutam | aphalaprepsunā karma yattatsāttwikamuchyate || Bha.Gī.18.23 ||

[Niyataṁ] Tari swādhikārācheni mārge | āle je mānile āṅge | pativratecheni pariṣhwaṅge | priyāte jaise || Jñāne.18.586 || Sāṁvaḷyā āṅgā chaṅdana | pramadālochanā aṅjana | taise adhikārāsī maṅḍaṇa | nityapaṇe je || Jñāne.18.587 || Te nitya karma bhale | hoya naimittikī sāvāile | sonayāsī ĵoḍale | saurabhya jaise || Jñāne.18.588 || [Saṅggarahitaṁ] Āṇi āṅgā jīvāchī saṁpattī | veṅchūni karī bāḷāchī pāḷatī | pari jīve ubagaṇe he sthitī | na pāhe māya || Jñāne.18.589 || [Aphalaprepsunā karma] Taise sarvaswe karma anuṣhṭhī | pari phala na sūye diṭhī | ukhitī kriyā paiṭhī | brahmīṅchi karī || Jñāne.18.590 || [Arāgadweṣhataḥ(kh) krutaṁ] Āṇi priya āliyā swabhāve | shaṁbaḷa ure veṅche ṭhāuve navhe | taise satprasaṅge karāve | pāruṣhe ĵarī || Jñāne.18.591 || Tarī akaraṇācheni khede | dweṣhāṅte jivī na bāṅdhe | jāliyācheni ānaṅde | phuṅĵo neṇe || Jñāne.18.592 || Aisaaisiyā hātavaṭiyā | karma niphaje je dhanaṅjayā | [yattatsāttwikamuchyate] ĵāṇa sāttwika he tayā | guṇanāma gā || Jñāne.18.593 || [Chūrṇikā] Yāvarī rājasāche | lakṣhaṇa sāṅgijela sāche | na karī avadhānāche | vāṇeṁpaṇa || Jñāne.18.594 ||

Yattu kāmepsunā karma sāhaṅgkāreṇa vā punaḥ | kriyate bahulāyāsaṁ(n) tadrājasamudāhrutam || Bha.Gī.18.24 ||

[Yattu kāmepsunā] Tari gharī mātāpitarā | dhaḍa bolī nāhī saṁsārā | yera vishwa bharī ādarā | mūrkha jaisā || Jñāne.18.595 || Kā tuḷashīchiyā jhāḍā | durūni na ghāpe siṅtoḍā | drākṣhīṅcheyā tari buḍā | dūdhachi lāvije || Jñāne.18.596 || [Karma] Taisī nityanaimittike | karme jiye āvashyake | tayāṅcheviṣhī na shake | baisalā uṭhū || Jñāne.18.597 || Yerā kāmyācheni tari nāve | deha sarvaswa āghave | veṅchitāṅhī na manave | bahu aise || Jñāne.18.598 || Agā devaḍhī vāḍhī lāhije | tetha mola detā na dhāije | peritā pure na mhaṇije | bīja jevī || Jñāne.18.599 || Kā parisa jāliyā hātī | lohālāgī sarvasaṁpattī | veṅchitā ye unnatī | sādhaka jaisā || Jñāne.18.600 || Taisī phaḷe dekhoni puḍhe | kāmya karme duvāḍe | [punaḥ] karī pari te thoḍe | keleṁhī mānī || Jñāne.18.601 || Teṇe phaḷakāmuke | yathāvidhi neṭake | kāmya kīje tituke | kriyājāta || Jñāne.18.602 || [Sāhaṅgkāreṇa vā] Āṇi tayāhī keliyāche | toṅḍī lāvī dauṅḍīche | karmī yā nāmapāṭāche | vāṇe sārī || Jñāne.18.603 || Taisā bhare karmāhaṅkāru | maga pitā athavā guru | te na manī kāḷajvaru | auṣhadha jaise || Jñāne.18.604 || Taiseni sāhaṅkāre | phaḷābhilāṣhiye nare | kīje gā ādare | je je kāhī || Jñāne.18.605 || [Kriyate bahulāyāsaṁ] Pari teṅhī karaṇe bahuvasā | vaḷaghoni karī sāyāsā | jīvanopāya kā jaisā | kolhāṅṭiyāĉhā || Jñāne.18.606 || Ekā kaṇālāgī uṅdīra | avaghā upase ḍoṅgara | kā shevāḷoddeshe dardura | samudra ḍahuḷī || Jñāne.18.607 || Pai bhikeparate na lāhe | tarhī gāruḍī sāpa vāhe | kāya kīje shīṇachi hoye | goḍa yekā || Jñāne.18.608 || He aso paramāṇūcheni lobhe | pātāḷa laṅghitī voḷaṁbe | taise swargasukhalobhe | vichaṅbaṇe je || Jñāne.18.609 || [Yattadrājasamuchyate] Te kāmyakarma saklesha | ĵāṇāve yetha rājasa | [chūrṇikā] ātā chinha parisa | tāmasāche || Jñāne.18.610 ||

Anubandhaṁ(ṅ) kṣhayaṁ hiṁ(ñ)sāmanavekṣhya cha pauruṣham | mohādārabhyate karma yattattāmasamuchyate || Bha.Gī.18.25 ||

[Anubandhaṁ] Tari te gā tāmasa karma | je niṅdeche kāḷe dhāma | niṣhedhāche janma | sācha jeṇe || Jñāne.18.611 || Je nipajavilyāpāṭhī | kāhīṅcha na dise diṭhī | regha kāḍhiliyā poṭī | toyāche jevī || Jñāne.18.612 || Kā kāṅjī ghusaḷaliyā | kā rākha phuṅkiliyā | kāhī na dise gāḷiliyā | vāḷu ghāṇā || Jñāne.18.613 || Nā nā upaṇiliyā bhūṁsa | kā viṅdhiliyā ākāsha | nā nā māṅḍiliyā pāsha | vārayāsī || Jñāne.18.614 || He avaghechi jaise | vāṅjhe hoūni nāse | je keliyā pāṭhī taise | vāyāṅchi ĵāya || Jñāne.18.615 || [Kṣhayaṁ] Yerhavī naradehāhīyevaḍhe | dhana āṭaṇiye paḍe | te karma niphajavitā moḍe | jagāche sukha || Jñāne.18.616 || Jaisā kamaḷavanī phāṁsa | kāḍhiliyā kāṅṭasa | āpaṇa jhije nāsha | kamaḷā karī || Jñāne.18.617 || [Hiṁsā] Kā āpaṇa āṅge jaḷe | āṇi nāgavī jagāche ḍoḷe | pataṅga jaisā saḷe | dīpācheni || Jñāne.18.618 || Taise sarvaswa vāyā jāvo | varī swadehāhī hoya ghāvo | pari puḍhilā apāvo | niphajavije jeṇe || Jñāne.18.619 || Māshī āpaṇayāte giḷavī | pari puḍhilā vāṅtī shiṇavī | te kashmaḷa āṭhavī | ācharaṇa je || Jñāne.18.620 || [Anavekṣhya cha pauruṣhaṁ] Teṅhī karāvayā doṣhe | maĵa sāmarthya ase kī nase | heṁhī puḍhīla taise | na pāhātā karī || Jñāne.18.621 || Kevaḍhā mājhā upāvo | karitā koṇa prastāvo | keliyāhī āvo | kāya yetha || Jñāne.18.622 || [Mohādārabhyate karma] Iye jāṇivechī soye | avivekācheni pāye | pusoniyā hoye | sāṭopa karmī || Jñāne.18.623 || Āpalā vasauṭā jāḷunī | bisāṭe jaisā vahnī | kā swamaryādā giḷonī | siṅdhu uṭhī || Jñāne.18.624 || Maga neṇe bahu thoḍe | na pāhe māgee puḍhe | mārgāmārga yekavaḍhe | karīta chāle || Jñāne.18.625 || [Yattattāmasamuchyate] Taise krutyākrutya sarakaṭita | āpapara na vichārita | karma hoya te nishchita | tāmasa ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.626 || [Shlokatrayābhiprāyaḥ] Aisī guṇatrayabhinnā | karmāchī gā Arjunā | he kelī vivaṅchanā | upapattīsī || Jñāne.18.627 || Ātā iyāchi karmā bhajatā | karmābhimāniyā kartā | to jīvahī trividhatā | pātalā ase || Jñāne.18.628 || Chaturāshramavashe | eka puruṣha chaturdhā dise | kartayā traividhya taise | karmabhede || Jñāne.18.629 || Pari tayā tihīṁāṅta | sāttwika tava prastuta | sāṅgena dattachitta | ākarṇī tū || Jñāne.18.630 ||

Muktasaṅggo’nahaṁ(n)vādī dhrutyutsāhasamanvitaḥ | siddhyasiddhyornirvikāraḥ(kh) kartā sāttwika uchyate || Bha.Gī.18.26 ||

[Muktasaṅggaḥ] Tari phaḷoddeshe sāṅḍiliyā | vāḍhatī jevi saraḷiyā | shākhā kā chaṅdanāchiyā | bāvanayā || Jñāne.18.631 || Kā na phaḷatāṁhī sārthakā | jaisiyā nāgalatikā | taisiyā karī nityādikā | kriyā ĵo kā || Jñāne.18.632 || Pari phaḷashūnyatā | nāhī tayā viphaḷatā | pai phaḷāsīchi Paṅḍusutā | phaḷe kāyisī || Jñāne.18.633 || [Anahaṁvādī] Āṇi ādare karī bahuvase | pari mī kartā he numase | varṣhākāḷīṅche jaise | meghavruṅda || Jñāne.18.634 || Tevīṅchi paramātmaliṅgā | samarpāvayāĵogā | karmakalāpa pai gā | nipajāvayā || Jñāne.18.635 || Tayā kāḷāte nulaṅghaṇe | deshashuddhīhī sādhaṇe | kā shāstrāṅchyā vātī pāhaṇe | kriyānirṇaya || Jñāne.18.636 || [Dhrutyutsāhasamanvitaḥ] Vruttīkaraṇā yekavaḷā | chitta jāvo nedaṇe phaḷā | niyamāchiyā sāṅkhaḷā | vāhaṇe sadā || Jñāne.18.637 || Hā nirodha sāhāvayālāgī | dhairyāchiyā chāṅgāchāṅgī | chiṅtavaṇī jitī āṅgī | vāhe ĵo kā || Jñāne.18.638 || Āṇi ātmayāchiye āvaḍī | karme karitā varapaḍī | dehasukhāchiye paravaḍī | yevo na lāhe || Jñāne.18.639 || Aisā nidrā durhāve | kṣhudhā na bāṇave | suravāḍa na pāve | āṅgāchā ṭhāvo || Jñāne.18.640 || Tava adhikādhika | utsāha dharī āgaḷīka | sone jaise puṭī tuka | tuṭaliyā kasī || Jñāne.18.641 || Ĵarī āvaḍī āthī sācha | tarī jīviteṁhī salacha | āgī ghālitā romāṅcha | dekhijatī satiye || Jñāne.18.642 || Mā ātmayā yevaḍhiyā priyā | vālabhelā ĵo dhanaṅjayā | dehahī sidatā tayā | kāya kheda hoīla || Jñāne.18.643 || Mhaṇauni viṣhayasuravāḍa tuṭe | jaṅva jaṅva dehabuddhi āṭe | tava tava ānaṅda duṇavaṭe | karmī jayā || Jñāne.18.644 || [Siddhyasiddhyornirvikāraḥ] Aiseni ĵo karma karī | āṇi koṇe yeke avasarī | te ṭhāke aisī sarī | vāhe ĵarī || Jñāne.18.645 || Tarī kaḍāḍī moḍe gāḍā | to āpaṇape na manī avaghaḍā | taisā ṭhākalenihī thoḍā | nohe ĵo kā || Jñāne.18.646 || Nā tarī ādarile | avyaṅga siddhī gele | tari teṅhī jiṅtile | miravū neṇe || Jñāne.18.647 || Iyā khuṇā karma karitā | dekhije ĵo Paṅḍusutā | [kartā sāttwika uchyate] tayāte mhaṇipe tattwatā | sāttwika kartā || Jñāne.18.648 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā rājasā karteyā | voḷakhaṇe he dhanaṅjayā | je abhilāṣhā jagāchiyā | vasauṭā to || Jñāne.18.649 ||

Rāgī karmaphalaprepsurlubdho hiṁsātmako’shuchiḥ(hi) | harṣhashokānvitaḥ(kh) kartā rājasaḥ(ph) parikīrtitaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.27 ||

[Rāgī] Jaisā gāṅvīṅchiyā kashmaḷā | ukaraḍā hoya yekavaḷā | kā smashānī amaṅgaḷā | āghavayāṅchi || Jñāne.18.650 || Tayāparī ĵo asheṣhā | vishwāchiyā abhilāṣhā | pāyapākhāḷaṇiyā doṣhā | gharaṭā jālā || Jñāne.18.651 || [Karmaphalaprepsuḥ(hu)] Mhaṇoni phaḷāchā lāga | dekhe jiye asalaga | tiye karmī chāṅga | roho māṅḍī || Jñāne.18.652 || Āṇi āpaṇa jāliye ĵoḍī | upakho nedī kavaḍī | kṣhaṇakṣhaṇā kuroṅḍī | jīvāchī karī || Jñāne.18.653 || [Lubdhaḥ] Krupaṇachittī ṭhevā āpulā | taisā dakṣha parāviyā mālā | baka jaisā khutalā | māseyāsī || Jñāne.18.654 || [Hiṁsātmakaḥ] Āṇi goṅvī geliyā javaḷī | jhagaṭaliyā āṅga phāḷī | phaḷe tarī āṅta pokaḷī | borāṅṭī jaisī || Jñāne.18.655 || Taise mane vāchā kāye | bhalatayā duḥkha deta jāye | swārtha sādhitā na pāhe | parāche hita || Jñāne.18.656 || [Ashuchiḥ(hi)] Tevīṅcha āṅge karmī | ācharaṇa nohe kṣhamī | na nighe manodharmī | arochaka || Jñāne.18.657 || Kanakāchiye phaḷā | āṅta māja bāherī mauḷā | taisā sabāhya dubaḷā | shuchitwe ĵo || Jñāne.18.658 || [Harṣhashokānvitaḥ] Āṇi karmajāta keliyā | phaḷa lāhe ĵarī dhanaṅjayā | tari harikhe jagā yayā | vāṅkuliyā vāye || Jñāne.18.659 || [Kartā rājasaḥ(ph) parikīrtitaḥ] Athavā je ādarile | hīnaphaḷa hoya kele | tari shoke teṇe jiṅtile | dhiŠkāro lāge || Jñāne.18.660 || Karmī rāhāṭī aisī | jayāte hotī dekhasī | tochi ĵāṇa trishuddhīsī | rājasa kartā || Jñāne.18.661 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā yayā pāṭhī yera | ĵo kukarmāchā āgara | tohī karū gochara | tāmasa kartā || Jñāne.18.662 ||

Ayuktaḥ(ph) prākrutaḥ(s) stabdhaḥ(sh) shaṭho naiṣhkrutiko’lasaḥ | viṣhādī dīrghasūtrī cha kartā tāmasa uchyate || Bha.Gī.18.28 ||

[Ayuktaḥ] Tari miyā lāgaliyā kaise | puḍhīla jaḷata ase | he neṇije hutāshe | jiyāparī || Jñāne.18.663 || Pai shastre miyā tikhaṭe | neṇije kaiseni nivaṭe | kā neṇije kāḷakūṭe | āpale kele || Jñāne.18.664 || Taisā puḍhiliyā āpuliyā | ghāta karīta dhanaṅjayā | ādarī vokhaṭiyā | kriyā ĵo kā || Jñāne.18.665 || Tiyā karitāṁhī veḷī | kāya ĵāle he na sāṁbhāḷī | chaḷalā vāyū vāhaṭuḷī | cheṣhṭe taisā || Jñāne.18.666 || Pai karaṇiyā āṇi jayā | meḷa nāhī dhanaṅjayā | to pāhūni piseyā | kaiṅchī trāya || Jñāne.18.667 || [Prākrutaḥ] Āṇi iṅdriyāṅche vairile | charoni rākhe ĵo jiyāle | bailātaḷī lāgale | gochiḍa jaise || Jñāne.18.668 || Hāṁsayā rudanā veḷa | neṇatā ādarī bāḷa | rāhaṭe uchchhruṅkhaḷa | tayāparī || Jñāne.18.669 || Ĵo prakruti ātalepaṇe | krutyākrutyaswāda neṇe | phuge kere dhālepaṇe | ukaraḍā jaisā || Jñāne.18.670 || [Stabdhaḥ] Mhaṇauni mānyācheni nāve | īshwarāhī parī na khālave | stabdhapaṇe na manave | ḍoṅgarāsī || Jñāne.18.671 || [Shaṭhaḥ] Āṇi mana jayāche kalālī | rāhāṭī phuḍī chorilī | diṭhī kīra te votalī | paṇyāṅganechī || Jñāne.18.672 || Kiṅbahunā kapaṭāche | dehachi vaḷile tayāche | te jiṇe kī juvārāche | ṭiṭaghara || Jñāne.18.673 || Nohe tayāĉhā prādurbhāvo | to sābhilāṣha bhillāṅchā gāṁvo | mhaṇauni na ye yevo jāvo | tayā ṭhāyā || Jñāne.18.674 || [Naiṣhkrutikaḥ] Maga āṇikāche nike kele | viru hoya jayā āle | jaise apeya payā minale | lavaṇa karī || Jñāne.18.675 || Kā hiṁva aisā padārtha | ghātaliyā āgīāṅta | techi kṣhaṇī dhaḍāḍita | agni hoya || Jñāne.18.676 || Nā nā sudravye gomaṭī | jāliyā sharīrī paiṭhī | hoūni ṭhātī kirīṭī | maḷachi jevī || Jñāne.18.677 || Taise puḍhilāche barave | jayāchyā bhītarī pāve | āṇi viruddhachi āghave | hoūni nige || Jñāne.18.678 || Ĵo guṇa ghe de doṣha | amrutāche karī viṣha | dūdha pājiliyā dekha | vyāḷa jaisā || Jñāne.18.679 || [Alasaḥ] Āṇi aihikī jiyāve | jeṇe paratrā sācha yāve | te uchita krutya pāve | avasarī jiye || Jñāne.18.680 || Tevhā jayā āpaisī | nidrā ye ṭhevilī aisī | durvyavahārī jaisī | viṭāḷe loṭe || Jñāne.18.681 || Pai drākṣharasā āmrarasā | veḷe toṅḍa saḍe vāyasā | kā ḍoḷe phuṭatī divasā | ḍuḍuḷāche || Jñāne.18.682 || Taisā kalyāṇa kāḷa pāhe | tai tayāte āḷasa khāye | nā pramādī tari hoye | to mhaṇe taise || Jñāne.18.683 || [Viṣhādī] Jevīṅchi sāgarāchyā poṭī | jaḷe akhaṅḍa āgiṭhī | taisā viṣhāda vāhe gāṅṭhī | jivāchiye ĵo || Jñāne.18.684 || Leṅḍoṅrāāgī dhūmāvadhi | kā
