apānā āṅgī durgaṅdhi | taisā ĵo jīvitāvadhi | viṣhāde kelā || Jñāne.18.685 || [Dīrghasūtrī cha] Āṇi kalpāṅtāchiyā pārā | vegaḷeṅhī ĵo vīrā | sūtra dharī vyāpārā | sābhilāṣhā || Jñāne.18.686 || Agā jagāhī parautī | shuchā vāhe pai chittī | karitāṁviṣhī hātī | truṇahī na lage || Jñāne.18.687 || [Kartā tāmasa uchyate] Aisā ĵo lokāāṅta | pāpapuṅja mūrta | dekhasī to avyāhata | tāmasa kartā || Jñāne.18.688 || Eva karma kartā jñāna | yā tihīṅche tridhā chinha | dāvile tuĵa sujana- | chakravartī || Jñāne.18.689 || [Kartrutraividhyena jñāturapi traividhyamuktaṁ | karmatraividhyena jñeyasyāpyuktaṁ | buddhestraividhyena karaṇasyāpyuktaṁ | idānīṁ buddherdhruteshchāpi traividhyaṁ pratijānīte-]

Buddherbhedaṁ(n) dhruteshchaiva guṇatastrividhaṁ shrruṇu | prochyamānamasheṣheṇa pruthaktwena Dhanañjaya || Bha.Gī.18.29 ||

[Buddherbhedaṁ] Ātā avidyechyā gāṁvī | mohāchī veḍhūni madavī | saṅdehāchī āghavī | leūni leṇī || Jñāne.18.690 || Ātmanishchayāchī barava | jayā ārisā pāhe sāvayava | tiye buddhīchīhī dhāva | tridhā ase || Jñāne.18.691 || [Guṇatastrividhaṁ shrruṇu] Agā sattwādi guṇī iṁhī | kāi eka tihī ṭhāyī | na kījechi yetha pāhī | jagāmājī || Jñāne.18.692 || Āgī na vasatā poṭī | kavaṇa kāṣhṭha ase sruṣhṭī | taise te kaiṅche drushyakoṭī | trividha je nohe || Jñāne.18.693 || Mhaṇauni tihī guṇī | buddhī kelī triguṇī | [dhruteshchaiva] dhrutīsihī vāṅṭaṇī | taisīchi ase || Jñāne.18.694 || [Prochyamānamiti] Techi yeka vegaḷāle | yathāchinhī aḷaṅkārale | sāṅgijela upāile | bhedalepaṇe || Jñāne.18.695 || [Chūrṇikā] Pari buddhi dhruti iyā | dohī bhāgāṅmāji dhanaṅjayā | ādhī rūpa buddhīchiyā | bhedāsi karū || Jñāne.18.696 || Tari uttama madhyama nikruṣhṭā | saṅsārāsi gā subhaṭā | prāṇiyā yetiyā vāṭā | tinī āthī || Jñāne.18.697 || Je karaṇīya kāmya niṣhiddha | te he mārga tinhī prasiddha | saṁsāra bhaya saṁbaṅdha | jīvā yayā || Jñāne.18.698 ||

Pravruttiṁ(ñ) cha Nivruttiṁ(ñ) cha kāryākārye bhayābhaye | bandhaṁ mokṣhaṁ(ñ) cha yā vetti buddhiḥ(s) sā Pārth sāttwikī || Bha.Gī.18.30 ||

[Pravruttiṁ(ñ) cha] Mhaṇauni adhikāre mānile | je vidhīcheni voghe āle | te yekachi yetha bhale | nitya karma || Jñāne.18.699 || [Kāryeti] Techi ātmaprāpti phaḷa | diṭhī sūni kevaḷa | kīje jaise kā jaḷa | sevije tāhane || Jñāne.18.700 || Yetuleni te karma | [abhaye] sāṅḍī janmabhaya viṣhama | karūni de sugama | mokṣhasiddhi || Jñāne.18.701 || Aise karī to bhalā | saṁsārabhaye sāṅḍilā | kāraṇīyatwe ālā | mumukṣhubhāgā || Jñāne.18.702 || [Mokṣhaṁ(ñ) cha] Tetha je buddhi aisā | baḷiyā bāṅdhe bharaṁvasā | mokṣha ṭhevilā aisā | ĵoḍela yetha || Jñāne.18.703 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Mhaṇauni nivruttīchi māṅḍalī | sūni pravrutti taḷī | iye karmī buḍakuḷī | dyāvī kī nā || Jñāne.18.704 || Truṣhārtā udake jiṇe | kā purī paḍaliyā pavhaṇe | aṅdhakūpī gati kiraṇe | sūryācheni || Jñāne.18.705 || Nā nā pathyeṁsī auṣhadha lāhe | tarī roge dāṭalāhī jiye | kā mīnā jivhāḷā hoye | jaḷāchā ĵarī || Jñāne.18.706 || Tari tayāchyā jīvitā | nāhī jevi anyathā | taise karmī iye vartatā | ĵoḍechi mokṣha || Jñāne.18.707 || He karaṇīyāchiyā kaḍe | je jñāna āthī ĉhokhaḍe | [Nivruttiṁ(ñ) cha] āṇi akaraṇīya he phuḍe | aise ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.708 || [Akārye] Jī tiye kāmyādike | saṁsārabhayadāyake | akrutyapaṇāche āṁbukhe | paḍile jayā || Jñāne.18.709 || Tiye karmī akāryī | [bhaye] janmamaraṇasamayī | pravrutti paḷavī pāyī | māgilīchi || Jñāne.18.710 || Pai āgīmāji na righave | athāvī na ghalave | dhagadhagīta nāgave | shūḷa jevī || Jñāne.18.711 || Kā kāḷiyā nāga dhuṅdhuvāta | dekhoni na ghālave hāta | na vachave khoṁpeāṅta | vyāghrāchiye || Jñāne.18.712 || Taise karma akaraṇīya | dekhoni mahābhaya | upaĵe niḥsaṅdeha | buddhi jiye || Jñāne.18.713 || [Bandhaṁ] Vāḍhile rāṅdhūni viṣhe | tetha jāṇije mrutyu na chuke | tevi niṣhiddhī kā dekhe | baṅdhāte ĵo || Jñāne.18.714 || [Yā vetti] Maga baṅdhabhayabharitī | tiye niṣhiddhī prāptī | viniyoga ĵāṇe nivruttī | karmāchiye || Jñāne.18.715 || Aiseni kāryākāryavivekī | je pravruttiNivrutti-māpakī | kharā kuḍā pārakhī | jiyāparī || Jñāne.18.716 || [Buddhiḥ(s) sā Pārth sāttwikī] Taisī krutyākrutyashuddhī | bujhe je niravadhī | sāttwika mhaṇipe buddhī | techi tū ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.717 ||

Yayā dharmamadharmaṁ(ñ) cha kāryaṁ(ñ) chākāryameva cha | ayathāvatprajānāti buddhiḥ(s) sā Pārth rājasī || Bha.Gī.18.31 ||

[Yayeti] Āṇi bakāchyā gāṁvī | ghepe kṣhīranīra sakalavī | kā ahorātrīṅchī goṁvī | āṅdhaḷe neṇe || Jñāne.18.718 || Jayā phulāchā makaraṅda phāve | to kāṣhṭhe korū dhāṁve | pari bhramarapaṇā navhe | avhāṅṭā jevī || Jñāne.18.719 || Taisī iye kāryākārye | dharmādharmarūpe jiye | [ayathāvatprajānāti] tiye na chojavitā jāye | ĵāṇatī je kā || Jñāne.18.720 || Agā ḍoḷāṁvīṇa motiye | ghetā pāḍa miḷe vipāye | na miḷaṇe te āhe | ṭhevile tethe || Jñāne.18.721 || Taise akaraṇīya avachaṭe | noḍave tarīcha loṭe | yeravī ĵāṇe ekavaṭe | donhī je kā || Jñāne.18.722 || [Buddhiḥ(s) sā Pārth rājasī] Te gā buddhi chokhavikhī | ĵāṇa yetha rājasī | akṣhata ṭākilī jaisī | māṅdiyevarī || Jñāne.18.723 ||

Adharmaṁ(n) dharmamiti yā manyate tamasāvrutā | sarvārthānviparītāṁshcha buddhiḥ(s) sā Pārth tāmasī || Bha.Gī.18.32 ||

[Adharmamiti] Āṇi rājā jiyā vāṭā jāye | te chorāṁsi āḍava hoye | kā rākṣhasā divo pāhe | rāti houni || Jñāne.18.724 || Nā nā nidhānachi nidaivā | hoye koḷasayāĉhā uḍavā | pai asate āpaṇape jīvā | nāhī ĵāle || Jñāne.18.725 || Taise dharmajāta titake | jiye buddhīsī pātake | sācha te laṭike | aiseṅchi bujhe || Jñāne.18.726 || [Sarveti] Te āghavechi artha | karūni ghālī anartha | guṇa te te vyavasthita | doṣhachi mānī || Jñāne.18.727 || Kiṁbahunā shrutijāte | adhiṣhṭhūni kele sarate | tetuleṁhi uparate | ĵāṇe je buddhī || Jñāne.18.728 || Koṇāteṅhī na pusatā | tāmasī jāṇāvī Paṅḍusutā | rātrī kāya dharmārthā | sācha karāvī || Jñāne.18.729 || Eva buddhīche bheda | tinhī tuĵa vishada | sāṅgītale swabodha- | kumudachaṅdrā || Jñāne.18.730 || Ātā yayāchi buddhivruttī | niṣhṭaṅkilā karmajātī | khāṅda māṅḍije dhrutī | trividhā jayā || Jñāne.18.731 || Tiye dhrutīchehī vibhāga | tinhī yathāliṅga | sāṅgījatī chāṅga | avadhāna de || Jñāne.18.732 ||

Dhrutyā yayā dhārayate manaḥprāṇendriyakriyāḥ(hā) | yogenāvyabhichāriṇyā dhrutiḥ(s) sā Pārth sāttwikī || Bha.Gī.18.33 ||

[Dhrutyā yayā] Tari udeliyā dinakara | chorīsī thoke aṅdhakāra | kā rājājñā avyavahāra | kuṅṭhavī jevī || Jñāne.18.733 || Nā nā pavanāchā sāṭa | vājīnaliyā nīṭa | āṅgeṁsī bobhāṭa | sāṅḍitī megha || Jñāne.18.734 || Kā agastīcheni darshane | siṅdhu gheunī ṭhātī maune | chaṅdrodayī kamaḷavane | miṭhī detī || Jñāne.18.735 || He aso pāvo uchalilā | madamukha na ṭhevitī khālā | garĵoni puḍhā jālā | siṅha ĵarī || Jñāne.18.736 || Taisā ĵo dhīra | uṭhaliyā aṅtara | manādike vyāpāra | sāṅḍitī ubhī || Jñāne.18.737 || [Indriyakriyāḥ(hā)] Iṅdriyā viṣhayāṅchiyā gāṅṭhī | apaisā suṭatī kirīṭī | mana māyechyā poṭī | rigatī dāhī || Jñāne.18.738 || [Prāṇa-] Adhordhwa guḍhe kāḍhī | prāṇa navāṅchī peṅḍī | bāṅdhoni ghālī uḍī | madhyamemājī || Jñāne.18.739 || Saṅkalpavikalpāche lugaḍe | sāṅḍūni mana ughaḍe | buddhi māgilekaḍe | ugīchi baise || Jñāne.18.740 || [Dhārayate] Aisī dhairyarāje jeṇe | mana prāṇa karaṇe | swacheṣhṭāṅchī saṁbhāṣhaṇe | sāṅḍa-vījatī || Jñāne.18.741 || [Yogena] Maga āghavīṅchi saḍī | dhyānāchyā āṅtulyā maḍhī | koṅḍijatī niravaḍī | yogāchiye || Jñāne.18.742 || [Avyabhichāriṇyā] Parī paramātmayā chakravartī | ugāṇitī ĵava hātī | tava lāṅcha na ghetā dhrutī | dharijatī jiyā || Jñāne.18.743 || [Dhrutiḥ(s) sā Pārth sāttwikī] Te gā dhruti yethe | sāttwika he nirute | āīka Arjunāte | Shreekāṅta mhaṇe || Jñāne.18.744 ||

Yayā tu dharmakāmārthāndhrutyā dhārayate’rjuna | prasaṅggena phalākāṅgkṣhī dhrutiḥ(s) sā Pārth rājasī || Bha.Gī.18.34 ||

[Yayeti] Āṇi hoūniyā sharīrī | swargasaṅsārāchyā dohī gharī | nāṅde ĵo poṭabharī | trivargopāye || Jñāne.18.745 || To manorathāṅchyā sāgarī | dharmārthakāmāṅchyā tāruvāvarī | jeṇe dhairyabaḷe karī | kriyā vāṇijya || Jñāne.18.746 || [Prasaṅggeneti] Je karma bhāṅḍavalā suye | tayāchī chauguṇī yetī pāhe | yevaḍhe sāhasa vāhe | jayā dhrutī || Jñāne.18.747 || Te gā dhrutī rājasa | Pārthā yetha pariyesa | ātā āika tāmasa | tisarī je kā || Jñāne.18.748 ||

Yayā swapnaṁ bhayaṁ shokaṁ viṣhādaṁ madameva cha | na vimuñchati durmedhā dhrutiḥ(s) sā Pārth tāmasī || Bha.Gī.18.35 ||

[Yayā] Tarī sarvādhame guṇe | jayāche kā rūpā yeṇe | koḷasā kāḷepaṇe | ghaḍalā jaisā || Jñāne.18.749 || Aho prākruta āṇi hīna | tayāhī kī guṇatwāchā māna | pari na mhaṇije puṇyajana | rākṣhasa kāī || Jñāne.18.750 || Pai grahāṁmāji iṅgaḷa | tayāte mhaṇije maṅgaḷa | taisā tamī dhasāḷa | guṇashabda hā || Jñāne.18.751 || Je sarva doṣhāṅĉhā vasauṭā | tamachi kāmaūni subhaṭā | ubhārilā āṅgavaṭhā | jayā narāchā || Jñāne.18.752 || [Swapnaṁ] To āḷasa sūni ase kāṅkhe | mhaṇauni nidre kaṅhī na muke | pāpe poshitā duḥkhe | na sāṅḍije jevī || Jñāne.18.753 || [Bhayaṁ] Āṇi dehā dhanāchiyā āvaḍī | sadā bhaya tayāte na sāṅḍī | visaṅbū na sake dhoṅḍī | kāṭhiṇya jaise || Jñāne.18.754 || [Shokaṁ] Āṇi padārthajātī sneho | bāṅdhe mhaṇauni to shoke ṭhāvo | kelā na shake pāpa jāvo | krutaghnauni jaise || Jñāne.18.755 || [Viṣhādaṁ] Āṇi asaṅtoṣha jīveṁsī | dharūni ṭhelā aharnishī | mhaṇauni maitrī teṇeṁsī | viṣhāde kelī || Jñāne.18.756 || Lasaṇāte na sāṅḍī gaṅdhī | kā apathyashīḷāte vyādhī | taisī kelī maraṇāvadhī | viṣhāde tayā || Jñāne.18.757 || [Madameva cha] Āṇi vayasā vitta kāma | yayāṅchā vāḍhavī saṁbhrama | mhaṇauni made āshrama | tochi kelā || Jñāne.18.758 || [Dhrutiḥ(s) sā Pārth tāmasī] Āgīte na sāṅḍī tāpa | saḷāte jātīchā sāpa | kā jagāchā vairī vāsipa | akhaṅḍa jaisā || Jñāne.18.759 || Nā tari sharīrāte kāḷa | na visaṅbe kavaṇe veḷa | taisā āthi aḍhaḷa | tāmasī mada || Jñāne.18.760 || [Na vimuñchati durmedhā] Eva pāṅchahī he nidrādika | tāmasāchyā ṭhāī dokha | jiyā dhrutī dekha | dharile āhātī || Jñāne.18.761 || Tiye gā dhrutī nāve | tāmasī tetha he ĵāṇāve | mhaṇītale teṇe deve | jagāchenī || Jñāne.18.762 || [Shlokatrayabhāvaḥ] Eva trividha je buddhi | kīje karmanishchayo ādhi | to dhrutī yā siddhi | neiĵo yetha || Jñāne.18.763 || Sūrye mārga gochara hoye | āṇi to chālatī kīra pāye | pari chālaṇe te āhe | dhairye jevī || Jñāne.18.764 || Taisī buddhi karmāte dāvī | te karaṇasāmagrī niphajavī | pari niphajāvayā hoāvī | dhīratā je || Jñāne.18.765 || Te he gā tuĵaprati | sāṅgītalī trividha dhruti | yayā karmatrayā niṣhpatti | jāliyā maga || Jñāne.18.766 || [Chūrṇikā] Yetha phaḷa je eka niphaje | sukha jayāte mhaṇije | teṅhī trividha jāṇije | karmavashe || Jñāne.18.767 || Tari phaḷarūpa te sukha | triguṇī bhedale dekha | vivachū ātā chokha | chokhī bolī || Jñāne.18.768 || Pari chokhī te kaisī sāṅge | pai ghevo jātā bolabage | kānīṅchiyehī lāge | hātīĉhā maḷa || Jñāne.18.769 || Mhaṇauni jayāĉheni avhere | avadhānahī hoya bahire | teṇe āika ho ādare | jivācheni || Jñāne.18.770 || Aise mhaṇauni devo | trividhā sukhāchā prastāvo | māṅḍalā to nirvāho | nirūpita ase || Jñāne.18.771 ||

Sukhaṁ(n) twidānīṁ(n) trividhaṁ shrruṇu me bharatarṣhabha | abhyāsādramate yatra duḥ(hu)khāntaṁ(ñ) cha nigachchhati || Bha.Gī.18.36 ||

[Sukhaṁ(n) twidānīmiti] Mhaṇe sukhatrayasaṅjñā | sāṅgo mhaṇauni pratijñā | bolilo te prājñā | aika ātā || Jñāne.18.772 || Tari sukha te gā kirīṭī | dāvijela tuĵa diṭhī | je ātmayāchiye bheṭī | jīvāsi hoya || Jñāne.18.773 || [Abhyāsādramate yatra] Pari mātrecheni māpe | divyauṣhadha jaise ghepe | kā kathilāche kīje rupe | rasabhāvanī || Jñāne.18.774 || Nā nā lavaṇāche jaḷa | hoāvayā donī chāra veḷa | deūni sāṅḍijatī ḍhāḷa | toyāche jevī || Jñāne.18.775 || Tevi ĵāleni sukhaleshe | jīva bhāviliyā abhyāse | [duḥ(hu)khāntaṁ(ñ) cha nigachchhati] jīvapaṇāche nāse | duḥkha jethe || Jñāne.18.776 || [Chūrṇikā] Te yetha ātmasukha | ĵāle ase triguṇātmaka | teṁhī sāṅgo ekaika | rūpa ātā || Jñāne.18.777 ||

Yattadagre viṣhamiva pariṇāme’mrutopamam | tatsukhaṁ sāttwikaṁ proktamātmabuddhiprasādajam || Bha.Gī.18.37 ||

[Yattadagre viṣhamiva] Ātā chaṅdanāche buḍa | sarpī jaise duvāḍa | kā nidhānāche toṅḍa | vivasiyā jevi || Jñāne.18.778 || Agā swargīṅche gomaṭe | āḍava yāgasaṅkaṭe | kā bāḷapaṇa dāsaṭe | trāsakāḷe || Jñāne.18.779 || He aso dīpāchiye siddhī | avaghaḍa dhūma ādhī | nā tari to auṣhadhī | jibhechā ṭhāvo || Jñāne.18.780 || Tayāpari Pāṅḍavā | jayā sukhāchā rigāvā | viṣhama tetha meḷāvā | yamadamāṅchā || Jñāne.18.781 || Deta sarvasnehā miṭhī | āṅgī aise vairāgya uṭhī | swargasaṅsārā kāṅṭī | kāḍhītachi || Jñāne.18.782 || Viveka shravaṇe kharapuse | jetha vratācharaṇe karkashe | karitā jātī bhokase | buddhyādikāṅche || Jñāne.18.783 || Suṣhumnecheni toṅḍe | giḷije prāṇāpānāṅche loṅḍhe | bohaṇiyesīchi yevaḍhe | bhārī jetha || Jñāne.18.784 || Je sārasāṁhī vighaḍatā | hoya vohāhūni vatsa kāḍhitā | nā bhaṇaṅga davaḍitā | bhāṇayāvarūnī || Jñāne.18.785 || Pai māyepuḍhauni bāḷaka | kāḷe netā ekulate eka | hoya kā udaka | tuṭatā mīnā || Jñāne.18.786 || Taise viṣhayāṅche ghara | iṅdriyā sāṅḍitā thora | yugāṅta hoya te vīra | virāga sāhātī || Jñāne.18.787 || Aisā jayā sukhāchā āraṁbha | dāvī kāṭhiṇyāĉhā kṣhobha | [pariṇāme’mrutopamaṁ] maga kṣhīrābdhī lābha | amrutāchā jaisā || Jñāne.18.788 || Pahilayā vairāgyagaraḷā | dhairyaShaṁbhu voḍavī gaḷā | tari jñānāmrute sohaḷā | pāhe jethe || Jñāne.18.789 || Pai kavalitāhi kope aise | drākṣhāṅche hiravepaṇa ase | te paripākī kā jaise | mādhurya āte || Jñāne.18.790 || [Ātmabuddhiprasādajaṁ] Te vairāgyādika taise | pikaliyā ātmaprakāshe | maga vairāgyeṅsīṅhī nāshe | avidyājāta || Jñāne.18.791 || Tevhā sāgarī Gaṅgā jaisī | ātmī mīnalyā buddhi taisī | adwayānaṅdāchī āpaisī | khāṇī ughaḍe || Jñāne.18.792 || Aise swānubhavavishrāme | vairāgyamūḷa je pariṇame | [tatsukhaṁ sāttwikaṁ proktaṁ] te sāttwika yeṇe nāme | bolije sukha || Jñāne.18.793 ||

Viṣhayendriyasaṁyogādyattadagre’mrutopamam | pariṇāme viṣhamiva tatsukhaṁ rājasaṁ smrutam || Bha.Gī.18.38 ||

[Viṣhayateti] Āṇi viṣhayeṅdriyā | meḷa hotā dhanaṅjayā | je sukha ĵāya thaḍiyā | sāṅḍūni donhī || Jñāne.18.794 || Adhikāriyā rigatā gāṁvo | hoya jaisā utsāho | kā riṇāvarī vivāho | vistārilā || Jñāne.18.795 || Nā nā rogiyā jibhepāsī | keḷe goḍa sākharesī | kā bachanāgāchī jaisī | madhuratā pahilī || Jñāne.18.796 || Pahile saṁvachorāche maitra | hāṭabheṭīche kalatra | kā lāghavīyāche vichitra | vinoda te || Jñāne.18.797 || Taise viṣhayeṅdriyadokhī | je sukha jīvāte pokhī | [pariṇāme viṣhamiva] maga upaḍilā khaḍakī | haṅsa jaisā || Jñāne.18.798 || Taisī ĵoḍī āghavī āṭe | jīvitāchā ṭhāya phiṭe | sukrutāchiyāhī suṭe | dhanāchī gāṅṭhī || Jñāne.18.799 || Āṇika bhogile je kāhī | te swapna taise hoya nāhī | maga hānīchāchi ghāī | loḷāve ure || Jñāne.18.800 || Aise āpattī je sukha | aihikī pariṇame dekha | paratrī kīra vikha | houni parate || Jñāne.18.801 || Je iṅdriyajātā laḷā | didhaliyā dharmāchā maḷā | ĵāḷūni bhogije sohaḷā | viṣhayāṅchā jetha || Jñāne.18.802 || Tetha pātake bāṅdhitī thāvo | tiye narakī detī ṭhāvo | jeṇe sukhe hā apāvo | paratrī aisā || Jñāne.18.803 || Pai nāme viṣha madhure | pari mārūni aṅtī khare | taise ādi je goḍire | aṅtī kaḍu || Jñāne.18.804 || [Tatsukhaṁ rājasaṁ smrutam] Pārthā te sukha sāche | vaḷile āhe rajāche | mhaṇauni na shive tayāche | āṅga kaṁhī || Jñāne.18.805 ||

Yadagre chānubandhe cha sukhaṁ mohanamātmanaḥ | nidrālasyapramādotthaṁ(n) tattāmasamudāhrutam || Bha.Gī.18.39 ||

[Yadagre iti] Āṇi apeyācheni pāne | akhādyācheni bhojane | swairastrīsaṅnidhāne | hoya je sukha || Jñāne.18.806 || Kā puḍhilāṅcheni māre | tari paraswāpahāre | je sukha avatare | bhāṭāchyā bolī || Jñāne.18.807 || [Nidrālasyapramādotthaṁ] Je ālasyāvarī pokhije | nidremājī je dekhije | jayāchyā ādyaṅtī bhulije | āpulī vāṭa || Jñāne.18.808 || [Tattāmasamudāhrutam] Te gā sukha Pārthā | tāmasa ĵāṇa sarvathā | he bahudhā na sāṅgoṅchi je kathā | asaṁbhāvya he || Jñāne.18.809 || Aise karmabhede mudale | phaḷasukhahī tridhā ĵāle | te he yathāgame kele | gochara tuĵa || Jñāne.18.810 || Te kartā karma phaḷa | he tripuṭī yekī kevaḷa | vāṅchūni kāhīṅchi nase sthūḷa- | sūkṣhmī iye || Jñāne.18.811 || Āṇi he tava tripuṭī | tihī guṇī iṅhī kirīṭī | guṁphilī ase paṭī | tāṅtuvī jaisī || Jñāne.18.812 ||

Na tadasti pruthivyāṁ vā divi deveṣhu vā punaḥ | sattwaṁ prakrutijairmuktaṁ yadebhiḥ(s) syāttribhirguṇaiḥ(hi) || Bha.Gī.18.40 ||

[Sattwaṁ prakrutijairiti] Mhaṇauni prakrutīchyā ālokī | na baṅdhije iṁhī sattwādikī | [na tadastīti] taisī swargī nā mrutyulokī | āthī vastu || Jñāne.18.813 || Kaiṅchā loṅvevīṇa kāṁbaḷā | mātiyevīṇa modaḷā | kā jaḷeṅvīṇa kalloḷā | hoṇe āhe || Jñāne.18.814 || Taise na honi guṇāche | sruṣhṭīchyā rachanā rache | aise nāhīṅcha gā sāche | prāṇijāta || Jñāne.18.815 || Yālāgī he sakaḷa | tihī guṇāṅchechi kevaḷa | ghaḍale āhe nikhiḷa | aise ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.816 || Guṇī devā trayī lāvilī | guṇī lokī tripuṭī [trutīyādhyāyoktaṁ(ṅ) karmayogaṁ(n) darshayituṁ prakaraṇāntaramārabhate brāmhaṇetyaṣhṭabhiḥ(hi)] pāḍilī | [chūrṇikā] chaturvarṇā ghātalī | sinānī uḷige || Jñāne.18.817 ||

Brāmhaṇakṣhatriyavishāṁ shūdrāṇāṁ(ñ) cha parantapa | karmāṇi pravibhaktāni swabhāvaprabhavairguṇaiḥ(hi) || Bha.Gī.18.41 ||

[Brāmhaṇakṣhatriyeti] Techi chārī varṇa | pusasī ĵarī koṇa koṇa | tari jayā mukhya brāmhaṇa | dhureche kā || Jñāne.18.818 || Yera kṣhatriya vaishya donhī | tehī brāmhaṇāchyāchi mānije mānī | je te vaidika vidhānī | yogya mhaṇaunī || Jñāne.18.819 || Chauthā shūdra ĵo dhanaṅjayā | vedī lāga kīra nāhī tayā | tarhī vrutti varṇatrayā- | adhīna tayāchī || Jñāne.18.820 || Tiye vruttīchiyā javaḷikā | varṇatrayā brāmhaṇāṅdikā | aho shūdrahī kī dekhā | chauthā jālā || Jñāne.18.821 || Jaisā phulācheni sāṅgāte | tāṅtu turaṁbije Shreemaṅte | taise dwijasaṅge shūdrāte | swīkārī shrutī || Jñāne.18.822 || Aisaisī gā Pārthā | he chaturvarṇavyavasthā | karū ātā karmapathā | yāṅchiyā rūpa || Jñāne.18.823 || [Karmāṇi pravibhaktāni] Jihī guṇī te varṇa chārī | janmamrutyūṅchiye kātarī | chukoniyā īshwarī | paiṭhe hotī || Jñāne.18.824 || Jiye ātmaprakrutīche iṁhī | guṇī sattwādikī tihī | karme chaughā chahū ṭhāī | vāṅṭilī varṇā || Jñāne.18.825 || Jaise bāpe ĵoḍile leṅkā | vāṅṭile sūrye mārga pāṅthikā | nā nā vyāpāra sevakā | swāmīne jaise || Jñāne.18.826 || [Swabhāvaprabhavairguṇaiḥ(hi)] Taisī prakrutīchyā guṇī | jayā karmāchī velhāvaṇī | kelī āhe varṇī | chahū iṁhī || Jñāne.18.827 || Tetha sattwe āpalyā āṅgī | samīnanimīna bhāgī | doghe kele niyogī | brāmhaṇa kṣhatriya || Jñāne.18.828 || Āṇi raja parī sāttwika | tetha ṭhevile vaishya loka | rajachi tamabhesaka | tetha shūdra te gā || Jñāne.18.829 || Aisā yekāchi prāṇivruṅdā | bheda chaturvarṇadhā | guṇīṅchi iṁhī prabuddhā | kelā ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.830 || Maga āpale ṭhevile jaise | āitechi dīpe dise | guṇabhinna karma taise | shāstra dāvī || Jñāne.18.831 || Techi ātā koṇa koṇa | varṇavihitāche lakṣhaṇa | he sāṅgo aika shravaṇa- | saubhāgyanidhī || Jñāne.18.832 ||

Shamo damastapaḥ(sh) shauchaṁ(ṅ) kṣhāntirārjavameva cha | jñānaṁ vijñānamāstikyaṁ brahmakarma swabhāvajam || Bha.Gī.18.42 ||

[Shamaḥ] Tari sarveṅdriyāṅchiyā vruttī | gheūni āpulyā hātī | buddhi ātmayā miḷe yekāṅtī | priyā jaisī || Jñāne.18.833 || Aisā buddhīchā uparama | tayā nāma mhaṇipe shama | to guṇa gā upakrama | jayā karmāchā || Jñāne.18.834 || [Damaḥ] Āṇi bāhyeṅdriyāṅche dheṅḍe | piṭūni vidhīcheni daṅḍe | nedije adharmākaḍe | kaṅhīṅchi jāvo || Jñāne.18.835 || To pai gā shamā virajā | dama guṇa jetha dujā | āṇi swadharmāchiyā vojā | jiṇe je kā || Jñāne.18.836 || [Tapaḥ] Tevīṅchi saṭavīchiye rātī | na visaṅbije jevi vātī | taisā īshwaranirṇaya chittī | vāhaṇe sadā || Jñāne.18.837 || Tayā nāma tapa | he tijayā guṇāche rūpa | [shauchaṁ] āṇi shauchahī niṣhpāpa | dwividha jetha || Jñāne.18.838 || Mana bhāvashuddhī bharale | āṅga kriyā aḷaṅkārile | aise sabāhya jiyāle | sājire je kā || Jñāne.18.839 || Tayā nāma shaucha Pārthā | to karmī guṇa jaye chauthā | [kṣhāntiḥ(hi)] āṇi pruthvīchiyā parī sarvathā | sarva je sāhāṇe || Jñāne.18.840 || Te gā kṣhamā Pāṅḍavā | guṇa jetha pāṅchavā | swarāmāji suhāvā | paṅchama jaisā || Jñāne.18.841 || [Ārjavameva cha] Āṇi vāṅkaḍeni vogheṁsī | Gaṅgā vāhe uĵūchi jaisī | kā pruṣhṭhī vaḷalā usī | goḍī jaisī || Jñāne.18.842 || Taisā viṣhamāṅhī jīvāṁ- | lāgī ujukāra baravā | te ārjava gā sāhāvā | jethīṅchā guṇa || Jñāne.18.843 || [Jñānaṁ] Āṇi pāṇiye prayatne māḷī | akhaṅḍa jache jhāḍāmuḷī | pari te āghaveṅchi phaḷī | ĵāṇe jevī || Jñāne.18.844 || Taise shāstrāchāre teṇe | īshwaracha yeka pāvaṇe | he phuḍe je kā ĵāṇaṇe | te yetha jñāna || Jñāne.18.845 || Te gā karmī jiye | sātavā guṇa hoye | [vijñānaṁ] āṇi vijñāna he pāhe | evaṁrūpa || Jñāne.18.846 || Tari sattwashuddhīchiye veḷe | shāstre kā dhyānabaḷe | īshwaratattwīṅchi miḷe | niṣhṭaṅkabuddhī || Jñāne.18.847 || He vijñāna barave | te guṇaratna jetha āṭhave | [āstikyaṁ] āṇi āstikya ĵāṇāve | navavā guṇa || Jñāne.18.848 || Pai rājamudrā āthiliyā | prajā bhaje bhalatayā | tevi shāstre swīkāriliyā | mārgamātrāte || Jñāne.18.849 || Ādare je kā mānaṇe | te āstikya mī mhaṇe | to navavā guṇa jeṇe | karma te sācha || Jñāne.18.850 || [Brahmakarma swabhāvajaṁ] Eva navahī shamādika | guṇa jetha nirdoṣha | te karma ĵāṇa swābhāvika | brāmhaṇāche || Jñāne.18.851 || To navaguṇaratnākara | yayā navaratnāṅchā hāra | na pheḍīta le dinakara | prakāsha jaisā || Jñāne.18.852 || Nā nā chāṅpā chāṁpauḷī pūjilā | chaṅdra chaṅdrikā dhavaḷalā | kā chaṅdana nije charchilā | saurabhye jevī || Jñāne.18.853 || Tevi navaguṇaṭikalaga | leṇe brāmhaṇāche avyaṅga | kaṅhīṅchi na saṅḍī āṅga | brāmhaṇāche || Jñāne.18.854 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā uchita te kṣhatriyā | teṅhī karma dhanaṅjayā | sāṅgo aika prajñechiyā | bharovarī || Jñāne.18.855 ||

Shauryaṁ(n) teĵo dhrutirdākṣhyaṁ yuddhe chāpyapalāyanam | dānamīshwarabhāvashcha kṣhātraṁ(ṅ) karma swabhāvajam || Bha.Gī.18.43 ||

[Shauryaṁ] Tari Bhānu hā teje | nāpekṣhī jevi viraje | kā siṅhe na pāhije | jāvaḷiyā || Jñāne.18.856 || Aisā swayaṅbha ĵo jīve lāṭha | sāvāyeṁvīṇa udbhaṭa | te shaurya gā jetha shreṣhṭha | pahilā guṇa || Jñāne.18.857 || [Tejaḥ] Āṇi sūryācheni pratāpe | koḍihī nakṣhatra hārape | nā to tari na lope | sachaṅdrī tihī || Jñāne.18.858 || Taise āpuleni prauḍhīguṇe | jagā yā vismaya deṇe | āpaṇa tarī na kṣhobhaṇe | kāyasenahī || Jñāne.18.859 || Te prāgalbhyarūpa tejā | jiye karmī guṇa dujā | [dhrutiḥ(hi)] āṇi dhīra to tijā | jethīṅchā guṇa || Jñāne.18.860 || Varipaḍaliyā ākāsha | buddhīche ḍoḷe mānasa | jhāṅkī nā te pariyesa | dhairya jethe || Jñāne.18.861 || [Dākṣhyaṁ] Āṇi pāṇī ho kā bhalatetuke | pari te jiṇauni padma phāṅke | kā ākāsha uṅchiyā jiṅke | āvaḍe tayāte || Jñāne.18.862 || Tevi vividhā avasthā | pātaliyā jiṇauni Pārthā | prajñā phaḷatayā arthā | vejha deṇe je || Jñāne.18.863 || Te dakṣhatwa gā chokha | jetha chauthā guṇa dekha | [yuddhe chāpyapalāyanaṁ] āṇi ĵuṅĵha alaukika | pāṅchavā guṇa || Jñāne.18.864 || Ādityāchī jhāḍe | sadā sanmukha sūryākaḍe | tevi samora shatrūpuḍhe | hoṇe je kā || Jñāne.18.865 || Māhevaṇī prayatneṁsī | chukavije seje jaisī | ripū pāṭhī nedije taisī | samaraṅgaṇī || Jñāne.18.866 || Hā kṣhatriyācheyā āchārī | pāṅchavā guṇeṅdra avadhārī | chahū puruṣhārthī shirī | bhakti jaisī || Jñāne.18.867 || [Dānaṁ] Āṇi ĵāleni phule phaḷe | shākhiyā jaisī mokaḷe | kā udāra parimaḷe | padmākara || Jñāne.18.868 || Nā nā āvaḍīcheni māpe | chāṅdiṇe bhalateṇe ghepe | puḍhilāṅcheni saṅkalpe | taise je deṇe || Jñāne.18.869 || Te umapa gā dāna | jetha sahāve guṇaratna | [īshwarabhāvashcha] āṇi ājñe ekāyatana | hoṇe je kā || Jñāne.18.870 || Poṣhūni avayava āpule | karavijatī mātavile | tevi pālaṇe lobhavile | jaga je bhogaṇe || Jñāne.18.871 || Tayā nāma īshwarabhāvo | ĵo sarvasāmarthyāĉhā ṭhāvo | to guṇāṁmāji rāvo | sātavā jetha || Jñāne.18.872 || [Kṣhātraṁ(ṅ) karma swabhāvajaṁ] Aise je shauryādikī | iṁhī sāta guṇavishekhī | aḷaṅkruta saptarhukhī | ākāsha jaise || Jñāne.18.873 || Taise saptaguṇī vichitra | karma je jagī pavitra | te sahaja ĵāṇa kṣhātra | kṣhatriyāche || Jñāne.18.874 || Nā nā kṣhatriya navhe naru | to sattwasonayāĉhā Meru | mhaṇauni guṇaswargā ādhāru | sātā yiyā || Jñāne.18.875 || Nātari saptaguṇārṇavī | parivāralī baravī | he kriyā navhe pruthvī | bhogītase to || Jñāne.18.876 || Kā guṇāṅche sātāṁhī oghī | he kriyā te Gaṅgā jagī | tayā mahodadhīchiyā āṅgī | vilase jaisī || Jñāne.18.77 || Pari he bahu aso dekha | shauryādi guṇātmaka | karma gā naisargika | kṣhatrajātīsī || Jñāne.18.878 || [Chūrṇikā] Ātā vaishyāchiye jātī | uchita je mahāmatī | te aike nirutī | kriyā sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.879 ||

Kruṣhigaurakṣhyavāṇijyaṁ vaishyakarma swabhāvajam | paricharyātmakaṁ(ṅ) karma shūdrasyāpi swabhāvajam || Bha.Gī.18.44 ||

[Kruṣhi-] Tari bhūmi bīja nāṅgara | yayā bhāṅḍavalāchā ādhāra | gheūni lābha apāra | meḷavaṇe je || Jñāne.18.880 || Kiṅbahunā kruṣhījiṇe | [gorakṣhya-] godhane rākhoni vartaṇe | [vāṇijyaṁ] kā samarghāchī vikaṇe | mahārgha vastu || Jñāne.18.881 || [Vaishyakarma swabhāvajam] Yetulālāchi Pāṅḍavā | vaishyāte karmāchā meḷāvā | hā vaishyajātiswabhāvā | āṅtulā ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.882 || [Paricharyeti] Āṇi vaishya kṣhatriya brāmhaṇa | he dwijanme tīnhī varṇa | yayāṅche je shushrūṣhaṇa | te shūdrakarma || Jñāne.18.883 || Pai dwijaseveparaute | dhāṅvaṇe nāhī shūdrāte | eva chaturvarṇochite | dāvilī karme || Jñāne.18.884 ||

Swe swe karmaṇyabhirataḥ(s) saṁsiddhiṁ labhate naraḥ | swakarmanirataḥ(s) siddhiṁ yathā vindati tachchhruṇu || Bha.Gī.18.45 ||

[Swe swe karmaṇi] Ātā iyechi vichakṣhaṇā | vegaḷāliyā varṇā | uchita jaise karaṇā | shabdādika || Jñāne.18.885 || Nātari jaḷadachyutā | pāṇiyā uchita saritā | saritesī pāṅḍusutā | siṅdhu uchita || Jñāne.18.886 || Taise varṇāshramavashe | je karaṇīya āle ase | goreyā āṅgā jaise | gorepaṇa || Jñāne.18.887 || [Abhirataḥ] Tayā swabhāvavihitā karmā | shāstrācheni mukhe vīrottamā | pravartāvayālāgī pramā | aḍhaḷa kīje || Jñāne.18.888 || Pai āpuleṅcha ratna thite | ghepe pārakhiyācheni hāte | taise swakarma āpaite | shāstre karāve || Jñāne.18.889 || Jaisī diṭhī ase āpuliyā ṭhāī | pari dīpeṁvīṇa bhoga nāhī | mārgu na lāhatā kāī | pāya asatā hoya || Jñāne.18.890 || Mhaṇauni jñātivashe sāchāra | sahaja ase ĵo adhikāra | to āpulāliyā shāstre gochara | āpaṇa kīje || Jñāne.18.891 || [Saṁsiddhiṁ labhate naraḥ] Maga gharīṅchāchi ṭhevā | jevi ḍoḷyā dāvī divā | tarī ghetā kāya Pāṅḍavā | āḍaḷa ase || Jñāne.18.892 || [Swakarmanirataḥ] Taise swabhāve bhāgā āle | varī shāstre khare kele | te vihita ĵo āpule | āchare gā || Jñāne.18.893 || Pari āḷasa sāṅḍunī | phaḷakāma davaḍunī | āṅge jīve māṅḍunī | tethechi bharu || Jñāne.18.894 || Voghī paḍile pāṇī | neṇe ānānī vāhaṇī | taisā ĵāya ācharaṇī | vyavasthaunī || Jñāne.18.895 || [Yathā] Arjunā ĵo yāparī | te vihita karma swaye karī | [siddhiṁ] to mokṣhāchyā ailatīrī | [vindati tachchhruṇu] paiṭhā hoya || Jñāne.18.896 || Je akaraṇā āṇi niṣhiddhā | na vachechi kāhī saṁbaṅdhā | mhaṇauni bhavā viruddhā | mukalā to || Jñāne.18.897 || Āṇi kāmyakarmākaḍe | na paratechi jetha koḍe | tetha chaṅdanāchehī khoḍe | na lechi to || Jñāne.18.898 || Yera nitya karma tava | phaḷatyāge veṅchile sarva | mhaṇauni mokṣhāchī shiṁva | ṭhākū lāhe || Jñāne.18.899 || Aiseni shubhāshubhī saṁsārī | sāṅḍilā to avadhārī | vairāgya mokṣhadwārī | ubhā ṭhāke || Jñāne.18.900 || Je sakaḷabhāgyāchī sīmā | mokṣhalābhāchī je pramā | nānā karmamārgashramā | shevaṭu jetha || Jñāne.18.901 || Mokṣhaphaḷe didhalī vola | je sukrutatarūche phūla | taye vairāgyī ṭhevī pāula | bhaṅvaru jaisā || Jñāne.18.902 || Pāhī ātmajñānasudināchā | vādhāvā sāṅgatayā aruṇāchā | udaya tyā vairāgyāĉhā | ṭhāvo pāve || Jñāne.18.903 || Kiṁbahunā ātmajñāna | jeṇe hātā ye nidhāna | te vairāgya divyāṅjana | jīve le to || Jñāne.18.904 || Aisī mokṣhāchī yogyatā | siddhī ĵāya tayā Paṅḍusutā | anusaroni vihitā | karmā yayā || Jñāne.18.905 || [Chūrṇikā] He vihita karma Pāṅḍavā | āpulā ananya volāvā | āṇī hechi parama sevā | maĵa sarvātmakāchī || Jñāne.18.906 || Pai āghavāṅchi bhogeṁsī | pativratā krīḍe priyeṁsī | kī tayāchi nāme jaisī | tape tiyā kelī || Jñāne.18.907 || Kā bāḷakā ekī māye- | vāṅchoni jiṇe kāya āhe | mhaṇauni sevije kī to hoye | pāṭāchā dharma || Jñāne.18.908 || Nā nā pāṇī mhaṇauni māsā | Gaṅgā na sāṅḍitā jaisā | sarvatīrtha sahavāsā | varapaḍā jālā || Jñāne.18.909 || Taise āpaliyā vihitā | upāya ase na visaṁbatā | aisā kīje kī jagannāthā | ābhāra paḍe || Jñāne.18.910 || Agā jayāche vihita | te īshwarāche manogata | mhaṇauni keliyā nibhrāṅta | sāṅpaḍechi to || Jñāne.18.911 || Pai jīvāche kasī utaralī | te dāsī kī gosāvīṇa jālī | taisī sevechī tayā mavalī | vahi jevī || Jñāne.18.912 || Taise swāmīchiyā manobhāvā | na chukije hechi paramasevā | yera te gā Pāṅḍavā | vāṇijya karaṇe || Jñāne.18.913 ||

Yataḥ(ph) pravruttirbhūtānāṁ yena sarvamidaṁ(n) tatam | swakarmaṇā tamabhyarchya siddhiṁ vindati mānavaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.46 ||

[Yataḥ(ph) pravruttirbhūtānāṁ] Mhaṇauni vihita kriyā kelī | navhe tayāchī khūṇa pāḷilī | jayāpāsūni kā ālī | ākārā bhūte || Jñāne.18.914 || Ĵo avidyechiyā chiṅdhiyā | guṅḍūni jīva bāhuliyā | kheḷavītase tiguṇiyā | ahaṅkārarajjū || Jñāne.18.915 || [Yena sarvamidaṁ(n) tatam] Jeṇe jaga he samasta | āṅta bāherī pūrṇa bharita | ĵāle āhe dīpajāta | teje jaise || Jñāne.18.916 || [Swakarmaṇā tamabhyarchya] Tayā sarvātmakā īshwarā | swakarmakusumāṅchī vīrā | pūjā kelī hoya apārā | toṣhālāgī || Jñāne.18.917 || Mhaṇauni tiye pūje | rijhaleni ātmarāje | vairāgyasiddhī deyije | pasāya tayā || Jñāne.18.918 || [Siddhiṁ vindati mānavaḥ] Jiye vairāgyadashe | īshwarācheni vedhavashe | he sarvahī nāvaḍe jaise | vāṅta hota || Jñāne.18.919 || Prāṇanāthāchiyā ādhī | virahiṇīte jiṇeṁhī bādhī | taise sukhajāta trishuddhī | duḥkhachi lāge || Jñāne.18.920 || Samyakjñāna nudaijatā | vedhechi tanmayatā | upaĵe aisī yogyatā | bodhāchī lāhe || Jñāne.18.921 || [Chūrṇikā] Mhaṇauni mokṣhalābhālāgī | ĵo vrate vāhatase āṅgī | teṇe swadharma āsthā chāṅgī | anuṣhṭhāvā || Jñāne.18.922 ||

Shreyānswadharmo viguṇaḥ(ph) paradharmātswanuṣhṭhitāt | swabhāvaniyataṁ(ṅ) karma kurvannāpnoti kilbiṣham || Bha.Gī.18.47 ||

[Shreyānswadharmaḥ] Agā āpalā hā swadharma | ācharaṇī ĵarī viṣhama | tarī pāhāvā to pariṇāma | phaḷela jeṇe || Jñāne.18.923 || [Viguṇaḥ] Jai sukhālāgī āpaṇapayā | niṁbachi āthī dhanaṅjayā | tai kaḍuvaṭapaṇā tayāchiyā | ubagije nā || Jñāne.18.924 || Phaḷaṇayā ailīkaḍe | keḷīte pāhatā āsa moḍe | aisī tyajilī tarī ĵoḍe | taise ke gomaṭe || Jñāne.18.925 || Tevi swadharma sāṅkaḍu | dekhoni kelā ĵarī kaḍu | tari mokṣha suravāḍu | aṅtaralā kī || Jñāne.18.926 || Āṇi āpalī māye | kubja ĵarī āhe | tarī jiyete nohe | sneha kurhe kī || Jñāne.18.927 || [Paradharmātswanuṣhṭhitāt] Yerī jiyā parāviyā | raṁbhehūni baraviyā | tiyā kāya karāviyā | bālake teṇe || Jñāne.18.928 || Agā pāṇiyāhūni barave | tupī guṇa kīra āhe | pari mīnā kāya hoye | asaṇe tetha || Jñāne.18.929 || Pai āghaviyā jagā je vikha | te vikhakīḍiyā pīyūkha | āṇi jagā guḷa te dekha | maraṇa de tayā || Jñāne.18.930 || [Swabhāveti] Mhaṇauni je vihita jayā jeṇe | phiṭe saṅsārāche dharaṇe | kriyā kaṭhora jarhī teṇe | techi karāvī || Jñāne.18.931 || Yerā parāchārā baraviyā | aise hoīla ṭeṅkaleyā | pāyāṅche chālaṇe ḍoiyā | kele jaise || Jñāne.18.932 || Yālāgī karma āpale | je jātiswabhāve ase āle | te karī teṇe jiṅtile | karmabaṅdhāte || Jñāne.18.933 || [Chūrṇikā] Āṇi swadharmachi pāḷāvā | paradharma to gāḷāvā | hā nemahī Pāṅḍavā | na kījechi pai || Jñāne.18.934 || Tarī ātmā druṣhṭa nohe | tava karma karaṇe kā ṭhāye | āṇi karaṇe tetha āhe | āyāsa ādhī || Jñāne.18.935 ||

Sahajaṁ(ṅ) karma Kaunteya sadoṣhamapi na tyajet | sarvārambhā hi doṣheṇa dhūmenāgnirivāvrutāḥ(hā) || Bha.Gī.18.48 ||

[Sarvārambhā hi doṣheṇa] Mhaṇauni bhalatiye karmī | āyāsa jarhī upakramī | tarī kāya swadharmī | doṣha sāṅge || Jñāne.18.936 || Agā ujū vāṭā chālāve | tarhī pāyachi shiṇavāve | nā āḍarāne dhāṁvāve | tarhī teṅchī || Jñāne.18.937 || Pai shiḷā kā sidoriyā | dāṭaṇe eka dhanaṅjayā | pari je vāhatā visāvayā | miḷije te ghepe || Jñāne.18.938 || Yerhavī kaṇā āṇi bhūsā | kāṅḍitāṁhī sosa sarisā | jeṅchi raṅdhana shwānamāṁsā | techi havī || Jñāne.18.939 || Dadhī jaḷāchiyā ghusaḷaṇā | vyāpāra sārikhechi vichakṣhaṇā | vāḷuve tiḷā ghāṇā | gāḷaṇe eka || Jñāne.18.940 || [Dhūmenāgnirivāvrutāḥ(hā)] Pai nityahoma deyāvayā | kā sairā āgī suvāvayā | phuṅkitā dhūma dhanaṅjayā | sāhaṇe techi || Jñāne.18.941 || [Sadoṣhamapi] Parī dharmapatnī dhāṅgaḍī | positā ĵarī ekī voḍhī | tari kā aparavaḍī | āṇāvī āṅgā || Jñāne.18.942 || Hā gā pāṭhī lāgalā ghāī | maraṇa na chukechi pāhī | tari samoralā kāī | āgaḷe na kīje || Jñāne.18.943 || Kuḷastrī dāṅḍayāche ghāye | paraghara rigālīhī jari sāhe | tari swapatīte vāṁye | tyajile kī || Jñāne.18.944 || Taise āvaḍateṅhī karaṇe | na nipaje shiṇalyāviṇe | tari vihita bā re koṇe | bole bhārī || Jñāne.18.945 || Tari thoḍeṅchi amruta ghetā | sarvaswa veṅcho kā Paṅḍusutā | jeṇe ĵoḍe jīvitā | akṣhayatwa || Jñāne.18.946 || Yera kāṁhyā mole veṅchunī | viṣha piyāve gheunī | ātmahatyesi nimonī | jāyije jeṇe || Jñāne.18.947 || Taise jāchūniyā iṅdriye | veṅchūni āyuṣhyācheni diye | sāṅchale pāpī āna āhe | duḥkhāvāṅchūni || Jñāne.18.948 || [Sahajaṁ(ṅ) karma Kaunteya] Mhaṇoni karāvā swadharma | ĵo karitā hironi ghe shrama | uchita deīla parama | puruṣhārtharāja || Jñāne.18.949 || [Na tyajet] Yākāraṇe kirīṭī | swadharmāchiye rāhaṭī | na visaṁbije saṅkaṭī | siddhamaṅtra jaisā || Jñāne.18.950 || Kā nāva jaisī udadhī | mahārogī divyauṣhadhī | na visaṅbije tayā buddhī | swakarma yetha || Jñāne.18.951 || [Chūrṇikā] Maga yayāchi gā kapidhwajā | swakarmāchiyā mahāpūjā | toṣhalā īsha tama rajā | jhāḍā karūni || Jñāne.18.952 || Shuddha sattwāchiyā vāṭā | āṇi āpulī utkaṅṭhā | bhava swarga kāḷakūṭā- | aise dāvī || Jñāne.18.953 || Jiye vairāgya yeṇe bole | māgā saṁsiddhi rūpa kele | kiṅbahunā te āpule | meḷavī khāge || Jñāne.18.954 || Maga jiṅtiliyā he bhoye | puruṣha sarvatra jaisā hoye | kā jālāhī je lāhe | te ātā sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.955 || [Pañchamādhyāyoktaṁ saṁ(n)nyāsayogamāha tribhiḥ(hi)]

Asaktabuddhiḥ(s) sarvatra jitātmā vigataspruhaḥ | naiṣhkarmyasiddhiṁ paramāṁ saṁ(n)nyāsenādhigachchhati || Bha.Gī.18.49 ||

[Asaktabuddhiḥ(s) sarvatra] Tari dehādika he saṁsāre | sarvahī māṅḍaleṅse je guṁphire | tetha nātuḍe to vāgure | vārā jaisā || Jñāne.18.956 || Pai paripākāchiye veḷe | phaḷa deṭhe nā deṭha phaḷe | na dhare taise sneha khuḷe | sarvatra hoya || Jñāne.18.957 || Putra vitta kalatra | he jāliyāhī swataṅtra | māĵhe na mhaṇe pātra | viṣhāche jaise || Jñāne.18.958 || [Jitātmā] He aso viṣhayajātī | buddhi poḷalī aisī māghautī | pāule gheūni ekāṅtī | hrudayāchyā righe || Jñāne.18.959 || Aisayā aṅtaḥkaraṇa | bāhya yetā tayāchī āṇa | na moḍī samarthā bheṇa | dāsī jaisī || Jñāne.18.960 || Taise aikyāchiye muṭhī | mājivaḍe chitta kirīṭī | karūni vedhī nehaṭī | ātmayāchyā || Jñāne.18.961 || [Vigataspruhaḥ] Tevhā druṣhṭādruṣhṭa spruhe | nimaṇe ĵāleṅchi āhe | āgī daḍapaliyā dhuye | rāhije jaise || Jñāne.18.962 || Mhaṇauni niyamiliyā mānasī | spruhā nāsoni ĵāya āpaisī | kiṅbahunā to aisī | bhūmikā pāve || Jñāne.18.963 || [Naiṣhkarmyasiddhiṁ paramāṁ] Pai anyathābodha āghavā | māvaḷoni tayā Pāṅḍavā | bodhamātrīṅchi jivā | ṭhāva hoya || Jñāne.18.964 || Dharavaṇī veṅche sare | taise bhoge prāchīna pure | nave tava nupakare | kāhīṅchi karū || Jñāne.18.965 || Aishī karme sāmya dashā | hoya tetha vīreshā | maga Shreeguru āpaisā | bheṭechi gā || Jñāne.18.966 || Rātrīchī chaupāharī | veṅchaliyā avadhārī | ḍoḷayā tamārī | miḷe jaisā || Jñāne.18.967 || Kā yeūni phaḷāchā ghaḍa | pāruṣhavī keḷīchī vāḍha | Shreegurū bheṭoni karī pāḍa | mumukṣhū taisā || Jñāne.18.968 || Maga āliṅgilā pūrṇimā | jaisā uṇīva sāṅḍī chaṅdramā | taise hoya vīrottamā | gurukrupā tayā || Jñāne.18.969 || Tevhā abodhamātra ase | to tava tayā krupā nāshe | tetha nishisave jaise | āṅdhāre ĵāya || Jñāne.18.970 || Taisī abodhāchiye kushī | karma kartā kārya aishī | tripuṭī ase te jaisī | gābhiṇī mārilī || Jñāne.18.971 || [Saṁ(n)nyāsenādhigachchhati] Taiseṅchi abodhanāshāsave | nāshe kriyājāta āghave | aisā samūḷa saṁbhave | saṅnyāsa hā || Jñāne.18.972 || Yeṇe mūḷājñānasaṅnyāse | drushyāĉhā jetha ṭhāvo puse | tetha bujhāve te āpaise | tochi āhe || Jñāne.18.973 || Cheiliyāvari pāhī | swapnīṅchiyā tiye ḍohī | āpaṇayāte kāī | kāḍhū jāije || Jñāne.18.974 || Tai mī neṇe ātā ĵāṇena | he sarale tayā duḥswapna | jālā jñātrujñeyāvihīna | chidākāra || Jñāne.18.975 || Mukhābhāseṁsī ārisā | paratā neliyā vīreshā | pahātepaṇeṅvīṇa jaisā | pāhatā ṭhāke || Jñāne.18.976 || Taise neṇaṇe je gele | teṇe ĵāṇaṇeṅhī nele | maga niṣhkriya urale | chinmātrachi || Jñāne.18.977 || Tetha swabhāve dhanaṅjayā | nāhī koṇīchi kriyā | mhaṇauni pravāda tayā | naiṣhkarmya aisā || Jñāne.18.978 || Te āpule āpaṇape | asatachi hoūni hārape | taraṅga kā vāyulope | samudra jaisā || Jñāne.18.979 || [Paramāṁ] Taise na hoṇe nipaje | te naiṣhkarmyasiddhi jāṇije | sarvasiddhīṅta sahaĵe | parama hechī || Jñāne.18.980 || Deuḷāchiyā kāmā kaḷasa | parama gaṅgesī siṅdhupravesha | kā suvarṇashuddhī kasa | soḷāvā jaisā || Jñāne.18.981 || Taise āpule neṇaṇe | pheḍije kā ĵāṇaṇe | teṅhi giḷūni asaṇe | aishī je dashā || Jñāne.18.982 || Tiyeparate kāhī | nipajaṇe yetha nāhī | mhaṇauni mhaṇipe pāhī | paramasiddhi te || Jñāne.18.983 || [Chūrṇikā] Pari hechi ātmasiddhi | ĵo koṇī bhāgyanidhi | Shreegurukrupālabdhi- | kāḷī pāve || Jñāne.18.984 ||

Siddhiṁ prāpto yathā brahma tathāpnoti nibodha me | samāsenaiva Kaunteya niṣhṭhā jñānasya yā parā || Bha.Gī.18.50 ||

[Niṣhṭhā jñānasya yā parā] Udayajatā dinakara | prakāshachi āte āṅdhāra | kā dīpasaṅge karpūra | dīpachi hoya || Jñāne.18.985 || Tayā lavaṇāchī kaṇikā | miḷatakheṁvo udakā | udakachi hoūni dekhā | ṭhāke jevī || Jñāne.18.986 || Kā nidrita chevaviliyā | swapneṅsī nīda vāyā | jāūni āpaṇapayā | miḷe jaisā || Jñāne.18.987 || Taise jayā koṇhāsi daive | guruvākya shravaṇāchisave | dwaita giḷoni visaṁve | āpaṇayā vruttī || Jñāne.18.988 || Tayāsī maga karma karaṇe | he bolijelachi kavaṇe | ākāshā yeṇe ĵāṇe | āhe kāī || Jñāne.18.989 || Mhaṇauni tayāsi kāhī | trishuddhi karaṇe nāhī | pari aise jari he kāhī | navhe jayā || Jñāne.18.990 || Kānā vachanāchiye bheṭī- | sarisāchi pai kirīṭī | vastu hoūni uṭhī | kavaṇi eka ĵo || Jñāne.18.991 || Yerhavī swakarmācheni vahnī | kāmyaniṣhiddhāchiyā iṅdhanī | raja tama kīra donhī | jāḷilī ādhī || Jñāne.18.992 || Putra vitta para loka | yayā tihīṅchā abhilākha | gharī hoi pāika | heṅhī ĵāle || Jñāne.18.993 || Iṅdriye sairā padārthī | rigatā viṭāḷalī hotī | tiye pratyāhāratīrthī | nhāṇilī kīra || Jñāne.18.994 || Āṇi swadharmāche phaḷa | īshwarī arpūni sakaḷa | gheūni kele aḍhaḷa | vairāgyapada || Jñāne.18.995 || Aisī ātmasākṣhātkārī | lābhe jñānāchī uĵarī | te sāmagrī kīra purī | meḷavilī || Jñāne.18.996 || [Siddhiṁ prāptaḥ] Āṇi techi samayī | sadgurū bheṭale pāhī | tevīṅchi tihī kāhī | vaṅchijenā || Jñāne.18.997 || [Tathā] Pari vokhada ghetakheṁvo | kāya lābhe āpalā ṭhāvo | kā udayajatāṅchi divo | madhyāhna hoya || Jñāne.18.998 || Sukṣhetrī āṇi volaṭe | bījahi perile gomaṭe | tari āloṭa phaḷa bheṭe | pari veḷe kī gā || Jñāne.18.999 || Ĵoḍalā mārga prāṅjaḷa | minalā susaṅgāchāhī meḷa | tari pāvije vāṅchūni veḷa | lāgechi kī || Jñāne.18.1000 || Taisā vairāgyalābha jālā | vari sadgurūhī bheṭalā | jīvī aṅkura phuṭalā | vivekāchā || Jñāne.18.1001 || Teṇe brahma eka āthi | yera āghavīchi bhrāṅti | heṅhī kīra pratīti | gāḍha kelī || Jñāne.18.1002 || [Brahma] Pari techi je parabrahma | sarvātmaka sarvottama | mokṣhācheṅhī kāma | sare jetha || Jñāne.18.1003 || Yayā tinhī avasthā poṭī | jiravī je gā kirīṭī | tayā jñānāsihī miṭhī | de je vastu || Jñāne.18.1004 || Aikyāche ekapaṇa sare | jetha ānaṅdakaṇahī vire | kāhīṅchi nuroni ure | je kāhī gā || Jñāne.18.1005 || [Āpnoti] Tiye brahmī aikyapaṇe | brahmachi hoūni asaṇe | te krameṅchi karūni teṇe | pāvije pai || Jñāne.18.1006 || Bhukeliyāpāsī | vogarile ṣhaḍrasī | to truptī pratigrasī | lāhe jevī || Jñāne.18.1007 || Taisā vairāgyāĉhā volāvā | vivekāchā to divā | āṁbuthitā ātmaṭhevā | kāḍhīchi to || Jñāne.18.1008 || Tarī bhogije ātmarhuddhī | yevaḍhī yogyatechī siddhī | jayāchyā āṅgī niravadhī | leṇe jālī || Jñāne.18.1009 || [Tathā] To jeṇe krame brahma | [samāsenaiva] hoṇe karī gā sugama | [nibodha me] tayā kramāche ātā varma | āīka sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.1010 ||

Buddhyā vishuddhayā yukto dhrutyātmānaṁ(n) niyamya cha | shabdādīnviṣhayāṁstyaktwā rāgadweṣhau vyudasya cha || Bha.Gī.18.51 ||

[Buddhyā vishuddhayā] Tarī gurū dāviliyā vāṭā | yeūni vivekatīrthataṭā | dhuūniyā maḷavaṭā | buddhīchā teṇe || Jñāne.18.1011 || [Yuktaḥ] Maga rāhūne ugaḷilī | prabhā chaṅdre āliṅgilī | taisī shuddhatwe jaḍalī | āpaṇayā buddhi || Jñāne.18.1012 || Sāṅḍūni kuḷe donhī | priyāsī anusare kāminī | dwaṅdwatyāge swachiṅtanī | paḍalī taisī || Jñāne.18.1013 || [Shabdādīnviṣhayāṁstyaktwā] Āṇi jñānāaise jivhāra | nevo nevo niraṅtara | iṅdriyī kele thora | shabdādika je || Jñāne.18.1014 || Te rashmijāḷa kāḍhaleyā | mrugajaḷa ĵāya layā | taise vruttirodhe tayā | pāṅchāṅhī kele || Jñāne.18.1015 || Neṇatā adhamāchiyā annā | khādaliyā kīje vamanā | taisī vokavilī savāsanā | iṅdriye viṣhayī || Jñāne.18.1016 || [Dhrutyātmānaṁ(n) niyamya cha] Maga pratyagāvruttī chokhaṭe | lāvilī gaṅgecheni taṭe | aisī prāyashchitte dhuvaṭe | kelī yeṇe || Jñāne.18.1017 || Pāṭhī sāttwike dhīre teṇe | shodhāralī tiye karaṇe | maga maneṁsī yogadhāraṇe | meḷavilī || Jñāne.18.1018 || [Rāgadweṣhau vyudasya cha] Teviṅchi prāchīne iṣhṭāniṣhṭe | bhogeṁsī yeunī bheṭe | tetha dekhiliyāhī vokhaṭe | dweṣha na karī || Jñāne.18.1019 || Nā gomaṭeṅchi vipāye | te āṇūni puḍhā sūye | tayālāgī na hoye | sābhilāṣha || Jñāne.18.1020 || [Chūrṇikā] Yāpari iṣhṭāniṣhṭī | rāgadweṣha kirīṭī | tyajūni girikapāṭī | nikuṅjī vase || Jñāne.18.1021 ||

Viviktasevī laghvāshī yatavākkāyamānasaḥ | dhyānayogaparo nityaṁ vairāgyaṁ samupāshritaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.52 ||

[Viviktasevī] Gajabajā sāṅḍiliyā | vasavī vanasthaḷiyā | aṅgāchiyā māṅdiyā | ekaleyā || Jñāne.18.1022 || Shamadamādikī kheḷe | na bolaṇeṅchi chāvaḷe | guruvākyācheni meḷe | neṇe veḷa || Jñāne.18.1023 || [Laghvāshī] Āṇi āṅgā baḷa yāve | nātarī kṣhudhā jāve | kā jibheche purāve | manoratha || Jñāne.18.1024 || Bhojana karitāṁvikhī | yayā tihīṅte na lekhī | āhārī mitī saṅtoṣhī | māpa na sūye || Jñāne.18.1025 || Anashanācheni pāvake | hārapatī prāṇa pokhe | itukiyāchi bhāga moṭake | ashana karī || Jñāne.18.1026 || [Yatavākkāyamānasaḥ] Āṇi parapuruṣhe kāmilī | kuḷavadhū āṅga na ghālī | nidrālasyā na mokalī | ashana taise || Jñāne.18.1027 || Daṅḍavatācheni prasaṅge | bhuyī hana aṅga lāge | vāṅchūni yera neghe | rābhasya tetha || Jñāne.18.1028 || Dehanirvāhāpurate | rāhāṭavī hātāṁpāyāte | kiṁbahunā āpaite | sabāhya kele || Jñāne.18.1029 || Āṇi manāchā uṁbarā | vruttīsī dekho nedī vīrā | tetha ke vāgvyāpārā | avakāsha ase || Jñāne.18.1030 || Aiseni deha vāchā mānasa | he jiṇoni bāhyapradesha | [dhyāna-] ākaḷile ākāsha | dhyānāche teṇe || Jñāne.18.1031 || Guruvākye uṭhavilā | bodhī nishchaya āpalā | nyāhāḷī hātī ghetalā | ārisā jaisā || Jñāne.18.1032 || Pai dhyātā Jñāne.18.1034 || Mhaṇauni to mumukṣhu | ātmajñānī jālā dakṣhu | [yogaparo nityaṁ] pari puḍhā sūni pakṣhu | yogābhyāsāchā || Jñāne.18.1035 || Apānaraṅdhradwayā- | māĵhārī dhanaṅjayā | pārṣhṇī piḍūniyā | kāṁvarumūḷa || Jñāne.18.1036 || Ākuṅchūni adha | deūni tinhī baṅdha | karūni ekavada | vāyubhedā || Jñāne.18.1037 || Kuṅḍalinī jāgaūni | madhyamā vikāshūni | ādhārādi bhedūni | agnivarī || Jñāne.18.1038 || Sahasradaḷāṅchā megha | pīyūṣhe varṣhoni chāṅga | to mūḷavarī vogha | āṇūniyā || Jñāne.18.1039 || Nāchatayā puṇyagirī | chidbhairavāchyā khāparī | manapavanāchī khīcha purī | vāḍhūniyā || Jñāne.18.1040 || Jāliyā yogāchā gāḍhā | meḷāvā sūni hā puḍhā | dhyāna māgilīkaḍā | swayaṅbha kele || Jñāne.18.1041 || [Vairāgyamiti pañchadashādhyāyoktamasaṅggashastramāha] Āṇi dhyāna Pahāve dise tavavarī | diṭhīte na saṅḍī dīpa ĵarī | tarī ke avasarī | dekhāvayā || Jñāne.18.1044 || Taise mokṣhī pravartaliyā | vruttī brahmī ĵāya layā | tava vairāgya āthī tayā | bhaṅga kaiṅchā || Jñāne.18.1045 || Mhaṇauni savairāgya | jñānābhyāsa to sabhāgya | karūni jālā yogya | ātmalābhā || Jñāne.18.1046 || Aisī vairāgyāchī āṅgī | bāṇūniyā vajrāṅgī | rājayogaturaṅgī | ārūḍhalā || Jñāne.18.1047 || Varī āḍa paḍile diṭhī | sāne thora nivaṭī | te baḷī vivekamuṣhṭī | dhyānāche khāṅḍe || Jñāne.18.1048 || Aiseni saṁsāraraṇāāṅta | āṅdhārī sūrya taisā ase jāta | mokṣha vijayashriye varaita | hoāvayālāgī || Jñāne.18.1049 || [Ṣhoḍashādhyāyoktamajñānavargaṁ(n) darshayati]

Ahaṅgkāraṁ balaṁ(n) darpaṁ(ṅ) kāmaṁ(ṅ) krodhaṁ parigraham | vimuchya nirmamaḥ(sh) shānto brahmabhūyāya kalpate || Bha.Gī.18.53 ||

[Ahaṅgkāraṁ] Tetha āḍavāvayā āle | doṣhavairī je dhopaṭile | tayāmājī pahile | dehāhaṅkāra || Jñāne.18.1050 || Ĵo na mokalī mārūni | jīvo nedī upajavonī | vichaṅbavī khoḍā ghālūnī | hāḍāṅchiyā || Jñāne.18.1051 || Tayāĉhā dehadurga hā thārā | moḍoni ghetalā to vīrā | [balaṁ] āṇi baḷa hā dusarā | mārilā vairī || Jñāne.18.1052 || Ĵo viṣhayāṅcheni nāve | chauguṇeṁhī varī thāṁve | jeṇe mrutāvasthā kāma koṇecha ṭhāyī | nase aise kele pāhī | [krodhaṁ] kī techi krodhāhī | sahaĵe āle || Jñāne.18.1059 || Muḷāche toḍaṇe jaise | hoya kā shākhoddeshe | kāma nāshaleni nāshe | taisā krodha || Jñāne.18.1060 || Mhaṇauni kāma vairī | jālā jetha ṭhāṇorī | tetha saralī vārī | krodhāchīhī || Jñāne.18.1061 || [Parigrahaṁ] Āṇi samartha āpulā khoḍā | shise vāhavī jaisā hoḍā | taisā bhuṅjauni ĵo gāḍhā | parigraho || Jñāne.18.1062 || Ĵo māthāṅchi pālāṇavī | aṅgā avaguṇa ghālavī | jīve dāṅḍī ghevavī | mamatwāchī || Jñāne.18.1063 || Shiṣhyashāstrādivilāse | maṭhādi mudrecheni mise | ghātale āhātī phāṁse | niḥsaṅgā jeṇe || Jñāne.18.1064 || Gharī kuṭuṁbapaṇe sare | tarī vanī vanya hoūni avatare | nāgavīyāhī sharīre | lāgalā āhe || Jñāne.18.1065 || [Vimuchya] Aisā durjaya ĵo parigraho | tayāĉhā pheḍūni ṭhāvo | bhavavijayāĉhā utsāho | bhogītase ĵo || Jñāne.18.1066 || [Trayodashādhyāyoktānyamānitwādilakṣhaṇāni darshayati] [nirmamaḥ] tetha amānitwādi āghave | jñānaguṇāche je meḷāve | te kaivalyadeshīṅche āghave | rāva jaise āle || Jñāne.18.1067 || Tevhā samyak-jñānāchiyā | rāṇivā ugāṇūni tayā | parivāra hoūniyā | rāhata āṅge || Jñāne.18.1068 || Pravruttīchiye rājabidī | avasthābhedapramadī | kījata āhe pratipadī | sukhāche loṇa || Jñāne.18.1069 || Puḍhā bodhāchiye kāṁbīvarī | viveka drushyāchī māṅdī sārī | yogabhūmikā āratī karī | yetī jaisiyā || Jñāne.18.1070 || Tetha rhuddhisiddhīṅchī anege | vruṅde miḷatī prasaṅge | tiye puṣhpavarṣhī āṅge | nāhātase to || Jñāne.18.1071 || Aiseni brahmaikyāsārikhe | swarājya yetā javaḷike | jhaḷaṁbita āhe harikhe | tinhī loka || Jñāne.18.1072 || Tevhā vairiyā kā maitriyā | tayāsi māĵhe mhaṇāvayā | samānatā dhanaṅjayā | urechihī nā || Jñāne.18.1073 || He nā bhalateṇe vyāĵe | to jayāte mhaṇe māĵhe | te noḍavechi kā duje | adwitīya jālā || Jñāne.18.1074 || Pai āpuliyā ekī sattā | sarvahī kavaḷūniyā Paṅḍusutā | kaṅhī na lagatī mamatā | dhāḍilī teṇe || Jñāne.18.1075 || [Shāntaḥ] Aisā jiṅtiliyā ripuvarga | apamāniliyā he jaga | apaisā yogaturaṅga | sthira jālā || Jñāne.18.1076 || Vairāgyāche gāḍhale | aṅgatrāṇa hote bhale | teṅhī nāveka ḍhile | tevhā karī || Jñāne.18.1077 || Āṇi nivaṭī dhyānāche khāṅḍe | te duje nāhīṅchi puḍhe | mhaṇūna hāta āsuḍe | vruttīchāhī || Jñāne.18.1078 || Jaise rasauṣhadha khare | āpule kāĵa karūni pure | āpaṇahī nure | taise hotase || Jñāne.18.1079 || Dekhoni ṭhākitāṭhāvo | dhāṅvatā
