|| Te shāṅti pai gā subhagā | saṁpūrṇa ye tayāchiyā āṅgā | [brahmabhūyāya kalpate] tai brahma hoāvayāĵogā | hoya to puruṣha || Jñāne.18.1086 || Punavehuni chaturdashī | jetule uṇepaṇa shashī | kā soḷeyā ūni jaisī | paṅdharāvī vānī || Jñāne.18.1087 || Sāgarīṁhī pāṇī vege | saṅchare te rūpa gaṅge | yera nishchaḷa je uge | te samudra jaisā || Jñāne.18.1088 || Brahmā āṇi brahmahotiye | yogyate taisā pāḍa āhe | techi shāṅtīcheni lāhe | hāte to gā || Jñāne.18.1089 || Pai techi hoṇenavīṇa | pratītī āle je brahmapaṇa | te brahma hotī ĵāṇa | yogyatā yetha || Jñāne.18.1090 || [Pañchadashokta-puuruṣhottamayogamāha] -

Brahmabhūtaḥ prasannātmā na shochati na kāṅgkṣhati | samaḥ sarveṣhu bhūteṣhu madbhakti labhate parām || Bha.Gī.18.54 ||

[Brahmabhūtaḥ(ph) prasannātmā] Te brahmabhāvayogyatā | puruṣha to maga Paṅḍusutā | ātmabodha prasannatā- | padī baise || Jñāne.18.1091 || Jeṇe nipaje rasasoya | to tāpahī jai ĵāya | tai te kā hoye | prasanna jaisī || Jñāne.18.1092 || Nā nā bharatiyā lagabagā | sharatkāḷī sāṅḍije Gaṅgā | kā gīta rāhatā upāṅgā | vohaṭa paḍe || Jñāne.18.1093 || Taisā ātmabodhī udyama | karitā hoya ĵo shrama | tohī jethe shama | hoūni ĵāya || Jñāne.18.1094 || Ātmabodhaprashastī | he tiye dashechī khyātī | te bhogītase mahāmatī | yogya to gā || Jñāne.18.1095 || [Na shochati na kāṅgkṣhati] Tevhā ātmatwe shochāve | kāhī pāvāvayā kāmāve | he sarale samabhāve | bharite tayā || Jñāne.18.1096 || [Samaḥ(s) sarveṣhu bhūteṣhu] Udayā yetā gabhastī | nānā nakṣhatravyaktī | hāravījatī dīptī | āṅgikā jevī || Jñāne.18.1097 || Tevī uṭhatiyā ātmaprathā | he bhūtabhedavyavasthā | moḍīta moḍīta Pārthā | vāsa pāhe to || Jñāne.18.1098 || Pāṭiyevarīla akṣhare | jaisī pusatā yetī kare | taisī hārapatī bhedāṅtare | tayāchiye druṣhṭī || Jñāne.18.1099 || Taiseni anyathājñāne | jiye ghepatī jāgaraswapne | tiye donhī kelī līne | avyaktāmājī || Jñāne.18.1100 || Maga teṁhī avyakta | bodha vāḍhatā jhijata | puralā bodhī samasta | buḍoni ĵāya || Jñāne.18.1101 || Jaisī bhojanāchyā vyāpārī | kṣhudhā jirata ĵāya avadhārī | maga truptīchyā avasarī | nāhīṅcha hoya || Jñāne.18.1102 || Nā nā chālīchiyā vāḍhī | vāṭa hota ĵāya thoḍī | maga pātalāṭhāyī buḍī | deūni nime || Jñāne.18.1103 || Kā jāgrutī ĵava uddīpe | tava tava nidrā hārape | maga jāgīnaliyā swarūpe | nāhīṅcha hoya || Jñāne.18.1104 || He nā āpule pūrṇatwa bheṭe | jetha chaṅdrāsī vāḍhī khuṅṭe | tetha shuklapakṣha āṭe | niḥsheṣha jaisā || Jñāne.18.1105 || Taisā bodhyajāta giḷita | bodhabodhe ye majaāṅta | misaḷalā tetha sādyaṅta | abodha gelā || Jñāne.18.1106 || [Madbhaktiṁ] Tevhā kalpāṅtāchiye veḷe | nadī-siṅdhūṅche peṅḍavaḷe | moḍuni bharile jaḷe | ābrahma jaise || Jñāne.18.1107 || Nā nā geliyā ghaṭa maṭha | ākāsha ṭhāke ekavaṭa | kā ĵaḷoni kāṣhṭhe kāṣhṭha | vahnīchi hoya || Jñāne.18.1108 || Nā tari leṇiyāche ṭhase | āṭoni geliyā muse | nāmarūpabhede jaise | sāṅḍije sone || Jñāne.18.1109 || Heṁhī aso cheilayā | he swapna nāhī jālayā | maga āpaṇachi āpaṇayā | urije jaise || Jñāne.18.1110 || [Labhate parāṁ] Taisā mī ekavāṅchūni kāhī | tayā tayāhīsakaṭa nāhī | he chauthī bhakti pāhī | mājhī to lāhe || Jñāne.18.1111 || Yera ārta jijñāsu arthārthī | he bhajatī jiye paṅthī | te tinhī pāvoni chauthī | mhaṇipata āhe || Jñāne.18.1112 || Yerhavī tijī nā chauthī | he pahilī nā saratī | pai mājhiye sahajasthitī | bhakti nāma || Jñāne.18.1113 || Je neṇaṇe māĵhe prakāshūni | anyathātwe māte dāūni | sarvahī sarvī bhajauni | bujhāvītase || Jñāne.18.1114 || Ĵo jetha jaise pāho base | tayā tetha taiseṅchi ase | he ujiyeḍe kā dise | akhaṅḍe jeṇe || Jñāne.18.1115 || Swapnāche disaṇe na disaṇe | jaise āpaleni asalepaṇe | vishwāche āhe nāhī jeṇe | prakāshe taise || Jñāne.18.1116 || Aisā hā sahaja mājhā | prakāsha ĵo kapidhwajā | to bhakti yā vojā | bolije gā || Jñāne.18.1117 || Mhaṇoni ārtāchyā ṭhāyī | he ārti hoūni pāhī | apekṣhaṇīya je kāhī | te mīchi kelā || Jñāne.18.1118 || Jijñāsupuḍhā vīreshā | hechi hoūni jijñāsā | mī kā jijñāsyu aisā | dākhavilā || Jñāne.18.1119 || Hechi hoūni arthanā | mīchi mājhyā arthī Arjunā | karūni arthābhidhānā | āṇī māte || Jñāne.18.1120 || Eva gheūni ajñānāte | mājhī bhakti je he varte | te dāvī maĵa draṣhṭayāte | drushya karūni || Jñāne.18.1121 || Yethe mukhachi dise mukhe | yā bolā kāhī na chuke | parī dujepaṇa he laṭike | ārisā karī || Jñāne.18.1122 || Diṭhī chaṅdrachi ghe sāche | pari yetule he timirāche | je ekachi ase tayāche | donī dāvī || Jñāne.18.1123 || Taisā sarvatra mīchi miyā | ghepatase dhanaṅjayā | pari drushyatwa he vāyā | ajñānavashe || Jñāne.18.1124 || Te ajñāna ātā phiṭale | māĵhe draṣhṭrutwa maĵa bheṭale | nijabiṁbī ekavaṭale | pratibiṅba jaise || Jñāne.18.1125 || Pai jevhāṁhī ase kiḍāḷa | tevhāṁhī soneṅchi aḍhaḷa | pari te kīḍa geliyā kevaḷa | ure jaise || Jñāne.18.1126 || Hā gā pūrṇame ādhī kāyī | chaṅdra sāvayava nāhī | pari tiye divasī bheṭe pāhī | pūrṇatā tayā || Jñāne.18.1127 || Taisā mīchi ajñānadwāre | dise pari hastāṅtare | maga draṣhṭrutwī te sare | miyāṅchi mī lābhe || Jñāne.18.1128 || Mhaṇauni drushyapathā | atīta mājhā Pārthā | bhaktiyoga chavathā | mhaṇitalā gā || Jñāne.18.1129 || [Dwādashokta-bhaktiyogamāha dwābhyām] -

Bhaktyā māmabhijānāti yāvānyashchāsmi tattwataḥ | tato mā tattwato jñātwā vishate tadanantaram || Bha.Gī.18.55 ||

[Bhaktyā] Iyā jñāna bhaktī sahaja | bhakta ekavaṭalā maĵa | to mīchi kevaḷa he tuĵa | shrutahī āhe || Jñāne.18.1130 || Je ubhaūniyā bhujā | jñāniyā to ātmā mājhā | he bolilo kapidhwajā | saptamādhyāyī || Jñāne.18.1131 || Te he kalpādi bhakti miyā | Shreebhāgavatamiṣhe brahmayā | uttama mhaṇoni dhanaṅjayā | upadeshilī || Jñāne.18.1132 || Jñānī iyete swasaṁviti | shaiva mhaṇatī shakti | āmhī parama bhakti | āpalī mhaṇo || Jñāne.18.1133 || [Māmabhijānāti] He maĵa miḷatiye veḷe | tayā karmayogiyā phaḷe | maga samastahī nikhiḷe | miyāṅchi bhare || Jñāne.18.1134 || Tetha vairāgya vivekeṁsī | āṭe baṅdha mokṣheṁsī | vruttī taye avruttīsī | buḍoni ĵāya || Jñāne.18.1135 || Gheūni ailapaṇāte | paratwa hārape jethe | giḷūni chārhī bhūte | ākāsha jaise || Jñāne.18.1136 || Tayāpari thaḍathāṅda | sādhyasādhanātīta shuddha | te mī hoūni aikavada | bhogito māte || Jñāne.18.1137 || Ghaḍoni siṅdhūchiyā āṅgā | siṅdhūvarī taḷape Gaṅgā | taisā pāḍa tayā bhogā | avadhāriĵo || Jñāne.18.1138 || Kā ārisayāsi ārisā | uṭūni dāviliyā jaisā | dekhaṇā atishaya taisā | bhogaṇā tiye || Jñāne.18.1139 || He aso darpaṇa neliyā | to mukhabodhahī geliyā | dekhalepaṇa ekaleyā | āswādije jevī || Jñāne.18.1140 || Cheilayā swapna nāshe | āpale aikyachi dise | te dujenavīṇa jaise | bhogije kā || Jñāne.18.1141 || Techi jāliyā bhoga tayāĉhā | na ghaḍe hā bhāva jayāṅchā | tihī bole kevi bolāchā | uchchāra kīje || Jñāne.18.1142 || [Yāvān] [sarvavyāpī] tayāṅchyā neṇo gāvī | ravī praKāshī hana divī | kī vyomālāgī māṅḍavī | ubhilī tihī || Jñāne.18.1143 || Hā gā rājanyatwa navhatā āṅgī | rāvo rāyapaṇa kāya bhogī | kā āṅdhāra hana āliṅgī | dinakarāte || Jñāne.18.1144 || Āṇi ākāsha je navhe | tayā ākāsha kāya ĵāṇave | ratnāchyā rūpī mirave | guṅjāṅche leṇe || Jñāne.18.1145 || Mhaṇauni mī hoṇe nāhī | tayā mīchi āhe keṁhī | maga bhajela he kāyī | bolo kīra || Jñāne.18.1146 || Yālāgī to karmayogī | mī jālāchi māte bhogī | tāruṇya kā taruṇāṅgī | jiyāparī || Jñāne.18.1147 || Taraṅga sarvāṅgī toya chuṁbī | prabhā sarvatra vilase biṁbī | nānā avakāsha nabhī | luṅṭhata jaisā || Jñāne.18.1148 || Taisā rūpa hoūni māĵhe | māte kriyāvīṇa to bhaje | alaṅkāra kā sahaĵe | sonayāte jevī || Jñāne.18.1149 || Kā chaṅdanāchī drutī taisī | chaṅdanī bhaje apaisī | kā akrutrima shashī | chaṅdrikā te || Jñāne.18.1150 || Taisī kriyā kīra na sāhe | tarhī adwaitī bhakti āhe | he anubhavāchiĵogee navhe | bolāaise || Jñāne.18.1151 || Tevhā pūrvasaṁskārachhaṅde | je kāhī to anuvāde | teṇe āḷavileni vode | bolatā mīchi || Jñāne.18.1152 || Bolatā bolatāchi bheṭe | tethe bolela he na ghaṭe | te māna tava gomaṭe | stavana māĵhe || Jñāne.18.1153 || Mhaṇoni tayā bolatā | bolī bolatā mī bheṭatā | mauna hoya teṇe tattwatā | stavito māte || Jñāne.18.1154 || Taiseṅchi buddhī kā diṭhī | je to dekho ĵāya kirīṭī | te dekhaṇe drushya loṭī | dekhatechi dāvī || Jñāne.18.1155 || Ārisayā ādhī jaise | dekhatechi mukha dise | tayāche dekhaṇe taise | meḷavī draṣhṭe || Jñāne.18.1156 || Drushya jāuniyā draṣhṭe | draṣhṭayāsīchi jai bheṭe | tai ekalepaṇe na ghaṭe | draṣhṭepaṇahī || Jñāne.18.1157 || Tetha swapnīṅchiyā priyā | chevoni jhoṅbo geliyā | ṭhāyije donhī na honiyā | āpaṇachi jaise || Jñāne.18.1158 || Kā dohī kāṣhṭhāṅchiye ghuṣhṭī- | mājī vahnī yeka uṭhī | to donhī he bhāṣha āṭī | āpaṇachi hoya || Jñāne.18.1159 || Nā nā pratibiṁba hātī | gheū geliyā gabhastī | biṁbatāhī asatī | ĵāya jaisī || Jñāne.18.1160 || Taisā mī hoūni dekhate | to gheū ĵāya drushyāte | tetha drushya ne thite | draṣhṭrutweṁsī || Jñāne.18.1161 || Ravi āṅdhāra praKāshitā | nurechi jevi prakāshatā | tevi drushyī nāhī draṣhṭratā | mī jāliyā || Jñāne.18.1162 || Maga dekhije nā na dekhije | aisī je dashā nipaje | te te darshana māĵhe | sāchokāre || Jñāne.18.1163 || Te bhalatayāhī kirīṭī | padārthāchiyā bheṭī | draṣhṭrudrushyātītā druṣhṭī | bhogito sadā || Jñāne.18.1164 || [Yashchāsmi] [chidānandaghanaḥ] āṇi ākāsha he ākāshe | dāṭale na ḍhaḷe jaise | miyā ātmena āpaṇape taise | ĵāle tayā || Jñāne.18.1165 || Kalpāṅtī udaka udake | ruṅdhiliyā vāho ṭhāke | taisā ātmeni miyā yeke | koṅdalā to || Jñāne.18.1166 || Pāvo āpaṇayā voḷaghe | kevi vahni āpaṇapayā lāge | āpaṇapā pāṇī righe | snānā kaise || Jñāne.18.1167 || Mhaṇoni sarva mī ĵālepaṇe | ṭhele tayā yeṇe ĵāṇe | techi gā yātrā karaṇe | adwayā maĵa || Jñāne.18.1168 || Pai jaḷāvarīla taraṅga | ĵarī dhāṁvinnalā savega | tarī nāhī bhūmibhāga | kramilā teṇe || Jñāne.18.1169 || Je sāṅḍāve kā māṅḍāve | je chālaṇee jeṇe chālāve | te toyachi yeka āghave | mhaṇoniyā || Jñāne.18.1170 || Geliyāhī bhalateutā | udakapaṇe Paṅḍusutā | taraṅgāchī ekātmatā | na moḍechi jevī || Jñāne.18.1171 || Taisā mīpaṇe hā loṭalā | to āghaveyāchi maĵa ālā | yā yātrā hoya bhalā | kāpaḍī mājhā || Jñāne.18.1172 || [Tato māṁ] Āṇi sharīra swabhāvavashe | kāhī yeka karū ĵarī baise | tari mīchi to teṇe miṣhe | bheṭe tayā || Jñāne.18.1173 || Tetha karma āṇi kartā | he jāūni Paṅḍusutā | miyā ātmeni maĵa pāhatā | mīchi hoya || Jñāne.18.1174 || Pai darpaṇāte darpaṇe | pāhiliyā hoya na pāhāṇe | sone jhāṅkiliyā suvarṇe | na jhāṅke jevī || Jñāne.18.1175 || Dīpāte dīpe praKāshije | te na prakāshaṇeṅchi nipaje | taise karma miyā kīje | te karaṇe kaiṅche || Jñāne.18.1176 || Karmahī karītachi āhe | jai karāve he bhāṣha jāye | tai na karaṇeṅchi hoye | tayāche kele || Jñāne.18.1177 || Kriyājāta mī ĵālepaṇe | ghaḍe kāhīṅchi na karaṇe | tayāchi nāṁva pūjaṇe | khuṇeche māĵhe || Jñāne.18.1178 || Mhaṇauni karitayāhī vojā | te na karaṇe hechi kapidhwajā | nipaje tiyā mahāpūjā | pūjī to māte || Jñāne.18.1179 || Eva to bole te stavana | to dekhe te darshana | adwayā maĵa gamana | to chāle techi || Jñāne.18.1180 || To karī tetulī pūjā | to kalpī to japa mājhā | to nije techi kapidhwajā | samādhi mājhī || Jñāne.18.1181 || Jaise kanakeṅsī kāṅkaṇe | asije ananyapaṇe | to bhaktiyoge yeṇe | majasī taisā || Jñāne.18.1182 || Udakī kalloḷa | kāpurī parimaḷa | ratnī ujāḷa | ananya jaisā || Jñāne.18.1183 || Kiṅbahunā taṅtūsī paṭa | kā mruttikesī ghaṭa | taisā to yekavaṭa | majasī mājhā || Jñāne.18.1184 || Iyā ananyasiddhā bhaktī | yā āghavāchi drushyajātī | maĵa āpaṇapeṁyā sumatī | draṣhṭayāte ĵāṇe || Jñāne.18.1185 || Tinhī avasthāṅcheni dwāre | upādhyupahitākāre | bhāvābhāvarūpa sphure | drushya je he || Jñāne.18.1186 || Te he āghaveṅchi mī draṣhṭā | aisiyā bodhāchā mājivaṭā | anubhavāchā subhaṭā | dheṅḍā to nāche || Jñāne.18.1187 || [Tattwataḥ] Rajju jāliyā gochara | ābhāsatā to vyāḷākāra | rajjūcha aisā nirdhāra | hoya jevī || Jñāne.18.1188 || Bhāṅgārāparate kāhī | leṇe guṅjahībharī nāhī | he āṭuniyā ṭhāyī | kīje jaise || Jñāne.18.1189 || Udakā yekāparate | taraṅga nāhīṅchi he nirute | ĵāṇoni tayā ākārāte | na ghepe jevī || Jñāne.18.1190 || Nā tarī swapnavikārā samastā | cheuniyā umāṇe ghetā | to āpaṇayā parautā | na dise jaisā || Jñāne.18.1191 || Taise je kāhī āthi nāthī | teṇe hoya jñeyasphūrtī | te jñātāchi mī he pratītī | hoūni bhogī || Jñāne.18.1192 || [Jñātwā] Ĵāṇe aja mī ajara | akṣhaya mī akṣhara | apūrva mī apāra | ānaṅda mī || Jñāne.18.1193 || Achaḷa mī achyuta | anaṅta mī adwaita | ādya mī avyakta | vyaktahī mī || Jñāne.18.1194 || Īshya mī īshwara | anādi mī amara | abhaya mī ādhāra | ādheya mī || Jñāne.18.1195 || Swāmī mī sadodita | sahaja mī satata | sarva mī sarvagata | sarvātīta mī || Jñāne.18.1196 || Navā mī purāṇu | shūnya mī saṁpūrṇu | asthūla anaṇu | je kāhī te mī || Jñāne.18.1197 || Akriya mī eka | asaṅga mī ashoka | vyāpta mī vyāpaka | puruṣhottama mī || Jñāne.18.1198 || Ashabda mī ashrotra | arūpa mī agotra | sama mī swataṅtra | brahma mī para || Jñāne.18.1199 || Aise ātmatwe maĵa ekāte | iyā adwayabhaktī ĵāṇoni nirute | āṇi yāhī bodhā ĵāṇate | teṁhī mīchi ĵāṇe || Jñāne.18.1200 || Pai cheileyānaṅtare | āpule ekapaṇa ure | teṅhī tayāvarī sphure | tayāsīṅchi jaise || Jñāne.18.1201 || Kā prakāshatā arka | tochi hoya prakāshaka | tayāhī abhedā dyotaka | tochi jaisā || Jñāne.18.1202 || Taisā vedyāṅchyā vilayī | kevaḷa vedaka ure pāhī | teṇe ĵāṇave tayāteṁhī | heṅhī ĵo ĵāṇe || Jñāne.18.1203 || Tayā adwayapaṇā āpuliyā | ĵāṇatī jñaptī je dhanaṅjayā | te īshwarachi mī he tayā | bodhāsi ye || Jñāne.18.1204 || [Vishate tadanantaraṁ] Maga dwaitādwaitātīta | mīchi ātmā eka nibhrāṅta | he ĵāṇoni ĵāṇaṇe jetha | anubhavī righe || Jñāne.18.1205 || Tetha cheilayā yekapaṇa | dise je āpulayā āpaṇa | teṅhī jātā neṇo koṇa | hoije jevī || Jñāne.18.1206 || Kā ḍoḷā dekhatiye kṣhaṇī | swarūpapaṇa suvarṇī | nāṭitā hoya āṭaṇī | aḷaṅkārāchīhī || Jñāne.18.1207 || Nā nā lavaṇa toya hoye | maga kṣhāratā toyatwe rāhe | tehī jiratā jevi jāye | ĵālepaṇa te || Jñāne.18.1208 || Taisā mī to he je ase | te swānaṅdānubhavasamarase | kālavūniyā praveshe | majachimājī || Jñāne.18.1209 || [Tattwataḥ] Āṇi to he bhāṣha jetha jāye | tethe mī he koṇhāsī āhe | aisā mī nā to tiye sāmāye | mājhyāchi rūpī || Jñāne.18.1210 || Jevhā kāpura ĵaḷo sare | tayāchi nāma agni pure | maga ubhayātīta ure | ākāsha jevī || Jñāne.18.1211 || Kā dhāḍiliyā ekā eka | vāḍhe to shūnya vishekha | taisā āhenāhīṅchā shekha | mīchi maga āthī || Jñāne.18.1212 || Tetha brahma ātmā īsha | yayā bolā moḍe saurasa | na bolaṇe yāhī paisa | nāhī tetha || Jñāne.18.1213 || Na bolaṇeṅhī na bolonī | te bolije toṅḍa bharūnī | jāṇīva neṇiva neṇonī | jāṇije te || Jñāne.18.1214 || Tetha bujhije bodha bodhe | ānaṅda ghepe ānaṅde | sukhavarī nusadhe | sukhachi bhogije || Jñāne.18.1215 || Tetha lābha ĵoḍalā lābhā | prabhā āliṅgilī prabhā | vismaya buḍālā ubhā | vismayāmājī || Jñāne.18.1216 || Shama tetha shamāvalā | vishrāma vishrāṅtī ālā | anubhava veḍāvalā | anubhūtipaṇe || Jñāne.18.1217 || [Ayamabhiprāyaḥ] Kiṁbahunā aise nikhaḷa | mīpaṇā ĵoḍe tayā phaḷa | sevūni velī velhāḷa | karmayogāchī te || Jñāne.18.1218 || Pai karmayogiyā kirīṭī | chakravartīchyā mukuṭī | mī chidratna te sāṭovāṭī | hoya to mājhā || Jñāne.18.1219 || Kī karmayoga-prāsādāchā | kaḷasa ĵo hā mokṣhāchā | tayā varīla avakāshāchā | uvāvo jālā to || Jñāne.18.1220 || Nā nā saṁsāra āḍavī | karmayoga vāṭa baravī | ĵoḍalī te madaikyagāṁvī | paiṭhī jālīse || Jñāne.18.1221 || He aso karmayogavoghe | teṇe bhaktichidgaṅge | mī swānaṅdodadhi vege | ṭhākilā kī gā || Jñāne.18.1222 || Hā ṭhāyavarī suvarmā | karmayogī āhe mahimā | mhaṇauni veḷoveḷā tumhā | sāṅgato āmhī || Jñāne.18.1223 || [Chūrṇikā] Pai deshe kāḷe padārthe | sādhūni gheije māte | taisā navhe mī āyate | sarvāṅche sarvahī || Jñāne.18.1224 || Mhaṇauni mājhyā ṭhāyī | jāchāve nalage kāhī | mī lābhe iye upāyī | sāchācha gā || Jñāne.18.1225 || Eka shiṣhya eka guru | hā rūḍhalā sācha vyavahārū | to matprāptiprakārū | jāṇāvayā || Jñāne.18.1226 || Agā vasudhechyā poṭī | nidhāna siddha kirīṭī | vahni siddha kāṣhṭhī | vohā dūdha || Jñāne.18.1227 || Pari lābhe te asate | tayā kīje upāyāte | yera siddhachi taisā tethe | upāyī mī || Jñāne.18.1228 || Hā phaḷavarī upāvo | kā pā prastāvītase devo | he pusatā tari abhiprāvo | yethiṅchā aisā || Jñāne.18.1229 || Je Gītārthāche chāṅgāve | mokṣhopāyapara āghave | āna shāstropāya navhe | pramāṇasiddha || Jñāne.18.1230 || Vārā ābhāḷachi pheḍī | vāṅchūna sūryāte na ghaḍī | kā hāta bāṅbuḷī dhāḍī | toya na karī || Jñāne.18.1231 || Taisā ātmadarshanī āḍaḷa | ase avidyechā ĵo maḷa | to shāstra nāshī yera nirmaḷa | mī prakāshe swaye || Jñāne.18.1232 || Mhaṇauni āghavīṅchi shāstre | avidyāvināshāchī pātre | vāṅchoni na hotī swataṅtre | ātmabodhī || Jñāne.18.1233 || Tayā adhyātmashāstrāṁsī | jai sāchapaṇāchī ye pusī | tai yeije jayā ṭhāyāsī | te he Gītā || Jñāne.18.1234 || Bhānubhūṣhitā prāchiyā | satejā dishā āghaviyā | taisī shāstreshwarā Gītā yā | sanāthe shāstre || Jñāne.18.1235 || He aso yeṇe shāstreshware | māgā upāya bahuve vistāre | sāṅgītalā jaisā kare | ghevo ye ātmā || Jñāne.18.1236 || Pari prathamashravaṇāsave | Arjunā vipāye he phāve | hā bhāva sakaṇave | dharūni Shreeharī || Jñāne.18.1237 || Techi prameya ekaveḷa | shiṣhyī hoāvayā aḍhaḷa | sāṅgatase mukuḷa- | mudrā ātā || Jñāne.18.1238 || Āṇi prasaṅge Gītā | ṭhāvahī hā saṁpatā | mhaṇauni dāvī ādyaṅtā | ekārthatwa || Jñāne.18.1239 || Je graṅthāchyā madhyabhāgī | nānā adhikāraprasaṅgī | nirūpaṇā anegī | siddhāṅtī kele || Jñāne.18.1240 || Tari tetulehī siddhāṅta | iye shāstrī prastuta | he pūrvāpāra neṇata | koṇhī jai mānī || Jñāne.18.1241 || Tai mahāsiddhāṅtāchā āvāṅkā | siddhāṅtakakṣhā anekā | bhiḍaūni āraṅbha dekhā | saṁpavīta ase || Jñāne.18.1242 || Etha avidyānāsha he sthaḷa | teṇe mokṣhāpādana phaḷa | yā dohī kevaḷa | sādhana jñāna || Jñāne.18.1243 || He ituleṅchi nānāparī | nirūpile graṅthavistārī | te ātā dohī akṣharī | anuvādāve || Jñāne.18.1244 || Mhaṇauni upeyahī hātī | jālayā upāyasthitī | deva pravartale te puḍhatī | yeṇeṅchi bhāve || Jñāne.18.1245 ||

Sarvakarmāṇyapi sadā kurvāṇo madwyapāshrayaḥ | matprasādādavāpnoti shāshwataṁ padamavyayam || Bha.Gī.18.56 ||

[Sarvakarmāṇyapi] Maga mhaṇe gā subhaṭā | to karmayogiyā niṣhṭhā | mī hounī hoya paiṭhā | mājhyā rūpī || Jñāne.18.1246 || Swakarmāṅchyā chokhauḷī | maĵa pūjā karūni bhalī | teṇe prasāde ākaḷī | jñānaniṣhṭhete || Jñāne.18.1247 || Te jñānaniṣhṭhā jetha hātavase | tetha bhakti mājhī ullāse | tiyā majasī samarase | sukhiyā hoya || Jñāne.18.1248 || [Madwyapāshrayaḥ] Āṇi vishwapraKāshitayā | ātmayā maĵa āpuliyā | anusare ĵo karūniyā | sarvatratā he || Jñāne.18.1249 || Sāṅḍūni āpalā āḍaḷa | lavaṇa āshrayī jaḷa | kā hiṅḍoni rāhe nishchaḷa | vāyu vyomī || Jñāne.18.1250 || Taisā buddhī vāchā kāye | ĵo māte āshraūni ṭhāye | [sadā kurvāṇaḥ] to niṣhiddheṁhī vipāye | karme karū || Jñāne.18.1251 || [Matprasādādavāpnoti] Pari gaṅgechyā saṁbaṅdhī | bidī āṇi mahānadī | aikya tevi mājhyā bodhī | shubhāshubhāṁsī || Jñāne.18.1252 || Kā bāvane āṇi ghure | hā nivāḍa tavachi sare | jaṅva na ghepatī vaishwānare | kavaḷūni donhī || Jñāne.18.1253 || Nānā pāṅchike āṇi soḷe | he sonayā tavachi āḷe | ĵava parisa āṅgameḷe | yekavaṭīnā || Jñāne.18.1254 || Taise shubhāshubha aise | he tavachivarī ābhāse | ĵava yeka na prakāshe | sarvatra mī || Jñāne.18.1255 || Agā rātri āṇi divo | hā tavachi dwaitabhāvo | jaṅva na rigije gāṁvo | gabhastīchā || Jñāne.18.1256 || Mhaṇauni mājhiyā bheṭī | tayāṅchī sarva karme kirīṭī | jāūni baise to pāṭī | sāyujyāchyā || Jñāne.18.1257 || [Shāshwataṁ padamavyayaṁ] Deshe kāḷe swabhāve | veṅcha jayā na saṁbhave | te pada māĵhe pāve | avināsha to || Jñāne.18.1258 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Kiṁbahunā Paṅḍusutā | maĵa ātmayāchī prasannatā | lāhe teṇe na pavijatā | lābha kavaṇa ase || Jñāne.18.1259 || [Chaturthoktabrahmārpaṇayogamāha] -

Chetasā sarvakarmāṇi mayi saṁ(n)nyasya matparaḥ | buddhiyogamupāshritya machchittaḥ(s) satataṁ bhava || Bha.Gī.18.57 ||

[Chetasā sarvakarmāṇi] Yākāraṇe gā tuvā iyā | sarva karmā āpuliyā | mājhyā swarūpī dhanaṅjayā | saṅnyāsa kīje || Jñāne.18.1260 || Pari tochi saṅnyāsa vīrā | karaṇīyāĉhā ĵhaṇe karā | ātmavivekī dharā | chittavrutti he || Jñāne.18.1261 || [Mayi] Maga teṇe vivekabaḷe | āpaṇape karmāvegaḷe | mājhyā swarūpī nirmaḷe | dekhijela sarva || Jñāne.18.1262 || [Saṁ(n)nyasya] Āṇi karmāchī janmabhoye | prakruti je kā āhe | te āpaṇayāhūni bahuve | dekhasī durī || Jñāne.18.1263 || Tetha prakruti āpaṇayāṁ- | vegaḷī nure dhanaṅjayā | rūpeṅvīṇa kā chhāyā | jayāparī || Jñāne.18.1264 || Aiseni prakrutināsha | jālayā karmasaṅnyāsa | niphajela anāyāsa | sakāraṇa || Jñāne.18.1265 || [Matparaḥ] Maga karmajāta geliyā | mī ātmā ure āpaṇapayā | [buddhiyogamupāshritya] tetha buddhi ghāpe karūniyā | pativratā || Jñāne.18.1266 || Buddhi ananya yeṇe yoge | majamājī jai rige | [machchittaḥ(s) satataṁ bhava] tai chitta chaityatyāge | mātechi bhaje || Jñāne.18.1267 || Aise chaityajāte sāṅḍile | chitta mājhyā ṭhāyī jaḍale | ṭhāke taise vahile | sarvadā karī || Jñāne.18.1268 || [Aṣhṭame ananyachetā ityādinoktamakṣharayogaṁ smārayati]

Machchittaḥ(s) sarvadurgāṇi matprasādāttariṣhyasi | atha chettwamahaṅgkārānna shroṣhyasi vinaṅgkṣhyasi || Bha.Gī.18.58 ||

[Machchittaḥ] Maga abhinnā iyā sevā | chitta miyāṅchi bharela jevhā | mājhā prasāda ĵāṇa tevhā | saṅpūrṇa ĵāhalā || Jñāne.18.1269 || [Sarvadurgāṇi] Tetha sakaḷa duḥkhadhāme | bhuṅjījatī jiye mrutyujanme | tiye durgameṅchi sugame | hotī tuĵa || Jñāne.18.1270 || Sūryācheni sāvāye | ḍoḷā sāvāilā hoye | tai āṅdhārāchā āhe | pāḍa tayā || Jñāne.18.1271 || [Matprasādāt] Taisā māĵheni prasāde | jīvakaṇa jayāĉhā upamarde | to saṁsārācheni bādhe | bāgule kevī || Jñāne.18.1272 || [Tariṣhyasi] Mhaṇauni dhanaṅjayā | tū saṁsāradurgatī yayā | tarasīla mājhiyā | prasādāstava || Jñāne.18.1273 || [Prathamādhyāyoktaviṣhādayogottaramāha atheti sārdhadwābhyām] [atha chettwamahaṅgkārānna shroṣhyasi] athavā hana ahaṁbhāve | māĵhe bolaṇe he āghave | kānāmanāchiye shive | nedisī ṭeṅko || Jñāne.18.1274 || Tari nityamukta avyaya | tū āhāsi te hovūni vāya | [vinaṅgkṣhyasi] dehasaṅbaṅdhāchā ghāya | vājela āṅgī || Jñāne.18.1275 || Jayā dehasaṁbaṅdhāāṅta | pratipadī ātmaghāta | bhuṅjatā usaṅta | kaṅhīṅcha nāhī || Jñāne.18.1276 || Yevaḍheni dāruṇe | nimaṇenavīṇa nimaṇe | paḍela ĵarī bolaṇe | neghasī māĵhe || Jñāne.18.1277 ||

Yadahaṅgkāramāshritya na yotsya iti manyase | mithyaiṣha vyavasāyaste prakrutistwāṁ(n) niyokṣhyati || Bha.Gī.18.59 ||

[Yadahaṅgkāramāshritya] Pathyadweṣhiyā poṣhī jvara | kā dīpadweṣhiyā aṅdhakāra | vivekadweṣhe ahaṅkāra | poṣhūni taisā || Jñāne.18.1278 || Swadehā nāma Arjun | paradehā nāma swajana | saṅgramā nāma malina | pāpāchāra || Jñāne.18.1279 || Iyā matī āpuliyā | tighā tīna nāme yayā | ṭheūniyā dhanaṅjayā | [na yotsya iti manyase] na juṅjhe aisā || Jñāne.18.1280 || [Mithyaiṣha vyavasāyaste] Jīvāmājī niṣhṭaṅka | karisī ĵo ātyaṅtika | to vāyā dhāḍīla naisargika | swabhāvachi tujhā || Jñāne.18.1281 || Āṇi mī Arjun he ātmika | yayā vadha karaṇe he pātaka | he māyā vāṅchūni tāttwika | kāhī āhe || Jñāne.18.1282 || Ādhī juṅjhāra tuvā hoāve | maga ĵuṅĵhāvayā shastra gheyāve | kā na ĵuṅĵhāvayā karāve | devāṅgaṇa || Jñāne.18.1283 || Mhaṇauni na juṅĵhaṇe | mhaṇasī te vāyāṇe | nā mānū lokapaṇe | lokadruṣhṭīhī || Jñāne.18.1284 || [Prakrutistwāṁ(n) niyokṣhyati] Tarhī na juṅjhe aise | niṣhṭaṅkisī je mānase | te prakruti anārise | karavīlachi || Jñāne.18.1285 ||

Swabhāvajena Kaunteya nibaddhaḥ(s) swena karmaṇā | kartuṁ(n) nechchhasi yanmohātkariṣhyasyavasho’pi tat || Bha.Gī.18.60 ||

[Swabhāvajena Kaunteya] Pai pūrve vāhatā pāṇī | pavhije pashchimeche vāhaṇī | tari āgrahachi ure te āṇī | āpuliyā lekhā || Jñāne.18.1286 || Kā sāḷīchā kaṇa mhaṇe | mī nugave sāḷīpaṇe | tarī āhe āna karaṇe | swabhāvāsī || Jñāne.18.1287 || [Nibaddhaḥ(s) swena karmaṇā] Taisā kṣhātrasaṁskārasiddhā | prakrutī ghaḍilāsi prabuddhā | ātā nuṭhī mhaṇasī hā dhāṅdā | pari uṭhavijasīchi tū || Jñāne.18.1288 || Pai shaurya teja dakṣhatā | evamādika Paṅḍusutā | guṇa didhale janmatā | prakrutī tuĵa || Jñāne.18.1289 || Tari tayāchiyā samavāyā- | anurūpa dhanaṅjayā | na karitā ugaliyā | na yela aso || Jñāne.18.1290 || Mhaṇauniyā tihī guṇī | bāṅdhalāsi tū kodaṅḍapāṇī | trishuddhi nighasī vāhāṇī | kṣhātrāchiyā || Jñāne.18.1291 || [Kartuṁ(n) nechchhasi yanmohāt] Nā he āpule janmamūḷa | na vichāritachi kevaḷa | na juṅjhe aise aḍhaḷa | vrata ĵarī ghesī || Jñāne.18.1292 || [Kariṣhyasyavasho’pi tat] Tari bāṅdhoni hāta pāye | ĵo rathī ghātalā hoye | to na chale tarī jāye | digaṅtā jevī || Jñāne.18.1293 || Taisā tū āpuliyākaḍūnī | mī kāhīṅcha na karī mhaṇaunī | ṭhāsī parī bharaṁvasenī | tūchi karisī || Jñāne.18.1294 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Uttara vairāṭīṅchā rājā | paḷatā tū kā nighālāsi juṅjhā | hā kṣhātraswabhāva tujhā | ĵuṅĵhavīla tuĵa || Jñāne.18.1295 || Mahāvīra akarā akṣhauhiṇī | tuvā yeke nāgavile raṇāṅgaṇī | to swabhāva kodaṅḍapāṇī | ĵuṅĵhavīla tūte || Jñāne.18.1296 || Hā gā roga kāyī rogiyā | āvaḍe daridra daridriyā | pari bhogavije baḷiyā | adruṣhṭe jeṇe || Jñāne.18.1297 || Te adruṣhṭa anārise | na karīla īshwaravashe | to īshwarahī ase | hrudayī tujhyā || Jñāne.18.1298 || [Dashamaikādashayoruktau vibhūtivishwarūpadarshanayogau darshayati īshwara iti dwābhyām]

Īshwaraḥ(s) sarvabhūtānāṁ hruddeshe’rjuna tiṣhṭhati | bhrāmayansarvabhūtāni yantrārūḍhāni māyayā || Bha.Gī.18.61 ||

[Sarvabhūtānāṁ] [‘bhoktāraṁ yajña’ iti pañchamādhyāyāṁ(n)tyashlokasyāpi bhāvārtho’tra draṣhṭavyaḥ’] sarva bhūtāṅchyā aṅtarī | hrudaya mahāaṁbarī | chidwruttīchyā sahasrakarī | udayalā ase ĵo || Jñāne.18.1299 || Avasthātraya tinhī loka | prakāshūni asheṣha | anyathādruṣhṭi pāṅthika | chevavile || Jñāne.18.1300 || Vedyodakāchyā sarovarī | phāṅkatā viṣhaya kalhārī | iṅdriyaṣhaṭpadā chārī | jīvabhramarāte || Jñāne.18.1301 || [Īshwaraḥ] Aso rūpaka he to īshwara | sakaḷa bhūtāṅchā ahaṅkāra | pāṅgharoni niraṅtara | ulhāsata ase || Jñāne.18.1302 || [Māyayā] Swamāyeche āḍavastra | lāvūni ekalā kheḷavī sūtra | bāherī naṭī chhāyāchitra | chauryāsī lakṣha || Jñāne.18.1303 || Tayā brahmādikīṭāṅtā | asheṣhāṁhī bhūtajātā | dehākāra yogyatā | pāhoni dāvī || Jñāne.18.1304 || [Yantrārūḍhāni] Tetha je deha jayāpuḍhe | anurūpapaṇe māṅḍe | te bhūta tayā ārūḍhe | he mī mhaṇauni || Jñāne.18.1305 || Sūta sūte guṅtale | truṇa truṇeṅchi bāṅdhale | kā ātmabiṅbā ghetale | bāḷake jaḷī || Jñāne.18.1306 || Tayāparī dehākāre | āpaṇapeṅchi dusare | dekhoni jīva āviṣhkare | ātmabuddhi || Jñāne.18.1307 || Aiseni sharīrākārī | yaṅtrī bhūte avadhārī | [bhrāmayan] vāhūni hālavī dorī | prāchīnāchī || Jñāne.18.1308 || Tetha jayā je karmasūtra | māṅḍūni ṭhevile swataṅtra | te tiye gatī pātra | hoṅchi lāge || Jñāne.18.1309 || Kiṅbahunā dhanurdharā | bhūtāṅte swarga- saṁsārā- | māji bhovaṅḍī truṇe vārā | āKāshī jaisī || Jñāne.18.1310 || Bhrāmakācheni saṅge | jaise loho veḍhā rige | taisī īshwarasattāyoge | cheṣhṭatī bhūte || Jñāne.18.1311 || Jaise cheṣhṭā āpulāliyā | samudrādika dhanaṅjayā | cheṣhṭatī chaṅdrāchiyā | sannidhi yekī || Jñāne.18.1312 || Tayā siṅdhū bharite dāṭe | somakāṅtā pājhara phuṭe | kumudāṅchakorāṅchā phiṭe | saṅkocha to || Jñāne.18.1313 || Taisī bījaprakrutivashe | aneke bhūte yeke īshe | cheṣhṭavījatī to ase | [hruddeshe’rjuna tiṣhṭhati] tujhyā hrudayī || Jñāne.18.1314 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Arjunapaṇa na ghetā | mī aise je Paṅḍusutā | uṭhatase te tattwatā | tayāche rūpa || Jñāne.18.1315 || Yālāgī to prakrutīte | pravartavīla he nirute | āṇi te ĵuṅĵhavīla tūte | na ĵuṅĵhasī jarhī || Jñāne.18.1316 || Mhaṇauni īshwara gosāvī | teṇe prakruti he nemāvī | tiyā sukhe rābavāvī | iṅdriye āpulī || Jñāne.18.1317 || Tū karaṇe nakaraṇe donhī | lāūni prakrutīchyā mānī | prakrutīhī kā adhīnī | hrudayasthā jayā || Jñāne.18.1318 ||

Tameva sharaṇaṁ(ṅ) gachchha sarvabhāvena Bhārata | tatprasādātparāṁ shāntiṁ sthānaṁ prāpsyasi shāshwatam || Bha.Gī.18.62 ||

[Tameva sharaṇaṁ(ṅ) gachchheti] Tayā aha vāchā chitta āṅga | deūniyā sharaṇa riga | mahodadhī kā gāṅga | rigāle jaise || Jñāne.18.1319 || [Tatprasādātparāṁ shāntiṁ] Maga tayācheni prasāde | sarvopashāṅtipramade | kāṅta hoūniyā swānaṅde | virūpīṅcha ramasī || Jñāne.18.1320 || [Sthānaṁ prāpsyasi shāshwataṁ] Saṅbhūti jeṇe saṁbhave | vishrāṅti jethe visaṁbe | anubhūtihī anubhave | anubhavā jayā || Jñāne.18.1321 || Tiye nijātmapadīṅchā rāvo | hoūni ṭhākasī avyayo | mhaṇe lakṣhmīnāho | Pārthā tū || Jñāne.18.1322 ||

Iti te jñānamākhyātaṁ(ṅ) guhyādguhyataraṁ mayā | vimrushyaitadasheṣheṇa yathechchhasi tathā kuru || Bha.Gī.18.63 ||

[Iti] He Gītānāma vikhyāta | sarvavāṅgmayāche mathita | ātmā jeṇe hastagata | ratna hoya || Jñāne.18.1323 || [Jñānamākhyātaṁ] Jñāna aisiyā rūḍhī | vedāṅte jayāchī prauḍhī | vānitā kīrti chokhaḍī | pātalī jagī || Jñāne.18.1324 || Buddhyādike ḍoḷase | he jayāche kā kaḍavase | mī sarvadraṣhṭāhi dise | pāhalā jayā || Jñāne.18.1325 || Te [guhyādguhyataraṁ] he gā ātmajñāna | maĵa gopyācheṅhī gupta dhana | pari tū mhaṇūni āna | kevi karū || Jñāne.18.1326 || [Mayā] Yākāraṇe gā Pāṅḍavā | āmhī āpalā hā gupta ṭhevā | [te] tuĵa didhalā kaṇavā | jākaḷilepaṇe || Jñāne.18.1327 || Jaisī bhulalī vorase | māya bole bāḷoddeshe | prīti hī parī taise | na karūṅchi ho || Jñāne.18.1328 || Tetha ākāsha āṇi gāḷije | amrutāhī sālī pheḍije | kā divyākaravī karavije | divya jaise || Jñāne.18.1329 || Jayāĉheni aṅgaprakāshe | pātāḷīṅchā paramāṇu dise | tayā sūryāhi kā jaise | aṅjana sudale || Jñāne.18.1330 || Taise sarvajñeṁhī miyā | sarvahī nirdhārūniyā | nike hoya te dhanaṅjayā | sāṅgītale tuĵa || Jñāne.18.1331 || [Vimrushyaitadasheṣheṇa] Ātā tū yayāvarī | nike he nirdhārī | nirdhārūni [yathechchhasi tathā kuru] karī | āvaḍe taise || Jñāne.18.1332 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Yayā devāchiyā bolā | Arjun ugāchi ṭhelā | tetha devo mhaṇatī bhalā | avaṅchaka hosī || Jñāne.18.1333 || Vāḍhitayā puḍhe bhukelā | uparodhe mhaṇe dhālā | tai tochi pīḍe āpalā | āṇi doṣhahī tayā || Jñāne.18.1334 || Taisā sarvajña Shreegurū | bheṭaliyā ātmanirdhārū | na pusije jai ābhārū | dharūniyā || Jñāne.18.1335 || Tai āpaṇapeṅchi vaṅche | āṇi pāpahī vaṅchanāche | āpaṇayāchi sāche | chukavile teṇe || Jñāne.18.1336 || Pai ugepaṇā tujhiyā | hā abhiprāvo kī dhanaṅjayā | je ekaveḷa āvāṅkuniyā | sāṅgāve jñāna || Jñāne.18.1337 || Tetha Pārth mhaṇe dātārā | bhale ĵāṇasī mājhiyā aṅtarā | he mhaṇo tarī dusarā | ĵāṇatā ase kāī || Jñāne.18.1338 || Yera jñeya he jī āghave | tū jñātā yekachi swabhāve | mā sūrya mhaṇauni vānāve | sūryāte kāī || Jñāne.18.1339 || Yā bolā ShreeKriṣhṇe | mhaṇītale kāya yeṇe | hechi thoḍe gā vānaṇe | je bujhatāsi tū || Jñāne.18.1340 || [Navamoktaṁ rājaguhyamāha sarvaguhyamiti dwābhyām]

Sarvaguhyatamaṁ bhūyaḥ(sh) shrruṇu me paramaṁ vachaḥ | iṣhṭo’si me druḍhamiti tato vakṣhyāmi te hitam || Bha.Gī.18.64 ||

[Shrruṇu me paramaṁ vachaḥ] Tari avadhāna paghaḷa | karūniyā āṇīka ekaveḷa | vākya māĵhe nirmaḷa | avadhārī pā || Jñāne.18.1341 || [Sarvaguhyatamaṁ bhūyaḥ] He vāchya mhaṇoni bolije | kā shrāvya maga āyikije | taise navhe pari tuĵhe | bhāgya barave || Jñāne.18.1342 || Kūrmīchiyā piliyā | diṭhī pānhā ye dhanaṅjayā | ākāsha bāhe bāpiyā | gharīṅche pāṇī || Jñāne.18.1343 || Ĵo vyavahāra jetha na ghaḍe | tayāche phaḷachi tetha ĵoḍe | kāya daive na sāpaḍe | sānukūḷe || Jñāne.18.1344 || Yeravī dwaitāchī vārī | sārūni aikyāchyā parivarī | bhogije te avadhārī | rahasya he || Jñāne.18.1345 || Āṇi nirupachārā premā | viṣhaya hoya je priyottamā | te duje navhe kī ātmā | aiseṅchi ĵāṇāve || Jñāne.18.1346 || [Iṣhṭo’si me] Ārisāchiyā dekhilayā | gomaṭe kīje dhanaṅjayā | te tayā nohe āpaṇayāṁ- | lāgī jaise || Jñāne.18.1347 || Taise Pārthā tuĵheni miṣhe | mī bole āpaṇayāchi doṣhe | mājhyā tujhyā ṭhāī ase | mītūṅpaṇā gā || Jñāne.18.1348 || Mhaṇauni jivhārīṅche guja | sāṅgatase jīvāsī tuĵa | he ananyagatīche maĵa | āthī vyasana || Jñāne.18.1349 || [Druḍhamiti] Pai jaḷā āpaṇape detā | lavaṇa bhulale Paṅḍusutā | kī āghave tayāche hotā | na lājechi te || Jñāne.18.1350 || Taisā tū mājhyā ṭhāī | rākho neṇasīchi kāhī | tarī ātā tuĵa kāī | gopya mī karī || Jñāne.18.1351 || [Tato vakṣhyāmi te hitaṁ] Mhaṇauni āghavīṅchi gūḍhe | je pāūni ati ughaḍe | te gopya māĵhe ĉhokhaḍe | vākya āika || Jñāne.18.1352 ||

Manmanā bhava madbhakto madyājī māṁ(n) namaskuru | māmevaiṣhyasi satyaṁ(n) te pratijāne priyo’si me || Bha.Gī.18.65 ||

[Manmanā bhava] Tari bāhya āṇi aṅtarā | āpuliyā sarva vyāpārā | maĵa vyāpakāte vīrā | viṣhaya karī || Jñāne.18.1353 || Āghavā āṅgī jaisā | vāyū miḷoni āhe ākāshā | tū sarva karmī taisā | majasīṅchi asa || Jñāne.18.1354 || Kiṁbahunā āpule mana | karī māĵhe ekāyatana | māĵheni shravaṇe kāna | bharūni ghālī || Jñāne.18.1355 || Ātmajñāne chokhaḍī | saṅta je mājhī rūpaḍī | tetha druṣhṭi paḍo āvaḍī | kāminī jaisī || Jñāne.18.1356 || Mī sarvavastīche vasauṭe | mājhī nāme jiye chokhaṭe | tiye jīvā yāvayā vāṭe | vāchechiye lāvī || Jñāne.18.1357 || Hātāche karaṇe | kā pāyāṅche chālaṇe | te hoya majakāraṇe | taise karī || Jñāne.18.1358 || [Madyājī] Āpulā athavā parāvā | ṭhāyī upakarasī Pāṅḍavā | teṇe yajñe hoyī baravā | yājñika mājhā || Jñāne.18.1359 || [Madbhaktaḥ] He yekaika shikaū kāī | pai sevakai āpulyā ṭhāī | uraūni yera sarvahī | mī sevyachi karī || Jñāne.18.1360 || [Māṁ(n) namaskuru] Tetha jāūni bhūtadweṣha | sarvatra namavainama mīchi yeka | aiseni āshraya ātyaṅtika | lāhasī tū mājhā || Jñāne.18.1361 || [Māmevaiṣhyasi] Maga bharaleyā jagāāṅta | jāūni tijayāchī māta | hoūni ṭhāyīla ekāṅta | āmhā tumhā || Jñāne.18.1362 || Tevhā bhalatiye avasthe | mī tūṅte tū māte | bhogisī aise āite | vāḍhela sukha || Jñāne.18.1363 || Āṇi tije āḍaḷa karite | nimāle Arjunā jethe | tai mīchi mhaṇauni tū māte | pāvasī shekhī || Jñāne.18.1364 || Jaisī jaḷīṅchī pratibhā | jaḷanāshī biṁbā | yetā gābhāgobhā | kāhī āhe || Jñāne.18.1365 || Pai pavana aṁbarā | kā kalloḷa sāgarā | miḷatā āḍavārā | koṇāchā gā || Jñāne.18.1366 || Mhaṇauni tū āṇi āmhī | he disatāhe dehadharmī | maga yayāchyā virāmī | mīchi hosī || Jñāne.18.1367 || [Satyaṁ(n) te] Yayā bolāmāĵhārī | hoya navhe ĵhaṇe karī | yetha āna āthī tarī | tujhīcha āṇa || Jñāne.18.1368 || [Pratijāne] Pai tujhī āṇa vāhaṇe | he ātmaliṅgāte shivaṇe | [priyo’si me] prītīchī jāti lājaṇe | āṭhavo nedī || Jñāne.18.1369 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Yerhavī veḍhūni prapaṅcha | jeṇe vishwābhāsa hā sācha | ājñechā naṭanācha | kāḷāte jiṇe || Jñāne.18.1370 || To deva mī satyasaṅkalpa | āṇi jagāchyā hitī bāpa | mā āṇechā ākṣhepa | kā karāvā || Jñāne.18.1371 || Pari Arjunā tuĵheni vedhe | miyā devapaṇāchī birude | sāṅḍilī gā mī ādhe | sagaḷeni tuvā || Jñāne.18.1372 || Pai kājā āpuliyā | rāvo āpalī āpaṇayā | āṇa vāhe dhanaṅjayā | taise he kī || Jñāne.18.1373 || Tetha Arjun mhaṇe deve | achāṭa he na bolāve | je āmache kāĵa nāve | tuĵheni eke || Jñāne.18.1374 || Yāvarī sāṅgo baisasī | kā sāṅgatā bhāṣhahī desī | yā tujhiyā vinodāsī | pāra āhe jī || Jñāne.18.1375 || Kamaḷavanā vikāshū | karī ravīchā eka aṁshū | tetha āghavāchi prakāshū | nitya deto || Jñāne.18.1376 || Pruthvī nivaūni sāgara | bharijatī yevaḍhe thora | varṣhe tetha miṣhāṅtara | chātaka kī || Jñāne.18.1377 || Mhaṇauni audāryā tuĵheyā | maĵa nimitta nā mhaṇāvayā | prāpti ase dānīrāyā | krupānidhī || Jñāne.18.1378 || Tava deva mhaṇatī rāhe | yā bolāchā prastāva nohe | pai māte pāvasī upāye | sāchachi yeṇe || Jñāne.18.1379 || Saiṅdhava siṅdhū paḍiliyā | ĵo kṣhaṇa rāhe dhanaṅjayā | teṇe virechi kī urāvayā | kāraṇa kāyī || Jñāne.18.1380 || Taise sarvatra bhajatā | sarva mī hotā ahaṅtā | niḥsheṣha jāūni tattwatā | mīchi hosī || Jñāne.18.1381 || Eva mājhiye prāptīvarī | karmālāgoni avadhārī | dāvilī tuĵa uĵarī | upāyāṅchī || Jñāne.18.1382 || [Chūrṇikā] Je ādhī tava Paṅḍusutā | sarva karme maĵa arpitā | sarvatra prasannatā | lāhije mājhī || Jñāne.18.1383 || Pāṭhī mājhyā iye prasādī | māĵhe jñāna ĵāya siddhī | teṇe miḷavije trishuddhī | swarūpī mājhyā || Jñāne.18.1384 || Maga Pārthā tiye ṭhāī | sādhya sādhana hoya nāhī | kiṅbahunā tuĵa kāhī | urechinā || Jñāne.18.1385 || Tarī sarva karme āpalī | tuvā sarvadā maĵa arpilī | teṇe prasannatā lādhalī | āji he mājhī || Jñāne.18.1386 || Mhaṇoni yeṇe pramādabaḷe | nave ĵuṅĵhācheni āḍaḷe | na ṭhākechi yekaveḷe | bhāḷalo tuĵa || Jñāne.18.1387 || Je saprapaṅcha ajñāna jāye | jeṇe yeka mī gochara hoye | te upapattīcheni upāye | Gītārūpa he || Jñāne.18.1388 || Miyā jñāna tuĵa āpule | nānāparī upadeshile | yeṇe ajñānajāta sāṅḍavale | dharmādharma je || Jñāne.18.1389 ||

Sarvadharmānparityajya māmekaṁ sharaṇaṁ vraja | ahaṁ(n) twā sarvapāpebhyo mokṣhayiṣhyāmi mā shuchaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.66 ||

[Sarvadharmānparityajya] Āshā jaisī duḥkhāte | vyālī niṅdā durite | he aso jaise dainyāte | durbhagatwa || Jñāne.18.1390 || Taise swarganarakasūchaka | ajñāna vyāle dharmādika | te sāṅḍūni ghālī ashekha | jñāne yeṇe || Jñāne.18.1391 || Hātī gheūni to dora | sāṅḍije jaisā sarpākāra | kā nidrātyāge gharāchāra | swapnīṅchā jaisā || Jñāne.18.1392 || Nā nā sāṅḍileni kavaḷe | chaṅdrīṅche dhupe pivaḷe | vyādhityāge kaḍuvāḷe- | paṇa mukhāche || Jñāne.18.1393 || Agā divasā pāṭhī deunī | mrugajaḷa ghāpe tyajūnī | kā kāṣhṭhatyāge vahnī | tyajije jaisā || Jñāne.18.1394 || Taise dharmādharmāche ṭavāḷa | dāvī ajñāna je kā mūḷa | te tyajūna tyajī sakaḷa | dharmajāta || Jñāne.18.1395 || [Māmekaṁ] Maga ajñāna nimāliyā | mīchi eka ase apaisayā | sanidra swapna gelayā | āpaṇape jaise || Jñāne.18.1396 || Taisā mī ekavāṅchūna kāhī | maga bhinnābhinna āna nāhī | so’haṅbodhe tayāchyā ṭhāyī | ananya hoya || Jñāne.18.1397 || [Sharaṇaṁ vraja] Pai āpaleni bhedeṁviṇa | māĵhe jāṇije je ekapaṇa | tayāchi nāṁva sharaṇa | maĵa yeṇe gā || Jñāne.18.1398 || Jaise ghaṭācheni nāshe | gaganī gagana praveshe | maĵa sharaṇa yeṇe taise | aikya karī || Jñāne.18.1399 || Suvarṇamaṇi sonayā | ye kalloḷa jaisā pāṇiyā | taisā maĵa dhanaṅjayā | sharaṇa ye tū || Jñāne.18.1400 || [Ahaṁ(n) twā sarvapāpebhyaḥ] Vāṅchūni sāgarāchyā poṭī | vaḍavānaḷa sharaṇa ālā kirīṭī | ĵāḷū na ṭake tayā goṭhī | vāḷūni de pā || Jñāne.18.1401 || Majahī sharaṇa righije | āṇi jīvatweṅchi asije | dhik bolī yiyā na laje | prajñā kevī || Jñāne.18.1402 || Agā prākrutāhī rāyā | āṅgī paḍe je dhanaṅjayā | te dāsiruṅhi kī tayā- | samāna hoya || Jñāne.18.1403 || Mā mī vishweshwara bheṭe | āṇi jīvagraṅthī na suṭe | he bola nako vokhaṭe | kānī lāū || Jñāne.18.1404 || Mhaṇauni mī hoūni māte | sevaṇe āhe āyite | taise karī hātā yete | jñāne yeṇe || Jñāne.18.1405 || Maga tākauniyā kāḍhile | loṇī māghaute tākī ghātale | pari na ghepechi kāhī kele | teṇe jevī || Jñāne.18.1406 || Taise adwayatwe maĵa | sharaṇa righāliyā tuĵa | dharmādharma he sahaja | lāgatīla nā || Jñāne.18.1407 || Loha ubhe khāya mātī | te parisāchiye saṅgatī | sone jālayā puḍhatī | na shivije maḷe || Jñāne.18.1408 || He aso kāṣhṭhāpāsonī | mathūni ghetalayā vahnī | maga kāṣhṭheṅhī koṅḍonī | na ṭake jaisā || Jñāne.18.1409 || Arjunā kāya dinakara | dekhata āhe āṅdhāra | kī prabodhī hoya gochara | swapnabhrama || Jñāne.18.1410 || Taise majasī yekavaṭaleyā | mī sarvarūpa vāṅchūniyā | āna kāhī urāvayā | kāraṇa ase || Jñāne.18.1411 || [Mokṣhayiṣhyāmi] Mhaṇauni tayāche kāhī | chiṅtī nā āpulyā ṭhāī | tuĵhe pāpapuṇya pāhī | mīchi hoīna || Jñāne.18.1412 || Tetha sarvabaṅdhalakṣhaṇe | pāpe urāve dujepaṇe | te mājhyā bodhī vāyāṇe | hoūni jāīla || Jñāne.18.1413 || Jaḷī paḍiliyā lavaṇā | sarvahī jaḷa hoya vichakṣhaṇā | tuĵa mī ananyasharaṇā | hoīna taisā || Jñāne.18.1414 || Yetuleni apaisayā | suṭalāchi āhāsi dhanaṅjayā | [mā shuchaḥ] gheī maĵa prakāshoniyā | soḍavīna tūte || Jñāne.18.1415 || Yākāraṇe puḍhatī | he ādhī na vāhe chittī | maĵa ekāsi ye sumatī | ĵāṇoni sharaṇa || Jñāne.18.1416 || Aise sarvarūparūpase | sarvadruṣhṭiḍoḷase | sarvadeshanivāse | bolile ShreeKriṣhṇe || Jñāne.18.1417 || [‘swānubhavasukhoktayaḥ’] Maga sāṁvaḷā sakaṅkaṇa | bāhu pasaroni dakṣhiṇa | āliṅgilā swasharaṇa | bhaktarāja to || Jñāne.18.1418 || Na pavatā jayāte | kākhe sūni buddhīte | bolaṇe māgaute | vosarale || Jñāne.18.1419 || Aise je kāhī yeka | bolā buddhīsihī aṭaka | te dyāvayā miṣha | kheṅvāche kele || Jñāne.18.1420 || Hrudayā hrudaya yeka ĵāle | ye hrudayīṅche te hrudayī ghātale | dwaita na moḍitā kele | āpaṇāaise Arjunā || Jñāne.18.1421 || Dīpe dīpa lāvilā | taisā pariṣhwaṅga to jālā | dwaita na moḍitā kelā | āpaṇape Pārth || Jñāne.18.1422 || Tevhā sukhāchā maga tayā | pūra ālā ĵo dhanaṅjayā | tetha vāḍa tarhī buḍoniyā | ṭhelā deva || Jñāne.18.1423 || Siṅdhu siṅdhute pāvo jāye | te pāvaṇe ṭhāke duṇā hoye | varī rige puravaṇiye | ākāshahī || Jñāne.18.1424 || Taise tayā doghāṅche miḷaṇe | doghā nāvare ĵāṇāve kavaṇe | kiṁbahunā Shreenārāyaṇe | vishwa koṅdale || Jñāne.18.1425 || [Gītāmāhātmyam] [‘gītāyāḥ(hā) garbhe trikāṇḍotpattiṁ vyākaroti’] eva vedāchee mūḷasūtra | sarvādhikāraikapavitra | ShreeKriṣhṇe Gītāshāstra | prakaṭa kele || Jñāne.18.1426 || Tetha Gītā mūḷa vedā | aise kevi pā āle bodhā | he mhaṇāla tarī prasiddhā | upapatti sāṅgo || Jñāne.18.1427 || Tarī jayāchyā niḥshwāsī | janma ĵhāle vedarāshī | to satyapratijña paijesī | bolilā swamukhe || Jñāne.18.1428 || Mhaṇauni vedā mūḷabhūta | Gītā mhaṇo he hoya uchita | āṇikahī yekī yetha | upapatti ase || Jñāne.18.1429 || Je na nashata swarūpe | jayāĉhā vistāra jetha lape | te tayāche mhaṇipe | bīja jagī || Jñāne.18.1430 || Tari kāṅḍatrayātmaka | shabdarāshī asheṣha | gītemāji ase rukha | bījī jaisā || Jñāne.18.1431 || Mhaṇauni vedāṅche bīja | Shreegītā hoya he maĵa | game āṇi sahaja | disatahī āhe || Jñāne.18.1432 || Je vedāṅche tinhī bhāga | gīte umaṭale asatī chāṅga | bhūṣhaṇaratnī sarvāṅga | shobhale jaise || Jñāne.18.1433 || Tiyeṅchi karmādike tinhī | kāṅḍe koṇakoṇe sthānī | gīte āhāti te nayanī | dākhaū āika || Jñāne.18.1434 || [‘gītāshāstrotpattyādiprastāvanā’] Tari pahilā ĵo adhyāva | to shāstra-pravruttiprastāva | dwitīyī sāṅkhyasadbhāva | praKāshilā || Jñāne.18.1435 || Mokṣhadānī swataṅtra | jñānapradhāna he shāstra | yetulāle dujī sūtra | ubhārile || Jñāne.18.1436 || [‘karmakāṇḍaṁ’] Maga ajñāne bāṅdhaleyā | mokṣhapadī baisāvayā | sādhanāraṅbha to trutīyā- | dhyāyī bolilā || Jñāne.18.1437 || Je dehābhimānabaṅdhe | sāṅḍūni kāmyaniṣhiddhe | vihita pari apramāde | anuṣhṭhāve || Jñāne.18.1438 || Aiseni sadbhāve karma karāve | hā tijā adhyāyī deve | nirṇaya kelā te ĵāṇāve | karmakāṅḍa yetha || Jñāne.18.1439 || [‘upāsanākāṇḍaṁ’] Āṇi techi nityādika | ajñānāche āvashyaka | ācharatā mochaka | keṁvī hoya pā || Jñāne.18.1440 || Aisī apekṣhā jāliyā | baddha mumukṣhute āliyā | deve brahmārpaṇatwe kriyā | sāṅgītalī || Jñāne.18.1441 || Je deha vāchā mānase | vihita nipaje je jaise | te eka īshwaroddeshe | kīje mhaṇītale || Jñāne.18.1442 || Hechi īshwarī karmayoge | bhajanakathanāche khāge | ādarile sheṣhabhāge | chaturthācheni || Jñāne.18.1443 || Te vishwarūpa akarāvā | adhyāya saṅpe ĵava aghavā | tava karme īsha bhajāvā | he je bolile || Jñāne.18.1444 || Te aṣhṭādhyāyī ughaḍa | ĵāṇa yethe devatākāṅḍa | shāstra sāṅgatase āḍa | moḍūni bole || Jñāne.18.1445 || [‘jñānakāṇḍaṁ’] Āṇi teṇechi īshaprasāde | Shreegurusaṁpradāyalabdhe | sācha jñāna udbodhe | kovaḷe je || Jñāne.18.1446 || Te adweṣhṭādiprabhrutikī | athavā amānitwādikī | vāḍhavije mhaṇauni lekhī | bārāvā gaṇū || Jñāne.18.1447 || To bārāvā adhyāya ādi | āṇi paṅdharāvā avadhi | jñānaphaḷapākasiddhi | nirūpaṇāsī || Jñāne.18.1448 || Mhaṇauni chahuṁhī iṁhī | ūrdhwamūḷāṅtī adhyāyī | jñānakāṅḍa ye ṭhāyī | nirūpije || Jñāne.18.1449 || Eva kāṅḍatrayarūpiṇī | shrutīcha he koḍisavāṇī | Gītāpadyaratnāchī leṇī | leyilī āhe || Jñāne.18.1450 || He aso kāṅḍatrayātmaka | shruti mokṣharūpa phaḷa yeka | bobhāve je āvashyaka | ṭhākāve mhaṇauni || Jñāne.18.1451 || [‘ṣhoḍashādyadhyāyatrayakāraṇaṁ(n) darshayati’] Tayācheni sādhana jñāneṁsī | vaira karī ĵo pratidivashī | to ajñānavarga ṣhoḍashī | pratipādije || Jñāne.18.1452 || Tochi shāstrāchā boḷāvā | ghevoni vairī jiṇāvā | hā niropa to satarāvā | adhyāya yetha || Jñāne.18.1453 || Aisā prathamālāgonī | satarāvā lāṇī karūnī | ātmaniḥshwāsa vivarūni | dāvilā deve || Jñāne.18.1454 || Tayā arthajātā asheṣhā | kelā tātparyāĉhā āvāṅkā | to hā aṭharāvā dekhā | kalashādhyāya || Jñāne.18.1455 || Eva sakaḷa sāṅkhyasiṅdhu | ShreeBhagawadgītāprabaṅdhu | hā audārye āgaḷā vedu | mūrta ĵāṇa || Jñāne.18.1456 || Veda saṁpanna hoya ṭhāī | pari krupaṇa aisā āna nāhī | je kānī lāgalā tihī | varṇāṅchyāchī || Jñāne.18.1457 || Yerā bhavavyathā ṭheliyā | strīshūdrādikā prāṇiyā | anavasara māṅḍūniyā | rāhilā āhe || Jñāne.18.1458 || Tarī maĵa pāhatā te māgīla uṇe | pheḍāvayā Gītāpaṇe | veda veṭhalā bhalateṇe | sevya hoāvayā || Jñāne.18.1459 || Nā he arthe rigoni manī | shravaṇe lāgoni kānī | japamiṣhe vadanī | vasoniyā || Jñāne.18.1460 || Ye gītechā pāṭha ĵo ĵāṇe | tayācheni sāṅgātīpaṇe | Gītā lihoni vāhaṇe | pustakamiṣhe || Jñāne.18.1461 || Aisaisā mīsakaṭā | saṅsārāchā chohaṭā | gavādi ghālīta chokhaṭā | mokṣhasukhāchī || Jñāne.18.1462 || Pari āKāshī vasāvayā | pruthvīvarī baisāvayā | ravidīptī rāhāṭāvayā | āvāra nabha || Jñāne.18.1463 || Tevi uttama adhama aise | sevitā kavaṇāteṅhī na puse | kaivalyadāne sarise | nivavīta jagā || Jñāne.18.1464 || Yālāgi māgilī kuṭī | bhyālā veda gītechyā poṭī | rigālā ātā gomaṭī | kīrti pātalā || Jñāne.18.1465 || Mhaṇauni vedāchī susevyatā | te he mūrta ĵāṇa Shreegītā | ShreeKriṣhṇe Paṅḍusutā | upadeshilī || Jñāne.18.1466 || Pari vatsācheni vorase | dubhate hoya gharoddeshe | ĵāle Pāṅḍavācheni miṣhe | jagaduddharaṇa || Jñāne.18.1467 || Chātakāchiye kaṇave | megha pāṇiyesi dhāṁve | tetha charāchara āghave | nivāle jevī || Jñāne.18.1468 || Kā ananyagatīkamaḷā- | lāgī sūrya ye veḷoveḷā | kī sukhiyā hoije ḍoḷā | tribhuvanīṅchā || Jñāne.18.1469 || Taise Arjunācheni vyāĵe | Gītā prakāshūni Shreerāje | saṅsārāyevaḍhe thora ojhe | pheḍile jagāche || Jñāne.18.1470 || Sarvashāstraratnadīptī | ujaḷitā hā trijagatī | sūrya navhe lakṣhmīpatī- | vaktrāKāshīṅchā || Jñāne.18.1471 || Bāpa kuḷa te pavitra | jethiṅchā Pārth yā jñānā pātra | jeṇe Gītā kele swataṅtra | āvāra jagā || Jñāne.18.1472 || [Chūrṇikā] He aso maga teṇe | sadgurushrīKriṣhṇe | Pārthāĉhe misaḷaṇe | āṇile dwaitā || Jñāne.18.1473 || Pāṭhī mhaṇatase Pāṅḍavā | shāstra he mānale kī jīvā | tetha yerū mhaṇe devā | āpuliyā krupā || Jñāne.18.1474 || Tari nidhāna ĵoḍāvayā | bhāgya ghaḍe gā dhanaṅjayā | pari ĵoḍile bhogāvayā | vipāye hoya || Jñāne.18.1475 || Pai kṣhīrasāgarāyevaḍhe | avirajī dudhāche bhāṅḍe | surā asurā kevaḍhe | mathitā ĵāle || Jñāne.18.1476 || Te sāhasahī phaḷā āle | je amrutahī ḍoḷā dekhile | pari varichila chukale | jatanene || Jñāne.18.1477 || Tetha amaratwā vogarile | te maraṇāchilāgī ĵāle | bhogo neṇatā ĵoḍale | aise āhe || Jñāne.18.1478 || Nahuṣha swargādhipati jālā | parī rāhāṭī bhāṁbāvalā | to bhujaṅgatwa pāvalā | neṇasī kāyī || Jñāne.18.1479 || Mhaṇauni bahuta puṇya tuvā | kele teṇe dhanaṅjayā | āji shāstrarājā iyā | jālāsi viṣhaya || Jñāne.18.1480 || Tari yayāchi shāstrāchenī | saṁpradāye pāṅghuraunī | shāstrārtha hā nikenī | anuṣhṭhī ho || Jñāne.18.1481 || Yerhavī amrutamathanā- | sārikhe hoīla Arjunā | jari righasī anuṣhṭhānā | saṁpradāyeṁvīṇa || Jñāne.18.1482 | Gāya dhaḍa ĵoḍe gomaṭī | te taiṅchi paya de kirīṭī | jai jāṇije hātavaṭī | sāṅjavaṇīchī || Jñāne.18.1483 || Taisā Shreeguru prasanna hoye | shiṣhya vidyāhī kīra lāhe | pari te phaḷe saṁpradāye | upāsiliyā || Jñāne.18.1484 || Mhaṇauni shāstrī ĵo iye | uchita saṁpradāya āhe | to aika ātā bahuve | ādaresī || Jñāne.18.1485 ||

Ida te nātapaskāya nābhaktāya kadāchana | na chāshushrūṣhave vāchya na cha mā yo’bhyasūyati || Bha.Gī.18.67 ||

[Idaṁ(n) te] Tari tuvā he je Pārthā | Gītāshāstra lādhale āsthā | [nātapaskāya] te tapohīnā sarvathā | [na] sāṅgāve nā ho || Jñāne.18.1486 || [Nābhaktāya] Athavā tāpasahī jālā | pari gurubhaktī ĵo ḍhilā | to vedī aṅtyaja vāḷilā | taisā vāḷī || Jñāne.18.1487 || Nā tari puroḍāshu jaisā | na ghāpe vruddha tarī vāyasā | Gītā nedī taisī tāpasā | gurubhaktihīnā || Jñāne.18.1488 || [Na chāshushrūṣhave vāchyaṁ] Kā tapahī ĵoḍe dehī | bhaje gurudevāṅchyā ṭhāī | pari ākarṇanī nāhī | ĉhāḍa ĵarī || Jñāne.18.1489 || Tari māgīla dohī āṅgī | uttama hoya kīra jagī | pari yā shravaṇālāgī | yogya nohe || Jñāne.18.1490 || Muktāphaḷa bhalataise | ho pari mukha nase | tava guṇa praveshe | tetha kāyī || Jñāne.18.1491 || Sāgara gaṁbhīra hoye | he koṇa nā mhaṇata āhe | pari vruṣhṭī vāyā jāye | jālī tetha || Jñāne.18.1492 || Dhāliyā divyānna suvāve | maga je vāyā dhāḍāve | te ārtī kā na karāve | udārapaṇa || Jñāne.18.1493 || [Kadāchana] Mhaṇauni yogya bhalataise | hota parī ĉhāḍa nase | tari ĵhaṇe vānivase | desī he tayā || Jñāne.18.1494 || Rūpāchā suĵāṇa ḍoḷā | voḍavū ye kāyi parimaḷā | jetha je māne te phaḷā | tethachi ye gā || Jñāne.18.1495 || Mhaṇauni tapī bhakti | pāhāve te Subhadrāpatī | pari shāstrashravaṇī anāsakti | vāḷāvechi te || Jñāne.18.1496 || [Na cha māṁ yo’bhyasūyati] Nā tarī tapabhakti | hoūni shravaṇī ārti | āthī aisī hī āyatī | dekhasī ĵarī || Jñāne.18.1497 || Tarī Gītāshāstranirmitā | ĵo mī sakaḷalokashāstā | tayā māte sāmānyatā | bolela ĵo || Jñāne.18.1498 || Mājhyā sajjaneṁsi māte | paishunyācheni āvhāte | yeka āhātī tayāte | yogya na mhaṇa || Jñāne.18.1499 || Tayāṅchī yera āghavī | sāmagrī aisī jāṇāvī | dīpeṅvīṇa ṭhāṇadivī | rātrīchī jaisī || Jñāne.18.1500 || Aṅga gore āṇi taruṇe | vari leyile āhe leṇe | pari yekaleni prāṇe | sāṅḍile jevī || Jñāne.18.1501 || Sonayāche suṅdara | nirvāḷile hoya ghara | pari sarpāṅganā dwāra | ruṅdhale āhe || Jñāne.18.1502 || Nipaje divyānna chokhaṭa | pari mājī kāḷakūṭa | aso maitrī kapaṭa- | garbhiṇī jaisī || Jñāne.18.1503 || Taisī tapabhaktimedhā | tayāchī ĵāṇa prabuddhā | ĵo mājhayāṅchī kā niṅdā | mājhīchi karī || Jñāne.18.1504 || Yākāraṇe dhanaṅjayā | to bhakta medhāvī tapiyā | tari nako bāpā iyā | shāstrā ātaḷo devo || Jñāne.18.1505 || Kāya bahu bolo niṅdakā | yogya sraṣhṭayāhīsārikhā | Gītā he kavatikā- | lāgīṅhī nedī || Jñāne.18.1506 || [Chūrṇikā] Mhaṇauni tapāchā dhanurdharā | taḷī dāṭoni gāḍorā | vari gurubhaktīchā purā | prāsāda ĵo jālā || Jñāne.18.1507 || Āṇi shravaṇechchhechā puḍhā | dāravaṅṭā sadā ughaḍā | varī kalasha chokhaḍā | aniṅdāratnāṅchā || Jñāne.18.1508 ||

Ya idaṁ paramaṁ(ṅ) guhyaṁ madbhakteṣhwabhidhāsyati | bhaktiṁ mayi parāṁ(ṅ) krutwā māmevaiṣhyatyasaṁshayaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.68 ||

[Ya idaṁ paramaṁ(ṅ) guhyaṁ] Aishā bhaktālayī chokhaṭī | Gītāratneshwara hā pratiṣhṭhī | maga mājhiyā saṁvasāṭī | tukasī jagī || Jñāne.18.1509 || Kā je ekākṣharapaṇeṁsī | trimātrakechiye kushī | praṇava hotā garbhavāsī | sāṅkaḍalā || Jñāne.18.1510 || To gītechiyā bāhaḷī | vedabīja gele pālhāḷī | kī gāyatrī phulī phaḷī | shlokāṅchyā ālī || Jñāne.18.1511 || Te he maṅtrarahasya Gītā | meḷavī ĵo mājhiyā bhaktā | ananyajīvanā mātā | bāḷakā jaisī || Jñāne.18.1512 || [Madbhakteṣhwabhidhāsyati] Taisī bhaktā gītesī | bheṭī karī ĵo ādaresī | to [māmevaiṣhyatyasaṁshayaḥ] dehāpāṭhī majasī | yekachi hoya || Jñāne.18.1513 ||

Na cha tasmānmanuṣhyeṣhu kashchinme priyakruttamaḥ | bhavitā na cha me tasmādanyaḥ(ph) priyataro bhuvi || Bha.Gī.18.69 ||

[Tasmāt] Āṇi dehācheṁhī leṇe | leūni vegaḷepaṇe | ase tava jīve prāṇe | tochi paḍhiye || Jñāne.18.1514 || [Manuṣhyeṣhu] Jñāniyā karmaṭhā tāpasā | yayā khuṇechiyā māṇusāṁ- | māji to eka gā jaisā | paḍhiye maĵa || Jñāne.18.1515 || [Na cha] Taisā bhūtaḷī āghavā | āna na dekhe Pāṅḍavā | ĵo Gītā sāṅge meḷāvā | bhaktajanāṅchā || Jñāne.18.1516 || [Bhaktiṁ mayi parāṁ(ṅ) krutwā iti pūrvashlokasthaṁ padaṁ] Maĵa īshwarācheni lobhe | he Gītā paḍhatā akṣhobhe | ĵo maṅḍana hoya sabhe | saṅtāṅchiye || Jñāne.18.1517 || Navapallavī romāṅchita | maṅdāniḷe kāṁpavita | āmodajaḷe vosaṅḍata | phulāṅche ḍoḷe || Jñāne.18.1518 || Kokiḷā kalaravācheni miṣhe | sadgada bolavita jaise | vasaṅta kā praveshe | madbhaktaārāmī || Jñāne.18.1519 || Kā janmāche phaḷa chakorā | hota jai chaṅdra ye aṁbarā | nā nā navaghana mayūrā | vo deta pāve || Jñāne.18.1520 || [Kashchinme priyakruttamaḥ] Taisā sajjanāṅchyā meḷāpī | Gītāpadyaratnī umapī | varṣhe ĵo mājhyā rūpī | hetu ṭheūni || Jñāne.18.1521 || [Bhaviteti] Maga tayācheni pāḍe | paḍhiyaṅte majaphuḍe | nāhīṅchi gā māgeṁphuḍe | nyāhāḷitā || Jñāne.18.1522 || [Chūrṇikā] Arjunā hā ṭhāyavarī | mī tayāte sūye jivhārī | ĵo Gītārthāche karī | paraguṇe saṅtā || Jñāne.18.1523 ||

Adhyeṣhyate cha ya imaṁ(n) dharmyaṁ saṁvādamāvayoḥ | jñānayajñena tenāhamiṣhṭaḥ(s) syāmiti me matiḥ(hi) || Bha.Gī.18.70 ||

[Adhyeṣhyate iti] Pai mājhiyā tujhiyā miḷaṇī | vāḍhīnalī je he kāhāṇī | mokṣhadharma kā jiṇī | ālāse jethe || Jñāne.18.1524 || To hā sakaḷārthaprada | āmhā doghāṅchā saṁvāda | na karitā padabheda | pāṭhechi ĵo paḍhe || Jñāne.18.1525 || [Jñānayajñeneti] Teṇe jñānānaḷī pradīptī | mūḷa avidyechiyā āhutī | toṣhavilā hoya sumatī | paramātmā mī || Jñāne.18.1526 || Gheūni Gītārtha ugāṇā | jñāniye je vichakṣhaṇā | ṭhākitī te gāṇāvāṇā | gītechā to lāhe || Jñāne.18.1527 || Gītāpāṭhakāsi ase | phaḷa arthajñāchi-sarise | Gītā māuliye kī nase | ĵāṇe tānhe || Jñāne.18.1528 ||

Shraddhāvānanasūyashcha shrruṇuyādapi yo naraḥ | so’pi muktaḥ(sh) shubhāँllokānprāpnuyātpuṇyakarmaṇām || Bha.Gī.18.71 ||

[Shraddhāvānanasūyashcha] Āṇi sarvamārgī niṅdā | sāṅḍūni āsthā pai shuddhā | Gītāshravaṇī shraddhā | ubhārī ĵo || Jñāne.18.1529 || [Shrruṇuyādapi yo naraḥ] Tayāchyā shravaṇapuṭī | gītechī akṣhare ĵava paiṭhī | hotī nā tava uṭhāuṭhī | paḷechi pāpa || Jñāne.18.1530 || [Puṇyakarmaṇāṁ] Aṭavīyemājī jaisā | vahni righatā sahasā | laṅghitī kā dishā | vanauke tiye || Jñāne.18.1531 || Kā udayāchaḷakuḷī | jhaḷakatā aṁshumāḷī | timire aṅtarāḷī | hārapatī || Jñāne.18.1532 || Taisā kānāchyā mahādwārī | Gītā gajara jetha karī | tetha sruṣhṭīchiye ādivarī | ĵāyachi pāpa || Jñāne.18.1533 || Aisī janmavallī dhuvaṭa | hoya puṇyarūpa chokhaṭa | yāhīvarī achāṭa | lāhe phaḷa || Jñāne.18.1534 || Je iye gītechī akṣhare | jetulī kā Karṇadwāre | righatī tetule hotī pure | ashwamedha kī || Jñāne.18.1535 || Mhaṇauni shravaṇe pāpe jātī | [shubhāँllokānprāpnuyāt] āṇi dharma dharī unnatī | teṇe swargarājya saṁpattī | lāhechi shekhī || Jñāne.18.1536 || [So’pi muktaḥ] To pai maĵa yāvayālāgī | pahile peṇe karī swargī | maga āvaḍe tava bhogī | pāṭhī majachi miḷe || Jñāne.18.1537 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Aisī Gītā dhanaṅjayā | aikatayā āṇi paḍhatayā | phaḷe mahānaṅde miyā | bahu kāya bolo || Jñāne.18.1538 || [Chūrṇikā] Yākāraṇe he aso | pari jayālāgī shāstrātiso | kelā te tava tuĵa puso | kāĵa tuĵhe || Jñāne.18.1539 ||

Kachchidetachchhrutaṁ Pārth twayaikāgreṇa chetasā | kachchidajñānasammohaḥ(ph) pranaṣhṭaste Dhanañjaya || Bha.Gī.18.72 ||

[Kachchidetachchhrutaṁ Pārtheti] Tari sāṅga pā Pāṅḍavā | hā shāstrasiddhāṅta āghavā | tuĵa ekachitte phāvā | gelā āhe || Jñāne.18.1540 || Āmhī jaise jayā rītī | ugāṇile kānāṅchyā hātī | yerī taiseṅchi tujhyā chittī | paiṭhe kele kī || Jñāne.18.1541 || Athavā māĵhārī | gele sāṅḍīvikhurī | kiṁvā upekṣhevarī | vāḷūni sāṅḍile || Jñāne.18.1542 || Jaise āmhī sāṅgītale | taiseṅchi hrudayī phāvale | tarī sāṅga pā vahile | pusena te mī || Jñāne.18.1543 || [Kachchidajñānasammoha iti] Tarī swājñānajanite | māgile mohe tūte | bhulavile to yethe | ase kī nāhī || Jñāne.18.1544 || He bahu puso kāī | sāṅge tū āpulyā ṭhāī | karmākarma kāhī | dekhatāsī || Jñāne.18.1545 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Pārth swānaṅdaikarase | virela aisā bhedadashe | āṇilā yeṇe miṣhe | prashnācheni || Jñāne.18.1546 || Pūrṇabrahma jālā Pārth | tarī puḍhīla sādhāvayā kāryārtha | maryādā ShreeKriṣhṇanātha | ullaṅgho nedī || Jñāne.18.1547 || Yerhavī āpale karaṇe | sarvajña kāya to neṇe | pari kele pusaṇe | yāchilāgī || Jñāne.18.1548 || Eva karoniyā prashna | nasatechi Arjunapaṇa | āṇūniyā ĵāle pūrṇapaṇa | te bolavī swaye || Jñāne.18.1549 || [Chūrṇikā] Maga kṣhīrābdhīte sāṅḍita | gaganī puṅja maṅḍita | nivaḍe jaisā na nivaḍita | pūrṇachaṅdra || Jñāne.18.1550 || Taisā brahma mī he visare | tetha jagachi brahmatwe bhare | heṁhī sāṅḍī tarī vire | brahmapaṇahī || Jñāne.18.1551 || Aisā moḍata māṅḍata brahme | to duḥkhe dehāchiye sīme | mī Arjun yeṇe nāme | ubhā ṭhelā || Jñāne.18.1552 || Maga kāṅpatā karataḷī | daḍapūni romāvaḷī | pulaku swedajaḷī | jiraūniyā || Jñāne.18.1553 || Prāṇakṣhobhe ḍolatayā | āṅgā āṅgachi ṭeṅkayā- | sūni staṅbha chāḷayā | bhulauniyā || Jñāne.18.1554 || Netrayuguḷācheni vote | ānaṅdāmrutāche bharite | vosaṅḍata te māgute | kāḍhūniyā || Jñāne.18.1555 || Vividhā autsukyāṅchī dāṭī | chīpa dāṭata hotī kaṅṭhī | te karūniyā paiṭhī | hrudayāmājī || Jñāne.18.1556 || Vācheche vituḷaṇe | sāṁvarūni prāṇe | akramāche shwasaṇe | ṭheūni ṭhāyī || Jñāne.18.1557 ||

Arjuna uvācha - Naṣhṭo mohaḥ(s) smrutirlabdhā twatprasādānmayāchyuta | sthito’smi gatasandehaḥ(kh) kariṣhye vachanaṁ(n) tava || Bha.Gī.18.73 ||

[Naṣhṭo mohaḥ] Maga Arjun mhaṇe kāya devo | pusatāti āvaḍe moho | tarī to sakuṭuṅba gelā jī ṭhāvo | gheūni āpalā || Jñāne.18.1558 || Pāsī yeūni dinakare | ḍoḷayāte āṅdhāre | pusije he kāyi sare | koṇe gāṁvī || Jñāne.18.1559 || Taisā tū ShreeKriṣhṇarāyā | āmuchiyā ḍoḷayā | gochara hechi kāyisayā | na pure tava || Jñāne.18.1560 || Vari lobhe māyepāsūni | te sāṅgasī toṅḍa bharūni | je kāyīsenihī karūni | jāṇū naye || Jñāne.18.1561 || Ātā moha ase kī nāhī | he aise jī pusasī kāī | krutakrutya jāhalo pāhī | tuĵhepaṇe || Jñāne.18.1562 || Guṅtalo hoto Arjunaguṇe | to mukta jhālo tuĵhepaṇe | ātā pusaṇe sāṅgaṇe | donhī nāhī || Jñāne.18.1563 || [Twatprasādānmayāchyuta] Mī tuĵheni prasāde | lādhaleni ātmabodhe | mohāche tayā kāṅde | nedīcha uro || Jñāne.18.1564 || [Smrutirlabdhā] Ātā karaṇe kā na karaṇe | he jeṇe uṭhī dujepaṇe | te tūṅvāṅchūni neṇe | sarvatra gā || Jñāne.18.1565 || [Sthito’smi gatasandehaḥ] Yeviṣhayī mājhyā ṭhāyī | saṅdehāche nurechi kāhī | trishuddhī karma jetha nāhī | te mī jālo || Jñāne.18.1566 || Tuĵheni maĵa mī pāvonī | kartavya nele nipaṭūni | [kariṣhye vachanaṁ(n) tava] pari ājñā tujhīvāṅchonī | āna nāhī prabho || Jñāne.18.1567 || Kā je drushya drushyāte nāshī | je duje dwaitāte grasī | je eka pari sarvadeshī | vasavī sadā || Jñāne.18.1568 || Jayāĉheni saṁbaṅdhe baṅdha phiṭe | jayāchiyā āshā āsa tuṭe | je bheṭalayā sarva bheṭe | āpaṇapāṅchi || Jñāne.18.1569 || Te tū guruliṅga jī māĵhe | je yekalepaṇīṅche viraje | jayālāgī volāṅḍije | adwaitabodha || Jñāne.18.1570 || Āpaṇachi hoūni brahma | sārije krutyākrutyāche kāma | maga kīje kā niḥsīma | sevā jayāchī || Jñāne.18.1571 || Gaṅgā siṅdhu sevū gelī | pāvatāṅchi samudra jālī | tevī bhaktā sela didhalī | nijapadāchī || Jñāne.18.1572 || To tū mājhā jī nirupachārū | ShreeKriṣhṇā sevya sadgurū | mā brahmatechā upakārū | hāchi mānī || Jñāne.18.1573 || Je maĵa tumhā āḍa | hote bhedāche kavāḍa | te pheḍoni kele goḍa | sevāsukha || Jñāne.18.1574 || Tarī ātā tujhī ājñā | sakaḷa devādhidevarājñā | karīna deyī anujñā | bhalatiyeviṣhayī || Jñāne.18.1575 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Yayā Arjunāchiyā bolā | deva nāche sukhe bhulalā | mhaṇe vishwaphaḷā jālā | phaḷa hā maĵa || Jñāne.18.1576 || Uṇeni umachalā sudhākara | dekhunī āpalā kumara | maryādā kṣhīrasāgara | visarechinā || Jñāne.18.1577 || [Chūrṇikā] Aise saṁvādāchā bahulā | lagna doghāṅchiyā āṅtulā | lāgale dekhoni jālā | nirbhara Saṅjay || Jñāne.18.1578 || Teṇe mhaṇatase Saṅjayo | bāpa krupānidhī rāvo | to āpulā manobhāvo | Arjuneṅsī kelā || Jñāne.18.1579 || Teṇe uchaṁbaḷalepaṇe | Saṅjay Dhrutarāṣhtrāte mhaṇe | jī kaise bādarāyaṇe | rakṣhilo doghe || Jñāne.18.1580 || Āji tumate avadhārā | nāhī charmachakṣhuhī saṁsārā | kī jñānadruṣhṭī vyavahārā | āṇileti || Jñāne.18.1581 || Āṇi rathīṅchiye rāhāṭī | gheī ĵo ghoḍeyāsāṭhī | tayā āmhā yā goṣhṭī | gocharā hotī || Jñāne.18.1582 || Varī juṅjhāche nirvāṇa | māṅḍale ase dāruṇa | dohī hārī āpaṇa | hārapije jaise || Jñāne.18.1583 || Yevaḍhā jiye sāṅkaḍā | kaisā anugraho pai gāḍhā | je brahmānaṅda ughaḍā | bhogavītase || Jñāne.18.1584 || Aise Saṅjay bolilā | pari na drave yeru ugalā | chaṅdrakiraṇī shivatalā | pāṣhāṇa jaisā || Jñāne.18.1585 || He dekhoni tayāchī dashā | maga karīchinā sarisā | pari sukhe jālā pisā | bolatase || Jñāne.18.1586 || Bhulavilā harṣhavege | mhaṇauni Dhrutarāṣhtrā sāṅge | yerhavī navhe tayāĵoge | he kīra ĵāṇe || Jñāne.18.1587 ||

Sañjay uvācha - Ityahaṁ vāsudevasya Pārthasya cha mahātmanaḥ | saṁvādamimamashrauṣhamadbhutaṁ romaharṣhaṇam || Bha.Gī.18.74 ||

[Iti] Maga mhaṇe pai kururājā | aisā bhrātruputra to tujhā | bolilā te adhokṣhajā | goḍa ĵāle || Jñāne.18.1588 || [Mahātmanaḥ iti KriṣhṇaPārthayorvisheṣhaṇaṁ] Agā pūrvāpara sāgara | yayā nāmāsīchi sināra | yera āghave te nīra | eka jaise || Jñāne.18.1589 || Taisā ShreeKriṣhṇa Pārth aise | he āṅgāchipāsī dise | maga saṅvādī jī nase | kāṁhīṅchi bheda || Jñāne.18.1590 || Pai darpaṇāhūni chokhe | donhī hotī sanmukhe | tetha yerī yera dekhe | āpaṇape jaise || Jñāne.18.1591 || [Saṁvādaṁ] Taisā deveṁsī Paṅḍusuta | āpaṇape devī dekhata | Pāṅḍaveṅsī dekhe anaṅta | āpaṇape Pārthī || Jñāne.18.1592 || Deva devā bhaktālāgī | jiye vivara dekhe āṅgī | yeru tiyechihī bhāgī | donhī dekhe || Jñāne.18.1593 || Āṇika kāhīṅchi nāhī | mhaṇauni karitī kāī | doghe yekapaṇe pāhī | nāṅdatātī || Jñāne.18.1594 || Ātā bheda ĵarī moḍe | tarī prashnottara kā ghaḍe | nā bhedachi tari ĵoḍe | saṁvādasukha kā || Jñāne.18.1595 || Aise bolatā dujepaṇe | saṅvādī dwaita giḷaṇe | [imamashrauṣha] te aikile bolaṇe | doghāṅche miyā || Jñāne.18.1596 || Uṭūni donhī ārase | voḍaviliyā sarise | koṇa koṇā pāhātase | kalpāve pā || Jñāne.18.1597 || Kā dīpāsanmukha | ṭheviliyā dīpaka | koṇa koṇā arthika | koṇa ĵāṇe || Jñāne.18.1598 || Nā nā arkāpuḍhe arka | udayaliyā āṇika | koṇa mhaṇe prakāshaka | prakāshya kavaṇa || Jñāne.18.1599 || [Adbhutaṁ] He nirdhārū jātā phuḍe | nirdhārāsi ṭhaka paḍe | te doghe ĵāle yevaḍhe | saṁvāde sarise || Jñāne.18.1600 || [Ahaṁ] Jī miḷatā donhī udakeṁ- | māji lavaṇa vāru ṭhāke | kī tayāsīhī nimikhe | techi hoya || Jñāne.18.1601 || Taise ShreeKriṣhṇa Arjun donhī | saṁvādale te manī | dharitā majahī vānī | techi hotase || Jñāne.18.1602 || Aise mhaṇe nā moṭake | tava hironi sāttwike | āṭhava nelā neṇo ke | Saṅjayapaṇāchā || Jñāne.18.1603 || [Romaharṣhaṇaṁ] Romāṅcha ĵava pharake | tava tava āṅga surake | staṅbhaswedāṅte jiṅke | ekalā kaṁpa || Jñāne.18.1604 || Adwayānaṅdasparshe | diṭhī rasamaya jālī ase | te ashru navhatī jaise | dravatwachi || Jñāne.18.1605 || Neṇo kāya na māya poṭī | kāya neṇo guṅphe kaṅṭhī | vāgarthā paḍata miṭhī | usasāchiyā || Jñāne.18.1606 || Kiṁbahunā sāttwikā āṭhā | chāchara māṅḍatā umeṭhā | Saṅjay ĵāhalāse chohaṭā | saṁvādasukhāchā || Jñāne.18.1607 || Tayā sukhāchī aisī jātī | je āpaṇachi dharī shāṅtī | maga puḍhatī dehasmrutī | lādhalī teṇe || Jñāne.18.1608 ||

Vyāsaprasādāchchhrutavānetadguhyamahaṁ param | yogaṁ yogeshwarātKriṣhṇātsākṣhātkathayataḥ(s) swayam || Bha.Gī.18.75 ||

[Vyāsaprasādāchchhrutavān] Tevhā baisateni ānaṅde | mhaṇe jī je upaniṣhade | neṇatī te Vyāsaprasāde | aikile miyā || Jñāne.18.1609 || [Etadguhyamahaṁ] Aikatāṅchi te goṭhī | brahmatwāchī paḍilī miṭhī | mītūṅpaṇeṅsī diṭhī | vironi gelī || Jñāne.18.1610 || [Yogaṁ yogeshwarātKriṣhṇāt] He āghavechi kā yoga | jayā ṭhāyā yete mārga | tayāche vākya savaṅga | kele maĵa Vyāse || Jñāne.18.1611 || [Sākṣhātkathayataḥ(s) swayaṁ] Aho Arjunācheni miṣhe | āpaṇapeṅchi duje aise | naṭoni āpaṇayā uddeshe | bolile je deva || Jñāne.18.1612 || [Ayaṁ bhāvaḥ] Tetha kī māĵhe shrotra | pāṭāche ĵāle jī pātra | kāya vānū swataṅtra | sāmarthya Shreegurūṅche || Jñāne.18.1613 ||

Rājansaṁsmrutya saṁsmrutya saṁvādamimamadbhutam | keshavārjunayoḥ(ph) puṇyaṁ hruṣhyāmi cha muhurmuhuḥ(hu) || Bha.Gī.18.76 ||

[Rājan iti spaṣhṭaṁ imaṁ adbhutaṁ] Rāyā he bolatā vismita hoye | [keshavārjunayoḥ(ph) puṇyaṁ] teṇechi moḍāvalā ṭhāye | ratnī kī ratnakiḷā ye | jhāṅkoḷita jaisī || Jñāne.18.1614 || [Hruṣhyāmi cha muhurmuhuḥ(hu)] Himavaṅtīṅchī sarovare | chaṅdrodayī hotī kāshmīre | maga sūryāgamī māghāre | dravatwa ye || Jñāne.18.1615 || [Saṁsmrutya saṁsmrutya saṁvādaṁ] Taisā sharīrāchiyā smrutī | to saṁvāda Saṅjay chittī | dharī āṇi puḍhatī | techi hoya || Jñāne.18.1616 ||

Tachcha saṁsmrutya saṁsmrutya rūpamatyadbhutaṁ hareḥ | vismayo me mahānrājanhruṣhyāmi cha punaḥ(ph) punaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.77 ||

[Rājan] Maga uṭhoni mhaṇe nrupā | [tachcheti] Shreeharīchiyā vishwarūpā | dekhilayā ugā kā pā | aso lāhasī || Jñāne.18.1617 || Na dekhaṇeni je dise | nāhīṅpaṇeṅchi je ase | visare āṭhave te kaise | chukavū ātā || Jñāne.18.1618 || [Vismayo me mahān] Dekhoni chamatkāra | kīje to nāhī paisāra | majahī sakaṭa mahāpura | neta āhe || Jñāne.18.1619 || Aisā ShreeKriṣhṇārjuna- | saṁvādasaṅgamī snāna | karūni detase tiḷadāna | ahaṅteche || Jñāne.18.1620 || [Hruṣhyāmi cha punaḥ(ph) punaḥ] Tetha asaṁvare ānaṅde | alaukikahī kāhī sphuṅde | ShreeKriṣhṇa mhaṇe sadgade | veḷoveḷā || Jñāne.18.1621 || Yā avasthāṅchī kāhī | Kauravāte parī nāhī | mhaṇauni rāye te kāhī | kalpāve ĵava || Jñāne.18.1622 || Tava jālā sukhalābha | āpaṇapā karūni swayaṁbha | bujhāvilā avaṣhṭaṁbha | Saṅjaye teṇe || Jñāne.18.1623 || Tetha koṇī yekī avasarī | hoāvī te karūni durī | rāvo mhaṇe Saṅjayā parī | kaisī tujhī gā || Jñāne.18.1624 || Teṇe tūṅte yethe Vyāse | baisavile kāsayā uddeshe | aprasaṅgāmāji aise | bolasī kāī || Jñāne.18.1625 || Rānīṅche rāūḷā neliyā | dāhī dishā mānī suniyā | kā rātrī hoya pāhalayā | nishācharā || Jñāne.18.1626 || Ĵo jethiṅche gaurava neṇe | tayāsi te bhiṅguḷavāṇe | mhaṇauni aprasaṅga teṇe | mhaṇāvā kī to || Jñāne.18.1627 || Maga mhaṇe sāṅge prastuta | udayaleṅse je utkaḷita | te koṇāsi bā re jaita | deīla shekhī || Jñāne.18.1628 || Yerhavī visheṣhe bahuteka | āmuche aise mānasika | je Duryodhanāche adhika | pratāpa sadā || Jñāne.18.1629 || Āṇi yerāṅcheni pāḍe | daḷahī yāche devhaḍe | mhaṇauni jaita phuḍe | āṇīla nā te || Jñāne.18.1630 || Āmhā tava game aise | mā tuĵhe ĵotiṣha kaise | te neṇo Saṅjayā ase | taise sāṅga pā || Jñāne.18.1631 ||

Yatra yogeshwaraḥ(kh) Kriṣhṇo yatra Pārtho dhanurdharaḥ | tatra Shreervijayo bhūtirdhruvā nītirmatirmama || Bha.Gī.18.78 || Oṁ tatsaditi ShreemadBhagawadgītāsūpaniṣhatsu brahmavidyāyāṁ yogashāstre ShreeKriṣhṇārjunasaṁvāde mokṣhasaṁ(n)nyāsayogo nāmāṣhṭādasho’dhyāyaḥ || Bha.Gī.18.puṣhpikā ||

[Yatra yogeshwaraḥ(kh) Kriṣhṇo] Yayā bolā Saṅjayo mhaṇe | jī yerayerāṅche mī neṇe | pari āyuṣhya tethe jiṇe | he phuḍe kī gā || Jñāne.18.1632 || Chaṅdra tethe chaṅdrikā | shaṅbhu tethe aṁbikā | saṅta tethe vivekā | asaṇe kī jī || Jñāne.18.1633 || Rāvo tethe kaṭaka | saujanya tethe soirīka | vahni tethe dāhaka | sāmarthya kī || Jñāne.18.1634 || Dayā tethe dharma | dharma tethe sukhāgama | sukhī puruṣhottama | ase jaisā || Jñāne.18.1635 || Vasaṅta tethe vane | vana tetha sumane | sumanī pāliṅgane | sāraṅgāṅchī || Jñāne.18.1636 || Guru tetha jñāna | jñānī ātmadarshana | darshanī samādhāna | āthī jaise || Jñāne.18.1637 || Bhāgya tetha vilāsa | sukha tethe ullāsa | he aso tetha prakāsha | sūrya jethe || Jñāne.18.1638 || Taise sakaḷa puruṣhārtha | jeṇe swāmī kā sanātha | to ShreeKriṣhṇa rāvo jetha | [tatra Shreeḥ(hi)] tetha lakṣhmī || Jñāne.18.1639 || [Bhūtiḥ(hi)] Āṇi āpaleni kāṅtesī | te jagadaṅbā jayāpāsī | aṇimādikī kāya dāsī | navhatī tayāte || Jñāne.18.1640 || [Vijayaḥ] Kriṣhṇa vijayaswarūpa nijāṅge | to rāhilā ase jeṇe bhāge | tai jaya lāgavege | tethechi āhe || Jñāne.18.1641 || [Yatra Pārtho dhanurdharaḥ] Vijayī nāme Arjun vikhyāta | vijayaswarūpa ShreeKriṣhṇanātha | shriyesī vijaya nishchita | tethechi ase || Jñāne.18.1642 || Tayāchiye deshīṅchyā jhāḍī | kalpatarūte hoḍī | na jiṇāve kā yevaḍhī | māyabāpe asatā || Jñāne.18.1643 || Te pāṣhāṇahī āghave | chiṅtāratne kā nohāve | tiye bhūmike kā na yāve | suvarṇatwa || Jñāne.18.1644 || Tayāchiyā gāṁvīṅchiyā | nadī amrute vāhāviyā | navala kāya rāyā | vichārī pā || Jñāne.18.1645 || Tayāche bisāṭa shabda | sukhe mhaṇo yetī veda | sadeha sachchidānaṅda | kā nohāve te || Jñāne.18.1646 || Pai swargāpavarga donhī | iye pade tayā adhīnī | ShreeKriṣhṇa bāpa jananī | kamaḷā jayā || Jñāne.18.1647 || Mhaṇauni jiyā bāhī ubhā | to lakṣhmīyechā vallabhā | tetha sarvasiddhi swayaṁbhā | yera mī neṇe || Jñāne.18.1648 || Āṇi samudrāchā megha | upayoge tayāhūni chāṅga | taisā Pārthī āji lāga | āhe taye || Jñāne.18.1649 || Kanakatwadīkṣhāgurū | lohā parīsa hoya kīrū | pari jagā positā vyavahārū | techi ĵāṇe || Jñāne.18.1650 || Yetha gurutwā yetase uṇe | aise ĵhaṇe koṇhī mhaṇe | vahni prakāsha dīpapaṇe | praKāshī āpalā || Jñāne.18.1651 || Taisā devāchiyā shaktī | Pārth devāsīcha bahutī | parī māne iye stutī | gaurava ase || Jñāne.18.1652 || Āṇi putre mī sarva guṇī | jiṇāvā he bāpā shirāṇī | tarī te Shāraṅggapāṇī | phaḷā ālī || Jñāne.18.1653 || Kiṁbahunā aisā nrupā | Pārth jālāse Kriṣhṇakrupā | to jayākaḍe sākṣhepā | rītī āhe || Jñāne.18.1654 || Tochi gā vijayāsi ṭhāvo | yetha tuĵa koṇa saṅdeho | tetha na ye tarī vāvo | vijayochi hoya || Jñāne.18.1655 || Mhaṇauni jetha Shree tetha Shreemaṅta | jetha to paṅḍūchā suta | tetha vijaya samasta | abhyudaya tetha || Jñāne.18.1656 || [Dhruvā] Ĵarī Vyāsācheni sāche | dhire mana tumache | tari yā bolāche | dhruvachi mānā || Jñāne.18.1657 || [Nītiḥ(hi)] Jetha to Shreevallabha | tetha bhaktakadaṁba | tetha sukha āṇi lābha | maṅgaḷāchā || Jñāne.18.1658 || [Matirmama] Yā bolā āna hoye | tarī Vyāsāchā aṅka na vāhe | aise gāĵoni bāhe | ubhilī teṇe || Jñāne.18.1659 || [‘shlokamāhātmyaṁ’] Eva Bhāratāchā āvāṅkā | āṇūni shlokā yekā | Saṅjaye kurunāyakā | dīdhalā hātī || Jñāne.18.1660 || Jaisā neṇo kevaḍhā vahnī | pari guṇāgrī ṭheūnī | āṇije sūryāchī hānī | nistarāvayā || Jñāne.18.1661 || Taise shabdabrahma anaṅta | ĵāle savālakṣha Bhārata | Bhāratāche shate sāta | sarvaswa Gītā || Jñāne.18.1662 || Tayāhī sātā shatāṅchā | ityartha hā shlokasheṣhīṅchā | Vyāsashiṣhya Saṅjayāĉhā | pūrṇodgāra ĵo || Jñāne.18.1663 || Yeṇe ekachi shloke | rāhe teṇe asake | avidyājātāche nike | jiṅtile hoya || Jñāne.18.1664 || Aise shlokashate sāta | gītechī pade āṅge vāhata | pade mhaṇo kī paramāmruta | GītāKāshīṅche || Jñāne.18.1665 || Kī ātmarājāchiye sabhe | gīte voḍavale he khāṁbe | maĵa shloka pratibhe | aise yeta || Jñāne.18.1666 || Kī Gītā he saptashatī | maṅtrapratipādya bhagavatī | mohamahiṣhā muktī | ānaṅdalī ase || Jñāne.18.1667 || Mhaṇauni mane kāye vāchā | ĵo sevaka hoīla iyechā | to swānaṅdasāmrājyāĉhā | chakravartī karī || Jñāne.18.1668 || Kī avidyātimirarokhe | shloka sūryāte paijā jiṅke | aise praKāshile Gītāmiṣhe | rāye ShreeKriṣhṇe || Jñāne.18.1669 || Kī shlokākṣharadrākṣhalatā | māṅḍava jālī āhe Gītā | saṁsārapathashrāṅtā | visaṁbāvayā || Jñāne.18.1670 || Kī sabhāgyasaṅtī bhramarī | sevile te shloka kalhārī | ShreeKriṣhṇākhya-sarovarī | sāsinnalī he || Jñāne.18.1671 || Kī shloka navhatī āna | game gīteche mahimāna | vākhāṇite baṅdījana | udaṅḍa jaise || Jñāne.18.1672 || Kī shlokāṅchiyā āvārā | sāta shate karūni suṅdarā | sarvāgama Gītāpurā | vaso āle || Jñāne.18.1673 || Kī nijakāṅtā ātmayā | āvaḍī Gītā miḷāvayā | shloka navhatī bāhyā- | pasara kā ĵo || Jñāne.18.1674 || Kī Gītākamaḷīṅche bhruṅga | kī he Gītāsāgarataraṅga | kī harīche he turaṅga | Gītārathīṅche || Jñāne.18.1675 || Kī shloka sarva tīrthasaṅghāta | ālā Shreegītegaṅge āṅta | je Arjun siṅhastha | jālā mhaṇauni || Jñāne.18.1676 || Kī nohe he shlokashreṇī | achiṅtachittachiṅtāmaṇī | kī nirvikalpā lāvaṇī | kalpatarūṅchī || Jñāne.18.1677 || Aisiyā shateṁsātashlokā | pari āgaḷā yekayekā | ātā koṇa vegaḷikā | vānāvā pā || Jñāne.18.1678 || Tānhī āṇi pāraṭhī | iyā kāmadhenūte diṭhī | sūni jaisiyā goṭhī | kījatī nā || Jñāne.18.1679 || Dīpā āgila māgila | sūryā dhākuṭā vaḍīla | amrutasiṅdhu khola | uthaḷa kāyasā || Jñāne.18.1680 || Taise pahile sarate | shloka na mhaṇāve gīte | junī navī pārijāte | āhātī kāī || Jñāne.18.1681 || Āṇi shlokā pāḍa nāhī | he kīra samarthū kāī | yetha vāchya vāchakahī | bhāga na dharī || Jñāne.18.1682 || [‘pāṭhamāhātmyaṁ’] Je iye shāstrī yeka | ShreeKriṣhṇachi vāchya vāchaka | he prasiddha ĵāṇe loka | bhalatāhī || Jñāne.18.1683 || Yethe arthe techi pāṭhe | ĵoḍe yevaḍheni dhaṭe | vāchyavāchaka yekavaṭe | sādhite shāstra || Jñāne.18.1684 || Mhaṇauni maĵa kāhī | samarthanī ātā viṣhaya nāhī | Gītā jāṇā he vāṅgmayī | Shreemūrti Prabhūchī || Jñāne.18.1685 || Shāstra vāchye arthe phaḷe | maga || Jñāne.18.1695 || Mhaṇauni ĵāṇatayā savā | Gītāchi yeekī sevā | kāya karāla āghavā | shāstrī yerī || Jñāne.18.1696 || [Gītā sugītā kartavyā shlo.] Āṇi Kriṣhṇārjunī mokaḷī | goṭhī chāvaḷilī je nirāḷī nirmāve nāhī || Jñāne.18.1788 || Shaṁbhū upamanyūcheni mohe | kṣhīrasāgarahī kelā āhe | yetha tohī upame sarī nohe | je viṣhagarbha kī || Jñāne.18.1789 || Aṅdhakāranishācharā | giḷitā sūrye charācharā | dhāṅvā kelā tarī kharā | tāunī kī to || Jñāne.18.1790 || Tātaliyā jagākāraṇe | chaṅdre veṅchile chāṅdiṇe | tayā sadoṣhā keṁvi mhaṇe | sārikhe he || Jñāne.18.1791 || Mhaṇoni tumhī maĵa saṅtī | graṅtharūpa ĵo hā trijagatī | upayoga kelā to puḍhatī | nirupama jī || Jñāne.18.1792 || Kiṅbahunā tumache kele | dharmakīrtana he siddhī nele | yetha māĵhe jī urale | pāīkapaṇa || Jñāne.18.1793 || [Varaprārthanā] Ātā vishwātmake devee | yeṇe vāgyajñe toṣhāve | toṣhoni maĵa dyāve | pasāyadāna he || Jñāne.18.1794 || Je khaḷāṅchī vyaṅkaṭī sāṅḍo | tayā satkarmī rati vāḍho | bhūtā paraspare paḍo | maitra jīvāṅche || Jñāne.18.1795 || Duritāṅche timira jāvo | vishwa swadharmasūrye pāho | ĵo je vāṅchchhīla to te lāho | prāṇijāta || Jñāne.18.1796 || Varṣhata sakaḷamaṅgaḷī | īshwaraniṣhṭhāṅchī māṅdiyāḷī | anavarata bhūtaḷī | bheṭo tayā bhūtā || Jñāne.18.1797 || Chalā kalpatarūṅche ārava | chetanā chiṅtāmaṇīche gāṁva | bolate je arṇava | pīyūṣhāche || Jñāne.18.1798 || Chaṅdrame je alāṅchchhana | mārtaṅḍa je tāpahīna | te sarvāṁhī sadā sajjana | soyare hotu || Jñāne.18.1799 || Kiṁbahunā sarvasukhī | pūrṇa hoūni tihī lokī | bhajiĵo ādipuruṣhī | akhaṅḍita || Jñāne.18.1800 || Āṇi graṅthopajīviye | visheṣhī lokī iye | druṣhṭādruṣhṭavijaye | hoāve jī || Jñāne.18.1801 || Yetha mhaṇe Shreevishwesharāvo | hā hoīla dānapasāvo | yeṇe vare Jñānadevo | sukhiyā jālā || Jñāne.18.1802 || [Vāstavyasthānamahimā] Aise yugī pari kaḷī | āṇi mahārāṣhṭramaṅḍaḷī | Shreegodāvarīchyā kūlī | dakṣhiṇilī || Jñāne.18.1803 || Tribhuvanaikapavitra | anādi paṅchakroshakṣhetra | jetha jagāche jīvanasūtra | Shreemahālayā ase || Jñāne.18.1804 || Tetha yaduvaṁshavilāsa | ĵo sakaḷakaḷānivāsa | nyāyāte poṣhī kṣhitīsha | Shreerāmachaṅdra || Jñāne.18.1805 || Tetha maheshānvayasaṁbhūte | ShreeNivruttināthasute | kele Jñānadeve gīte | deshīkāraleṇe || Jñāne.18.1806 || Eva Bhāratāchyā gāṁvī | Bhīṣhmanāma prasiddha parvī | ShreeKriṣhṇārjunī baravī | goṭhī je kelī || Jñāne.18.1807 || Je upaniṣhadāṅche sāra | sarvashāstrāṅche māhera | paramahaṁsī sarovara | sevije je || Jñāne.18.1808 || Tiye gītechā kalasha | saṁpūrṇa hā aṣhṭādasha | mhaṇe Nivruttidāsa | Jñānadev || Jñāne.18.1809 || Puḍhatī puḍhatī puḍhatī | iyā graṅthapuṇyasaṁpattī | sarvasukhī sarvabhūtī | saṁpūrṇa hoije || Jñāne.18.1810 || Shake bārāshate bārottare | tai ṭīkā kelī jñāneshware | sachchidānaṅdabābā ādare | lekhaku jāhālā || Jñāne.18.1811 ||

Iti ShreeJñānadevavirachitāyāṁ bhāvārthadīpikāyāmaṣhṭādasho’dhyāyaḥ || 18 || Iti Shreebhāvārthadīpikā samāptā || || ShreeKriṣhṇārpaṇamastu || Shloka 78, Ovyā 1811.

Shrīshake paṅdharāshe bārottarī | tāraṇanāmasaṁvatsarī | ekāĵanārdane atyādarī | Gītā Jñāneshwarīprati shuddha kelī || Jñāne.18.1 || Graṅtha pūrvīṅcha atishuddha | tarī pāṭhāṅtarī shuddha abaddha | to shodhūniyā evaṁvidha | pratishuddha siddhaJñāneshwarī || Jñāne.18.2 || Namo jñāneshwarā niṣhkalaṅkā | jayāchī gītechī vāchitā ṭīkā | jñāna hoya lokā | atibhāvikā graṅthārthiyā || Jñāne.18.3 || Bahukāḷaparvaṇī gomaṭī | bhādramāsa-kapilāṣhaṣhṭhī | pratiṣhṭhānī godātaṭī | lekhanakāmāṭhī saṅpūrṇa jālī || Jñāne.18.4 || Jñāneshwarīpāṭhī | ĵo vovī karīla marhāṭī | teṇe amrutāche tāṭī | ĵāṇa naroṭī ṭhevilī || Jñāne.18.5 || Jñāneshwarī bhāvārtha-dīpikā Gītāṭīkā samāptā ||

|| ShreeKriṣhṇārpaṇamastu ||
